# Skyrim:Infiltration

## Overview

Stalleo's camp; Secret Entrance through the large rock formation behind

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Stalleo](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalleo "Skyrim:Stalleo") outside [Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch").
2. Enter [Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch") through the secret tunnel.
3. Open the [Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch") main gate.
4. Talk to [Stalleo](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalleo "Skyrim:Stalleo").

### Stalleo

You will find [Stalleo](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalleo "Skyrim:Stalleo") next to a campfire along the narrow dirt road just outside of [Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch"). Mistaking you for a mercenary, he will tell you that invaders kidnapped his family and took possession of the fort while he and his bodyguards were away fighting in the war. He will tell you that his family is inside, and ask you to use a nearby secret tunnel (Treva's Watch Escape Tunnel; the "back door" in your journal) to access the fort, fight your way through, and then use a lever from inside to open the front gate for him.

### The Back Door/Secret Tunnel

Enter the nearby tunnel indicated by your objective marker. Inside, and around the first corner, three bandits stand at the top of some steps. Shooting down the lamp above them will cause an explosion. A fourth bandit lurks in the adjoining room. You will also find some chests and soul gems there.

There is a bear trap on the floor in the next hallway. Follow the hallway and ascend the stairs to find a bandit working at an anvil in the room straight ahead of you. He is facing away, facilitating a sneak attack.

Through an open doorway is a small storage room containing the corpses of two [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_(dead) "Skyrim:Nord (dead)") and an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_(dead) "Skyrim:Imperial (dead)"). It is possible that this is Stalleo's family, but they are not identified as such.

### Treva's Watch

Enter through the door into Treva's Watch. Two bear traps lie on the floor just around the turn. Ahead, you will hear two bandits conversing at the top of a stairway. Dispatch them and climb the stairs to find a short ramp ahead leading up to a somewhat crooked hallway. There are two bandits in a bedroom fairly near and to the right. Use caution when engaging these bandits, as the noise from this battle can alert 1-4 other bandits in nearby rooms, including a Bandit Chief and a powerful spellcaster. One way to try to avoid this is to provoke the initial two bandits, then immediately run back in the direction that you came, letting them chase you to fight out of earshot of their allies.

In the bedroom, you can find a few potions, including a [Potion of Brief Invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Brief_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Brief Invisibility"). Directly across the hall from this, behind a locked door, is a small treasure room.

At the end of the hallway, turn right. If you have not already killed the Bandit Chief, he or she will be sitting at a desk in the bedroom up ahead to the left. Again, a noisy battle here can attract the attention of a large nearby group of bandits. The chief will be facing away at a desk, so if you can make it into the room undetected, a sneak attack is possible. A [Spell Tome: Bound Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Bound_Sword "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Bound Sword") sits on the chief's desk.

Proceeding further into the fort, you will next find yourself on the upper tier of a large dining hall where several bandits are seated. Be prepared for a tough fight, as they will swarm you once alerted and at least one of them will be a powerful mage. A fourth bandit will likely be drawn into the fray from the nearby kitchen area.

Make your way through the kitchen and pantry then proceed through a wooden door. To the left is a pressure plate that activates a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") trap which can permanently pinch you against the stone wall. This is most likely to happen if a follower or enemy steps on the trap and you manage to get behind the spike wall after it is activated. Proceed around it with caution and make sure that a follower does not set it off.

After passing through a medium-sized room containing more smithing materials, you will reach a spiral staircase leading upwards into the fort's tower. Climbing it, you will find two more bandits, including another Chief, and a boss chest. It is also possible to ignore the tower and continue on to complete the quest, but you will miss some treasure. The room at the top contains the enchanting skill book *[Twin Secrets](/wiki/Skyrim:Twin_Secrets "Skyrim:Twin Secrets")*, and a [Spell Tome: Courage](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Courage "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Courage") sits on a wooden table near the Arcane Enchanter. Up on the tower roof is another chest. You can save yourself some trouble later by standing at the east and south edges of the tower roof and killing with ranged attacks all of the bandits below you on the rooftop encampments and in the courtyard.

If you took the stairway, return down and turn right into the hallway. Three leveled bandits await in a guards' room off the left of the hallway. This room contains two locked, empty jail cells. Past that room is a dart trap activated by a pressure plate.

Beyond this trap, a door to the left exits into the fort's front courtyard. Continuing straight past this door leads to a pressure plate trap which will release a swinging mace down into the area in front of the chest you can see ahead. Standing on the plate and waiting for the mace to fall will let you avoid receiving any damage.

### The Courtyard

Once you exit the door, you will find the lever immediately to your left. Unless you have killed all or some of them from the roof of the tower, there will be five or six bandits patrolling the courtyard, most of them guarding the front entrance from elevated platforms and rooftops. If you use the lever to open the entrance gate, Stalleo and his bodyguards will rush in from outside to help you fight them. Stalleo is a wizard and can help greatly in battle, but if you prefer, you can fight the bandits here on your own before opening the gate to let him in.

When all the bandits are dead, letting Stalleo know that he's regained possession of his home will complete the quest. When he asks about his family, you only have the option to say that you did not find them. He will then reward you with the [Spell Tome: Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Detect_Life "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Detect Life").

## Notes

- After the quest has been concluded, Stalleo and his men will return to their campsite and remain there for the duration of the game, leaving the fort to eventually become occupied by new groups of bandits and their chiefs.
- If there is a concurrent radiant quest from the Companions, either for a fragment of Wuuthrad or a set of the Silver Hand's plans, then you will encounter Silver Hand members and their leaders instead of normal bandits. Defeating them will have the same effect as if they were normal bandits.
- It is possible to get into the Treva's Watch courtyard without using the tunnel to enter the fort's interior. You can jump the rocky path to the left of the tunnel or climb the hill behind the fort (which give you an excellent vantage point from which to attack the enemies guarding the courtyard). However, doing this may not update the quest unless you enter and immediately exit the tunnel.
- If you clear out Treva's Watch before accepting the quest, you can complete it by closing and then reopening the lever. This may leave all objectives marked as incomplete.
- Bandits in the first level of the tunnel will not follow you out to Skyrim, and will remain in the same initial positions when you enter the tunnel again.
- One [Iron Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") vein can be found by walking west to the riverbank from the westernmost part of the fort's exterior.
- One treasure chest behind a tent on the rooftop perimeter may be hard to see if you're not looking for it.
- Brurid, the man Stalleo holds responsible for the current situation, is mentioned in conversation by bandits in the fort as being present but he is never encountered. However there are \*two\* Bandit Chiefs in here, and there is evidence in some of the in-game files that one of them was supposed to be Brurid.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.3, addresses this issue. Brurid now appears as one of the bosses.
- Likewise, there are three dead bodies in here (all Nord or Imperial) within the castle, but there is no evidence as to whether they are Stalleo's missing family or not, and when you talk to Stalleo and he asks whether you've seen his family, your only option is to say no, and he replies by saying he hopes they escaped. The family are never seen in-game.
- There is evidence that Stalleo's original reward was supposed to be a different Spell Tome: [Spectral Arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Spectral_Arrow "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Spectral Arrow"), which is found nowhere else in the game and not sold at any vendors.
- You will need to complete the entire conversation with Stalleo in order to begin the quest. If you don't, he will stay at his camp, irrespective of whether you've opened the gate or dealt with the bandits.

## Bugs

- The quest objectives don't update to indicate completion.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  -  A `sqs` query resolves this.
- If you had previously cleared the dungeon and opened the front gate before the quest starts, you'll still need to repeat everything.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.

| 60 |  | I've opened the front gate, I should return to Stalleo for my reward. |
| 100 | ☑ | I have discovered a back way into Treva's watch and was able to open the main gate from the other side. |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 60:* Meet up with Stalleo in the courtyard. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 1.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunTrevasWatchQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunTrevasWatchQST`.

# Skyrim:Ingredients

## Overview

This is an overview of *[Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")*'s **[alchemical](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") ingredients** (also called "alchemy reagents").

More information on each ingredient can be found on its individual page (see links in the [tables](#2) below). **[UESP's Skyrim Map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/)** and **[UESP's Dragonborn Map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim)** have the functionality to show the location of plants in Tamriel world space.

The [Alchemy Effects](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Effects "Skyrim:Alchemy Effects") article lists ingredients indexed by magical effect and contains additional information about the relationships between ingredients, alchemy, and magical effects. A few ingredients are also classified as [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food").

## Sources

There are several ways to obtain ingredients:

- **Purchasing from [merchants](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Skyrim:Merchants")**
  - General merchants usually offer a few ingredients. Apothecary merchants offer many more, each stocking:
    - Up to 15 common ingredients
    - Up to 10 uncommon ingredients
    - Up to 5 rare ingredients
  - Counterintuitively, your chances of finding a *specific* uncommon ingredient in an apothecary's stock are smaller than those for finding a rare ingredient. This is because there are so many more uncommon ingredients than rare ingredients, that: [(# of uncommon ingredients offered/total # of uncommon ingredients) < (# of rare ingredients offered/total number of rare ingredients)].
  - Some ingredients can be bought and sold only if the [merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_(perk) "Skyrim:Merchant (perk)") perk has been unlocked on the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") perk tree.
- **Already-harvested samples**
  - You can find some ingredients on shelves or tables, in baskets, pots, etc., in various locations throughout Skyrim. They are typically plentiful in apothecaries' businesses and living quarters. Their owners may let you take the relatively inexpensive of these for free if you have done them [favors](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors"). Mages and wizards around Skyrim, a concentration of which are [people living at the College of Winterhold,](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") tend to possess ingredients in their dwellings and rooms.
  - Some types of NPCs and enemies may carry ingredients on their person.
  - Ingredients can also be found in containers.
    - Certain [barrels](/wiki/Skyrim:Barrel "Skyrim:Barrel") contain multiple copies of a common ingredient.
    - [Apothecary's satchels](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") always contain one or more randomly-selected ingredients (plus a 25% chance of containing a healing [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions")). These satchels are tagged internally in the game as of common-, uncommon-, or rare-type. Rare-type satchels always contain one common, one uncommon, and one rare ingredient.
- **Harvesting from plants**
  - You can take ingredients from many of Skyrim's plants. Some of these are common and widespread, with thousands of plants growing in diverse areas, whereas others are quite rare and difficult to find. Once you have harvested a plant's ingredient, some or all of its flowers and stems disappear, allowing already-harvested plants to be easily identified. Harvested plants will later [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn"), at which point you can again harvest their ingredients.
- **Collecting from creatures**
  - Many [creatures'](/wiki/Skyrim:Creatures "Skyrim:Creatures") body parts—meat, wings, heart, skin, horns, teeth, etc—are alchemy ingredients. When you kill the creature, you can collect the ingredient from its corpse.
- **Catching passive creatures**
  - Various [passive creatures](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures "Skyrim:Passive Creatures") can be caught to obtain ingredients, including bees, fish, dragonflies, torchbugs, and butterflies.
- **Growing plants in [the homesteads](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")
  - With [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") installed, areas of fertile soils can be added to the homesteads. These soils can be planted with a sample. The plant will grow into maturity after typically 2 days and there will be 2-5 samples of the ingredient on each plant (depending on the plant). The plant will not die and will respawn every few days after harvesting. However, not all plant ingredients can be planted. A list of plants that can be grown may be found [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Greenhouse#Food_and_Ingredients "Skyrim:Greenhouse").

## Standard Ingredients

This table lists all of the standard ingredients in the game. You will experience a mild primary effect from eating an ingredient. [Brewing](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") two or more ingredients that share magical effects at an alchemy table will result in a potion or poison, with higher Alchemy skill levels resulting in stronger effects—longer duration, better fortifications or damage, etc. Special items such as Daedric Hearts and Void Salts are used in smithing [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric") equipment and improving [Nightingale armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Armor "Skyrim:Nightingale Armor"), respectively.

Ingredients added by [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") and [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") are included in the table below, but a quick list of all the ingredients each add-on adds can be seen [here (Dawnguard)](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Items#Alchemy "Skyrim:Dawnguard Items"), [here (Dragonborn)](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Items#Ingredients "Skyrim:Dragonborn Items") and [here (Hearthfire)](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire_Items#Ingredients "Skyrim:Hearthfire Items"). For [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") ingredients, see [this category](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Creation_Club-Ingredients "Category:Skyrim-Creation Club-Ingredients").

There are 91 ingredients in the base game, with 5 added by [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), 11 added by [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), 2 added by [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), and 1 added via the \_ResourcePack.esl file, for a total of 110 ingredients. Additionally there are 5 [unused](/wiki/Skyrim:Unobtainable_Items#Ingredients "Skyrim:Unobtainable Items") ingredients, 3 of which were later used in Creation Club content and 1 of which is obtainable via a glitch.

## Creation Club Ingredients

A total of 73 ingredients are added by the following [Creations](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"):

- [Bittercup](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup") (Ironwood Fruit)
- [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") (9 ingredients)
- [Forgotten Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons") (Wild Grass Pod)
- [Goblins](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblins "Skyrim:Goblins") (Steel-Blue Entoloma)
- [Rare Curios](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Curios "Skyrim:Rare Curios") (51 ingredients)
- [Plague of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Plague_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Plague of the Dead") (Mort Flesh)
- [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") (6 ingredients)
- [The Cause](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause") (3 ingredients)

In addition, two [quest ingredients](#Quest_Ingredients) are added by [Spell Knight Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Spell Knight Armor").

| Ingredient Name ([ID](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID")) | | Primary Effect | Secondary Effect | Tertiary Effect | Quaternary Effect | [Value](/wiki/File:SR-item-Gold-heads.png "Value") | [Weight](/wiki/File:SR-icon-clothing-Leather_Backpack_(square).png "Weight") | Merchant Avail. | Garden |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

# Skyrim:Inheritance

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **A friend has died.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | N/A |
| Location(s): | N/A |
| Reward: | Random amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") |
| ID: | WIKill03 |

A tragic event

## Walkthrough

If someone you were [friends](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") with has died, they will leave you a sum of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") in their will. A [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") will approach you and say, *"I've got a letter and a lot of gold. Something about it being your inheritance? Oh, and... sorry for your loss."* He will hand over a random amount of gold and a [letter of inheritance](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_of_Inheritance "Skyrim:Letter of Inheritance") from the court of the [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") that the person lived in.

### Reward

The base reward is 100 gold multiplied by your [relationship rank](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition#Relationship_Rank "Skyrim:Disposition") with the victim. A fixed 10% tax is then applied.

## Notes

- This quest does not appear in your journal.
- Sometimes your friend can be a generic NPC, such as an Arch Necromancer.
- Sometimes the note comes within mere minutes after the person has died.
- It is possible to receive inheritance from people that you have killed yourself.
- If you raise a friendly NPC with the master conjuration spell Dead Thrall, you may receive their inheritance after they are killed in combat, regardless of whether you have received it before.
- Rich victims were intended to have a base reward of 1000 gold, but no NPCs in the game are flagged as rich. Similarly, the tax applied can vary, but nothing ever alters its value from its default of 10%.

## Bugs

- If you already have a letter in your inventory, the new one will stack with the old one and the names will be the same on all of them.

## Quest Stages

- All of the quest stages are empty: 1.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage WIKill03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest WIKill03`.

# Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)

## Overview

Inner Sanctum

The **Inner Sanctum** is a relatively well-preserved portion of the Chantry of [Auri-El](/wiki/Lore:Auri-El "Lore:Auri-El") in the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"). It is the location of [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow"), and is where the final stages of [Touching the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky "Skyrim:Touching the Sky") take place.

## Related Quests

- **[Touching the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky "Skyrim:Touching the Sky")**: Find and retrieve [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow").

### Exterior

The exterior to this large building is the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"). A bridge leads to a flight of stairs ascending to the chantry courtyard, which is dominated by a statue of [Auri-El](/wiki/Lore:Auri-El "Lore:Auri-El"). The huge double doors beyond the two curved stairs are locked until you complete the pilgrimage ritual. To do so, after having used it at each of the five wayshrines, empty the [initiate's ewer](/wiki/Skyrim:Initiate%27s_Ewer "Skyrim:Initiate's Ewer") into the basin at the top of the stairs behind Auri-El's statue. The water will then empty from the bottom of the basin, flow along grooves cut in the floor, and collect in a carved sun design. A green crystal above will then shine onto the water, and the sun carving on the doors will revolve, unlocking the doors and granting access to the Inner Sanctum.

### Inner Sanctum

The Shrine of Auriel

The entrance leads into a large room with a number of frozen [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Frozen_Falmer "Skyrim:Frozen Falmer") and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Frozen_Chaurus "Skyrim:Frozen Chaurus") surrounding a [Shrine of Auriel](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines "Skyrim:Shrines"). Some of the statues are individual Falmer and chaurus, and some are in groups. A number of these statues hold items of interest. Taking one of these items may free its possessor from its icy paralysis, resulting in them attacking you, and possibly also releasing other nearby hostile creatures; however, at other times, the creatures are not released. The items that can be looted from the creatures in this room are: a [philter of resist cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_Resist_Cold "Skyrim:Philter of Resist Cold"), an [elven shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Shield "Skyrim:Elven Shield"), an [enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons") [elven sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Sword "Skyrim:Elven Sword"), a [philter of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Philter of Extra Magicka"), a [scroll of blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), a [philter of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_Health "Skyrim:Philter of Health"), a rare [staff of icy spear](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Icy_Spear "Skyrim:Staff of Icy Spear"), an elven sword, and a [silver emerald necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Emerald_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Emerald Necklace"). Around the central shrine are a number of offerings: two [gleamblossom](/wiki/Skyrim:Gleamblossom "Skyrim:Gleamblossom") flowers, four [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), a [scroll of fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fireball "Skyrim:Scroll of Fireball"), an [emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald"), a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), an [elixir of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Elixir_of_Health "Skyrim:Elixir of Health"), a quiver of sixteen [elven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Elven Arrow"), three [yellow mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Yellow_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Yellow Mountain Flower"), and an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"). There are many [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") found throughout the building, most of which can be looted.

By the west wall is a pedestal serving as an altar, which when activated will place the [initiate's ewer](/wiki/Skyrim:Initiate%27s_Ewer "Skyrim:Initiate's Ewer") on top and raise a concealed door with a sun symbol behind the altar. You must then pass through the door and turn around to retrieve the ewer, as you'll need it for other doors. Each altar is a waist-high pedestal featuring the sun design, and additional altars are on the far side of each concealed door to allow you to return the way you came. Another lootable skeleton lies in the passage beyond the door. The passage continues to a normal door, beyond which is a room containing the [frost giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Giant "Skyrim:Frost Giant") carrying the [ruby paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby_Paragon "Skyrim:Ruby Paragon"). Two lootable skeletons and a stone [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") are in the southeast corner. By the north wall is another altar and concealed door. Placing the ewer on the altar opens the door, granting access to a small room containing a stone table holding leveled [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") of [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), magicka, and [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), two quivers of elven arrows, and a stone chest.

Return to the first room, where doors in the northeast and northwest corners both lead to the same room. This room contains three lootable skeletons and more frozen Falmer, some of which again hold items that can be looted. The items that can be looted from the Falmer in this room are: a [potion of vigorous healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigorous_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Vigorous Healing"), an expert-level [spell tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), and a [staff of ice spikes](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Ice_Spikes "Skyrim:Staff of Ice Spikes"). Opposite each of the doors is a stone table holding a leveled potion of healing, a leveled [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), and a [scroll of conjure flame atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Flame Atronach"). In the middle of the south wall is another table holding a random potion of healing and a random potion of magicka, with a passage opposite to the north. To the left of the passage is a stone bench with a skeleton next to a [scroll of ironflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Ironflesh "Skyrim:Scroll of Ironflesh"). In the passage, the first frozen Falmer you encounter holds a leveled [necklace of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Necklace_of_Health "Skyrim:Necklace of Health"), and the next holds an [elven war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_War_Axe "Skyrim:Elven War Axe"). Southeast of the second frozen Falmer is a small room with a stone chest and a brazier containing a [scroll of grand healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Grand_Healing "Skyrim:Scroll of Grand Healing"), a leveled potion of health, and a leveled [potion of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka"). North of the second frozen statue is a room with two lootable skeletons by a stone table to the left. Open doors to the north lead into another room filled with frozen statues, including four chaurus and a single Falmer holding a [circlet of waterbreathing](/wiki/Skyrim:Circlet_of_Waterbreathing "Skyrim:Circlet of Waterbreathing"). Taking the circlet will cause each of the statues to burst free and attack. Once they are dealt with, continue through a hole in the ice-encrusted wall to the west.

Through the hole is an icy tunnel that splits into two paths, with one route straight ahead to the west, and the other branching to the south. The south path leads to a small area containing a stone chest with a random potion of healing, a random potion of magicka, and a [scroll of fire storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm") beside it. The west path leads to [Auriel's Chapel](#Auriel.27s_Chapel) in the exterior area of the vale.

### Auriel's Chapel

The exit from the Inner Sanctum leads onto a ledge, with a path below and no way to get back up. Dropping down, a small empty alcove is to the south, and the passage continues to the east, where a chamber filled with more frozen statues features a throne at the far end in which [Arch-Curate Vyrthur](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch-Curate_Vyrthur "Skyrim:Arch-Curate Vyrthur") sits behind a shimmering force field. As you approach, he will initiate conversation before beginning to release wave after wave of frozen Falmer and chaurus upon you. After several waves, he will start collapsing sections of the ceiling before raising an [ancient frost atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Ancient Frost Atronach") and the last of the frozen Falmer. Once you've defeated these creatures, he will blow the entire roof and large parts of the walls to rubble, at which point a cutscene plays with [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") instructing you to get up, followed by her moving to confront Vyrthur. You will be unable to do anything other than follow Serana as she passes another lowered wayshrine and climbs one of the two flights of stairs up to where Vyrthur stands on a balcony overlooking the frozen lake in the vale. At the end of the cutscene, you will be released to battle Vyrthur. As soon as he is defeated, the wayshrine below the stairs will rise and [Knight-Paladin Gelebor](/wiki/Skyrim:Knight-Paladin_Gelebor "Skyrim:Knight-Paladin Gelebor") will emerge; the wayshrine is displayed as "Temple Balcony". Don't forget to loot Vyrthur's corpse for his unique set of [ancient Falmer armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Falmer_Cuirass "Skyrim:Ancient Falmer Cuirass"). After a short conversation with Gelebor, he will grant you [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow"), which will appear above a capped basin in the wayshrine. Gelebor informs you about [sunhallowed arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunhallowed_Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Sunhallowed Elven Arrow") and will give you twelve such arrows, also offering to transmute 20 elven arrows to sunhallowed arrows as often as you want. If you are a Vampire Lord, be sure to keep some elven arrows in order to transmute them into [bloodcursed arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodcursed_Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Bloodcursed Elven Arrow"). On the walls of the wayshrine are the other five portals.

Using the [sapphire paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_Paragon "Skyrim:Sapphire Paragon") teleports you to an otherwise inaccessible badly damaged room in the Inner Sanctum. The broken stone arch forming the portal allows you to return directly to the paragon platform. The room contains three unlocked stone chests, with many loose [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems"), a random enchanted elven sword, an [elven helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Helmet "Skyrim:Elven Helmet"), a pair of [elven light gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Light_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Elven Light Gauntlets"), and an elven shield among them.

## Bugs

- If you have multiple followers, such as personal or quest-related companions, [armored trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Armored_Troll "Skyrim:Armored Troll"), permanently conjured beasts, or zombies, they may require some "coaxing" in order to follow you past various portals. A combination of waiting, saving, and reloading will eventually resolve this issue. **?**
- [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad")'s damage bonus against elves has no effect on the [Snow Elves](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Elf "Skyrim:Snow Elf") or [Frozen Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Frozen_Falmer "Skyrim:Frozen Falmer") here.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.
- Followers may enter through the wrong door due to a badly placed door link at the other end of the cell.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Innocence Lost

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Help an orphaned [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") avoid being returned to a sadistic [caretaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Aventus Aretino](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") |
| Location(s): | The [Aretino Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Aretino_Residence "Skyrim:Aretino Residence") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm")  [Honorhall Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") |
| Reward: | [Aretino Family Heirloom](/wiki/Skyrim:Aretino_Family_Heirloom "Skyrim:Aretino Family Heirloom") [Mysterious Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Note_(DB) "Skyrim:Mysterious Note (DB)") [Consider Adoption](/wiki/Skyrim:Consider_Adoption "Skyrim:Consider Adoption")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") (if you have not yet adopted two children) |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | 0→1 ([Aventus Aretino](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino")) |
| ID: | DB01 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** None; however, [Delayed Burial](/wiki/Skyrim:Delayed_Burial "Skyrim:Delayed Burial") is an optional prequel to this quest. | **Next →** [With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | None; however, [Delayed Burial](/wiki/Skyrim:Delayed_Burial "Skyrim:Delayed Burial") is an optional prequel to this quest. | | → Next | [With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...") | | |

Aventus Aretino calls upon mysterious forces for help

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Aventus Aretino](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") inside the [Aretino Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Aretino_Residence "Skyrim:Aretino Residence") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").
2. Kill [Grelod the Kind](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind") in the [Honorhall Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
3. Return to Aventus for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

The Aretino Residence in Windhelm

### Initiating the Quest

It seems a strange boy named [Aventus Aretino](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") is all the talk in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). By asking around town you will likely hear that Aventus is attempting to perform the [Black Sacrament](/wiki/Lore:A_Kiss,_Sweet_Mother "Lore:A Kiss, Sweet Mother"), a ritual designed to summon a [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") assassin. Once this topic arises in a dialogue, the objective *"Talk to Aventus Aretino"* will appear in your journal as a miscellaneous quest. Speaking to the children at [Honorhall Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") will also lead you to Aventus' door.

### Aventus Aretino

Aventus's fury is revealed

You will find Aventus in the [Aretino Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Aretino_Residence "Skyrim:Aretino Residence") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). If entering Windhelm through the main gate, immediately turn right and proceed up the stairs. Continue straight ahead, passing the house on your left, and turn left around its far corner. You should now be heading north, with the house on your left and a crumbling stone wall on your right. The Aretino Residence is a short distance ahead. If this is your first visit to the area, [Idesa Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Idesa_Sadri "Skyrim:Idesa Sadri") will be outside Aventus' house trying to dissuade [Grimvar Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Grimvar_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Grimvar Cruel-Sea") from playing with poor Aventus, warning him that, *"...Aventus Aretino walks a dark path"*. You can ask Idesa for more information, and she'll tell you that Aventus' mother recently died, and is performing the Black Sacrament to contact the Dark Brotherhood. She will, however, admit that she doesn't know why he's doing it.

If you have previously entered the house without the objective in your journal, it will be added at this point. To speak with Aventus, [pick the lock](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking#Skill_Usage "Skyrim:Lockpicking") on the door where you will discover Aventus performing the Black Sacrament, chanting over and over again. He is so engrossed in the ritual that he fails to notice you. When you speak to him, he will be overjoyed and mistake you for the assassin he was trying to summon, *"I did the Black Sacrament, over and over. With the body, and the... the things. And then you came! An assassin from the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood")!"*

He will tell you about his mother's death and that afterward he was sent to Honorhall Orphanage in Riften, where he was subjected to the cruelties of its headmistress, [Grelod the Kind](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind"). He escaped the orphanage and returned to his home where he set about performing the Sacrament to get his revenge and to ensure that neither he or his friends will have to suffer any more. He expects you to kill Grelod, further stating, *"She's a monster."* You can ask for further details, but whatever the course of your conversation with him, it will conclude with your journal advancing the Innocence Lost quest. He will also ask you not to harm [Constance Michel](/wiki/Skyrim:Constance_Michel "Skyrim:Constance Michel"), Grelod's servant, because she was kind to him and the other orphans.

### Grelod The Dead

Grelod tells the orphans they aren't going anywhere

Travel to Honorhall Orphanage in Riften. Here Grelod the Kind is a cruel tyrant, verbally abusing her charges, *"Nobody needs you, nobody wants you"*, and that her nickname is a term of endearment that she has bestowed on herself and imposed on the children. Killing Grelod does not constitute a crime so you may kill her in whatever fashion you see fit, however attacking any of the children or Constance is a crime. Whatever manner you choose will be successful as she only has one point of health.

While Constance runs about in a panic once Grelod dies, the orphans will come to gloat over the body, expressing reactions ranging from philosophical reflection, *"Kill one person, and you can solve so many problems. I wonder at the possibilities"*, to simple joy, *"Hurrah! Hurrah!"* If spoken to, each of the children will share one or more thoughts and feelings about her death.

Return to Windhelm and speak to Aventus. He will greet the news with happiness and show his gratitude by giving you a [family heirloom](/wiki/Skyrim:Aretino_Family_Heirloom "Skyrim:Aretino Family Heirloom"), which is *"Supposed to be sort of valuable"*, however the dinner plate is only worth 100 gold. This quest counts as a favor quest for Aventus, who is a citizen of Eastmarch.

### Alternate Path

If you have killed Grelod prior to starting the quest, then when you speak with Aventus for the first time you can tell him that you killed her. He will state that *"I knew the Dark Brotherhood was good... just not that good! You killed the old hag before I even asked!"* There are no negative consequences to the quest and the reward is the same.

## Notes

- If you revisit the orphanage after completing the quest, the children will make general comments about things being better with Grelod gone. Guards in the city will also make similar comments about the latter.
- After killing her, guards may say *"Been a murder, over in Riften. Some old lady who runs an orphanage. Those poor children must be heartbroken."* Guards in Riften may also suggest some suspicion toward you with *"That old woman who runs the orphanage has been murdered. Say, didn't I see you coming out of there...?"*
- [Followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") with a morality value of 3 won't kill Grelod if you order them to do so. Although Grelod is cruel and killing her doesn't result in a bounty, she is classified as an "innocent" or non-hostile NPC until attacked, making her death a "crime" in the eyes of the follower's programming. The fact that Grelod has only 1 health point adds to that reasoning.
- After the quest, Aventus will always view you as his savior regardless if you [join](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...") or [eliminate](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!") the Dark Brotherhood.
- Finishing the quest will prevent further [assassination attempts against you](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Dark_Brotherhood_Assassin_Sent_to_Kill_the_Player "Skyrim:World Interactions"), regardless if you join or eliminate the Dark Brotherhood.
- After Grelod is killed, Constance Michel will run around in a panic. She will remain in this state even if you return days or weeks later, only returning to normal once Innocence Lost has been completed by speaking to Aventus Aretino.
  - If you have installed [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), Constance will assume ownership of the orphanage once the quest is finished and allow you to [adopt children](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption") from there. You'll get a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Consider_Adoption "Skyrim:Consider Adoption") from her as well.
  - If you don't have Hearthfire installed, Constance will continue to run around in a panic after the quest is finished, even if you return days or weeks later.

## Bugs

- Although you will note in your journal that Aventus can return to the orphanage at the completion of the quest, he never does so. He will remain alone in his home. If spoken to there, he will say that he's planning on growing up to be an assassin, *"like you"*. If you talk to him right after killing Grelod, he will say *"I'll give them some time to clean up the mess."*
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.3, fixes this bug.
- After completing the quest, the ritual mess that's still sitting in Aretino's house won't be cleaned up.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.
- The fix from Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.2.3 created another bug. Although Aventus now returns to Honorhall Orphanage after completion of the quest with Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.2.3, he does so too early. He should be delayed until the player has actually left the city, which is when the courier will begin tracking you down to deliver the note.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.
- The fix from Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.2.3 created a third bug. Although Aventus now returns to Honorhall Orphanage after completion of the quest with Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.2.3, he can sometimes be found stuck trying to navigate his way to the city because [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall") may not yet be cleared when he leaves Windhelm.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.7, fixes this bug.
- Even if you kill Grelod in another room, her body may teleport to the main room upon death.

## Quest Stages

| (DB01Objective) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Talk to Aventus Aretino |
| 200 | ☑ |  |
| Innocence Lost (DB01) | | |
| 5 |  | I heard a rumor that a boy named Aventus Aretino, in Windhelm, has been attempting to contact the Dark Brotherhood. I should find this boy and speak with him, and find out why he wants to contact a guild of assassins. *Objective 5:* Talk to Aventus Aretino |
| 20 |  | The mother of Aventus Aretino recently died, and the boy was sent to live at Honorhall Orphanage in Riften. He thinks I'm a Dark Brotherhood assassin, and wants me to kill the Orphanage's sadistic headmistress, Grelod the Kind. *Objective 20:* Kill Grelod the Kind |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Tell Aventus Aretino that Grelod is dead |
| 200 | ☑ | I killed Grelod the Kind, and Aventus Aretino rewarded me with a family heirloom. Now the boy can return to Honorhall Orphanage, and live out his childhood peacefully. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table:
  - DB01Objective: 0, 255.
  - DB01: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DB01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DB01`.

# Skyrim:Interception

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Aid the Hammerfell resistance.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Talking to [Azadi](/wiki/Skyrim:Azadi "Skyrim:Azadi") in [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") |
| Location(s): | [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"), [Purewater Run](/wiki/Skyrim:Purewater_Run "Skyrim:Purewater Run"), [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten"), [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") |
| Reward: | 400, 800 or 1600 gold, [Boneshaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Boneshaver "Skyrim:Boneshaver") |
| ID: | ccEDHSSE003\_Quest |
| Added by: | [Redguard Elite Armaments](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Elite_Armaments "Skyrim:Redguard Elite Armaments") |

Interception

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Azadi](/wiki/Skyrim:Azadi "Skyrim:Azadi") in [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone").
2. Read [Azadi's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Azadi%27s_Note "Skyrim:Azadi's Note") and wait for a courier to deliver another [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Fijeh%27s_Letter_to_(Player) "Skyrim:Fijeh's Letter to (Player)") to you.
3. Travel to [Purewater Run](/wiki/Skyrim:Purewater_Run "Skyrim:Purewater Run") and speak to [Fijeh](/wiki/Skyrim:Fijeh "Skyrim:Fijeh").
4. Read [Fijeh's instructions](/wiki/Skyrim:Fijeh%27s_Instructions "Skyrim:Fijeh's Instructions").
5. Head to the Vilemyr Inn in Ivarstead, and speak to [Sirayar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sirayar "Skyrim:Sirayar").
6. Return to Fijeh at Purewater Run.
7. Travel to Sunderstone Gorge where you can either attack the caravan on your own or meetup with the Remnants.
8. Head back to Purewater Run and speak to Rakeed and Fijeh.

### Azadi

Azadi

To begin this quest, speak to Azadi in [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") where you can either brawl him or speak him down:

:   *"Well, look what we have here."*
:   **Looking for a fight?**
:   *"Yes."*

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Alright, which side of your face would you like rearranged? (Brawl)** | *"I'll teach you to talk to me that way!"* | | | | Brawl begins |
| **You don't frighten me. All you're doing is being insufferable. Leave. (Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"Okay, okay. You've talked me into it. Thank you. Here, this is for you."* **Failed**: *"I'll teach you to talk to me that way."* | | | | **Passed**: Gives [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Azadi%27s_Note "Skyrim:Azadi's Note") and warps away **Failed**: Brawl begins |
| **I don't have time for this right now.** | *"I can smell your shame!"* | | | | Nothing |

After defeating him in a brawl:

:   *"You're tougher than you look. You got me, fair and square. Thank you. Here this is for you."*

He will then hand you a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Azadi%27s_Note "Skyrim:Azadi's Note") and disappear. Read the note and wait for a courier to deliver another [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Fijeh%27s_Letter_to_(Player) "Skyrim:Fijeh's Letter to (Player)") to you.

### Purewater Run

Fijeh awaits your arrival

Once you have read the courier's letter, you will need to travel to [Purewater Run](/wiki/Skyrim:Purewater_Run "Skyrim:Purewater Run"). Once you arrive, speak to [Fijeh](/wiki/Skyrim:Fijeh "Skyrim:Fijeh"):

:   *"Out with it."*
:   **You must be Fijeh.**
:   *"Correct."*

:   :   **I'd like to help your missing Remnant, Rakeed. What comes next?**
    :   *"It's all in this note."*

:   :   **I don't work for free. Before this goes further, we need to talk about payment.**
    :   *"A little coin always greases the wheels. How much?"*

| Option | Dialogue | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **400 gold seems reasonable.** | *"For that price? Sure."* | | | |
| **I wouldn't do this for any less than 800 gold. (Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"How can I argue with that?"* **Failed**: *"Nah, I don't think so."* | | | |
| **There's other contracts I could be working right now. 1600 gold. (Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"How can I argue with that?"* **Failed**: *"You expect me to believe that?"* | | | |

Josla

Sirayar

All three options will lead to the following dialogue:

:   **It's settled then. What's next?**
:   *"It's all in this note. Now... this conversation never happened. Understood?"*

:   :   **I'll return soon.**
    :   *"Good luck out there."*

:   :   **I hope Rakeed is worth all of this trouble.**
    :   *"Good luck out there."*

Alternatively, you can tell him:

:   **Actually, I don't have time to deal with this right now.**

He will then hand you [instructions](/wiki/Skyrim:Fijeh%27s_Instructions "Skyrim:Fijeh's Instructions") which explain that the Remnants have agents that have lived in Skyrim for over 20 years, that one lives in the Miner's Barracks in Karthwasten and the other should be waiting for you in front of Vilemyr Inn in Ivarstead.

### Karthwasten

Head to the [Miner's Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten_Miner%27s_Barracks "Skyrim:Karthwasten Miner's Barracks") in Karthwasten, where you will find [Josla](/wiki/Skyrim:Josla "Skyrim:Josla") sitting behind the barracks. Speak to her:

:   **"The ravens take flight once more."**
:   *"Of course. Let's both get on with our lives now, hmm?"*

She will then hand you a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Josla%27s_Note "Skyrim:Josla's Note") which states that she overheard that a Hammerfell noble from Sentinel would be crossing the border in the next few days and paid a hefty coin purse to the Thalmor to ensure safe passage to [Blacklight](/wiki/Lore:Blacklight "Lore:Blacklight"). She suspects that the noble is [Ismal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ismal "Skyrim:Ismal") and that Rakeed would most likely be with him.

### Ivarstead

Head to the Vilemyr Inn in Ivarstead, where you will find [Sirayar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sirayar "Skyrim:Sirayar"):

:   **"The ravens take flight once more."**
:   *"I understand. Anyway, it's done. Time to move on."*

He will then hand you a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Sirayar%27s_Note "Skyrim:Sirayar's Note") which states that the wagon will be passing by [Sunderstone Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunderstone_Gorge "Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge").

### Ambush the Thalmor

The Remnants await you.

Return to Fijeh at Purewater Run:

:   **Ismal has been traveling with a caravan of Thalmor to Morrowind.**
:   *"You've done well."*

    :   **They will enter Skyrim from the southwest, passing by Sunderstone Gorge.**
    :   *"It just so happens I've got some scouts along the road. Meet up with them, and together see if you can't overpower the caravan."*

:   :   :   **Sounds good.**
        :   *"Here. This is for you."*

:   :   :   **I prefer to work alone.**
        :   *"I understand. Go in quiet, break our man out, then get out of there. Don't risk combat if you can avoid it. If you can't, then give 'em hell. Here. This is for you."*

:   :   :   :   **I'll make sure your man gets out safely.**
            :   *"Stay sharp out there."*

:   :   :   :   **I only want to kill Thalmor. I can't promise anything else.**
            :   *"It can't be helped."*

He will then hand you the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Remnant_Supply_Chest_Key "Skyrim:Remnant Supply Chest Key") to the remnant supply chest that can be found near him. Unlock the chest and it contains:

- [Remnant Agent Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Remnant_Agent_Armor "Skyrim:Remnant Agent Armor")
- [Remnant Agent Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Remnant_Agent_Boots "Skyrim:Remnant Agent Boots")
- [Remnant Agent Gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Remnant_Agent_Gloves "Skyrim:Remnant Agent Gloves")
- [Remnant Agent Hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Remnant_Agent_Hood "Skyrim:Remnant Agent Hood")
- [Remnant Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Remnant_Shield "Skyrim:Remnant Shield")
- [Remnant Scimitar of Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Remnant_Scimitar_of_Fire "Skyrim:Remnant Scimitar of Fire") x 2
- [Potion of Extended Invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extended_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Extended Invisibility") x 2
- [The Ebon Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ebon_Arm "Skyrim:The Ebon Arm")

Travel to Sunderstone Gorge where you can either attack the caravan on your own or meetup with the Remnants.

Rakeed and the fight.

Meet up with the three Remnants and they will charge to the caravan alongside you. You will have to fight four Thalmor soldiers and [Ismal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ismal "Skyrim:Ismal"), who wields [Boneshaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Boneshaver "Skyrim:Boneshaver").

Once the Thalmor and Ismal have been dispatched, rescue Rakeed:

:   *"Please! Have mercy... I beg you..."*

:   :   **Wait Here. I'll be back.**
    :   *"This doesn't look good."*

:   :   **(Cut Rakeed's Bonds)**
    :   *"Thanks a lot."*

When freed he will then turn himself invisible and disappear. Additionally before leaving the three remaining Remnant Agents can be pickpocketed from or killed with no consequence to gain even more enchanted Remnant sets of armor and weapons. Finally head back to Purewater Run where Rakeed and Fijeh are waiting:

:   *"You made it! I'm impressed. It was a gamble, but turned out well."*

:   :   **Good luck out there. I hope we meet again someday.**
    :   *"Thank you. Here, this is for you. May the gods keep you."*

:   :   **More than deserving of some payment, I'd say.**
    :   *"Thank you. Here, this is for you. May the gods keep you."*

You will receive the gold you and Fijeh agreed on, and both Rakeed and Fijeh will vanish with the casting of Invisibility spells. This ends the quest.

In addition to the rewards from the chest, you will now be able to smith the Remnant Armor, Boots, Gloves, Hood, Shield and Scimitars. These are the unenchanted versions of the Remnant Agent armor pieces and scimitars that you picked from the chest (all of which are enchanted except for the shield): they are to be found in the Steel menu, but require the Advanced Armors perk (on the left side of the Smithing tree) to forge, or to temper properly.

## Notes

- When Rakeed is rescued he is wearing a white variant of the Execution Hood which was always in the game files yet unobtainable and marked as unplayable.

## Bugs

- Both Josla and Sirayar can have the code phrase repeated to them indefinitely resulting in an unlimited number of their notes. **?**
- Azadi may not initiate dialogue when speaking to him and will only respond in generic dialogue such as "Need something?" and "Huh?"
- When you talk to Azadi and choose the brawl option, he may not initiate combat. This will give you a bounty for assault if you attack him.
- When you win the brawl with Azadi, he may only say "You're tougher than you look. You got me, fair and square." and not say the second line "Thank you. Here, this is for you.", so you will not get his note. Talking to him again will only result in "Need something?" and "Huh?" **?**
  -  To fix this, use the console command `setstage ccEDHSSE003_Quest 22`. Afterwards talk to Azadi and he will have the proper dialogue and give you the note.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccEDHSSE003_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccEDHSSE003_Quest`.

# Skyrim:Investigate the Bards College

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Alonella](/wiki/User:Alonella "User:Alonella"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Secunda](/wiki/User:Secunda "User:Secunda"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Investigate the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Any Bard |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | MS05Start |

Pay a visit to the Bards College.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to any bard in Skyrim.
2. Speak to [Viarmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Viarmo "Skyrim:Viarmo") at the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College").

## Detailed Walkthrough

Speak to any Bard you meet in Skyrim. Bards can be found wandering around the countryside or in taverns and inns. The bard will suggest that you should investigate The Bards College. Following their advice, go to  [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and speak to [Viarmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Viarmo "Skyrim:Viarmo").

## Bugs

- Starting this quest after you have already joined the Bards College will make this quest incompletable, permanently leaving this objective in your quest journal.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.
  -  You can clear the "Investigate the Bards College" quest by using the console command `SetObjectiveCompleted MS05Start 10 1`.
- Having King Olaf's verse before investigating the Bards College may make this quest incompletable, permanently leaving this objective in your quest journal.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
  -  This can be fixed with the console command `ResetQuest MS05Start` followed by `SetObjectiveCompleted MS05Start 10 1`.

## Quest Stages

| Investigate the Bards College (MS05Start) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Investigate the Bards College |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MS05Start stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MS05Start`.

# Skyrim:Irgnir's House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Irgnir's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Irgnir%27s+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DawnstarIrgnirsHouse | |
| Region | |
| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | |
| Location | |
| Eastern end of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Irgnir's House

**Irgnir's House** is the house of [Irgnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Irgnir "Skyrim:Irgnir"), located in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").

## Residents

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| | Residents | | --- | | **[Irgnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Irgnir "Skyrim:Irgnir")** | |

### Exterior

It is next to [Iron-Breaker Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron-Breaker_Mine "Skyrim:Iron-Breaker Mine"), at the end of the path through town, past [The White Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Hall "Skyrim:The White Hall"). There is a good view of the bay from the partially covered porch in front of the house, between [Brina's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina%27s_House "Skyrim:Brina's House") and [The Mortar and Pestle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mortar_and_Pestle "Skyrim:The Mortar and Pestle"). To the left of the main steps up to the porch is a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush. To the left of the building an area has been fenced in, however apart from a pile of firewood there is nothing in this area.

### Irgnir's House

Five skeever plaques

Another single room dwelling. On your left, against the southwest wall is a long wooden table holding a bottle of each, [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and two [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"). On the floor to the left is a basket containing three cabbages and another basket to the right contains two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and four [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"). To the right of this is a set of shelves holding two leeks, several loaves of bread, two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulbs, three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), two [gourds](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") and several cheese wheels. Above there are two garlic braids, three bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam").

In the western corner and along the northwest wall are three barrels, two of which containing [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). Further to the right against the same wall is a round wooden table and two chairs. On the table are six loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). Opposite the door on the northeast wall is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front, two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on the mantelpiece and three pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") on the hearth. To the left is a pile of firewood with five [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") heads mounted on plaques above. To the left of these is a rack hanging from the ceiling holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)").

To the right of the fireplace is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"). Further to the right against the northeast wall is a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and a chair beside it. Coming out from the southeast wall is a large double bed with two bottle of alto wine on the floor to the left of it, a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") at the foot of the bed and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and chair to the right. There is an unlocked wooden [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") against the southwest wall, with two more pickaxe to the right, next to the door.

## Notes

- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* describes the building as follows:

:   *"[Karl](/wiki/Skyrim:Karl "Skyrim:Karl") and Irgnir, the workers of Iron-Breaker Mine, live here in this modest dwelling. They have finally saved up enough gold to purchase from [Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Beitild "Skyrim:Beitild"). They sometimes board with [Gjak](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjak "Skyrim:Gjak") and [Bodil](/wiki/Skyrim:Bodil "Skyrim:Bodil"), who take the other shifts to keep the mine constantly productive."*

# Skyrim:Irkngthand

## Overview
