Irkngthand

**Irkngthand** is a large [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") west of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"), [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). It contains four zones: *[Irkngthand Arcanex](#Irkngthand_Arcanex)*, *[Irkngthand Grand Cavern](#Irkngthand_Grand_Cavern)*, *[Irkngthand Slave Pens](#Irkngthand_Slave_Pens)*, and *[Irkngthand Sanctuary](#Irkngthand_Sanctuary)*.

Entrance to the interior is impossible until you have started the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") quest [Blindsighted](/wiki/Skyrim:Blindsighted "Skyrim:Blindsighted"). The ruin contains a large statue depicting a [Snow Elf](/wiki/Lore:Snow_Elf "Lore:Snow Elf") before the race mutated into the Falmer.

## Related Quests

- **[Blindsighted](/wiki/Skyrim:Blindsighted "Skyrim:Blindsighted")**: Stop [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey").
- **[The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny")**: Find items for [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") throughout the [questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Primary_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").

### Exterior

The first bandit preparing a meal while keeping guard

Irkngthand is in a secluded area of Skyrim. The entrance can be reached via a dirt path south from [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn") in [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"). The path soon diverges, with a branch to [Tumble Arch Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Tumble_Arch_Pass "Skyrim:Tumble Arch Pass") to the southwest, so take the eastern path when it splits. You'll find a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") when you're close. The entrance can also be reached by descending the mountain from the south and climbing along a series of wood bridges.

As you pass through the outer wall, a bandit will rise from a seat hidden just behind the bushes and next to a lean-to ahead, and warn you to not approach any closer. If you force hostilities, the bandits farther into the ruins will be alerted to your presence. Be careful if trying to stealthily kill the bandit, as there are another two bandits patrolling the ruins to the west who may spot you.

Also hidden by the bush, along with the chair, is a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), two bedrolls, and a food barrel, with two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") in a pot over the fire, and two [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes") on the ground beside it. Progress is blocked by raised metal spikes, forcing you to go past the two patrolling bandits to bypass the gate. Under the fallen structure to the southwest is a table with an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a leveled potion of healing, a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"). The path narrows after doubling back on itself, and has a few [traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps "Skyrim:Traps"). There is a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") against the wall to the right, another to the left of the path, and a final one to the right of the path, just before the stairs.

At the top of the stairs to the right is a bandit, who is usually sitting in a chair overlooking the entrance, but sometimes patrols to the top of the stairs from the chair. To the left of the stairs is a bedroll with a random healing potion and a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") next to it. Past the bedroll, there is an alcove to the right with two bandits, two bedrolls, two food barrels, an unlocked chest, and a leveled potion of stamina on the table above the chest. There is a tower in the middle of the area from which it is possible to jump along the ruins and skip the next booby-trapped tunnel. The tunnel, lit by a torch, is fairly short, but beware of the [Dwarven pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate"). The plate, located in the center of the tunnel, activates a few [spears](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") from the wall on the right. There is a bandit patrolling the area after the tunnel, where the lever to lower the spikes at the entrance is located.

Past the patrolling bandit is a series of wooden stairs which ascend the cliff face and take you to the top of the ruins. Across the top of the ruins, linked by wooden platforms, is a bandit standing in a corner. Around the corner and across a wooden bridge is the bandit chief, sitting on a stone bench and looking along the path. Beside the bench is an unlocked chest and an adept-locked Dwarven wall chest. This is as far as you can go without having started the quest [Blindsighted](/wiki/Skyrim:Blindsighted "Skyrim:Blindsighted"). It is possible to reach the door to the Arcanex by climbing and descending the mountain behind the ruin, but the door will be key-locked prior to the start of the quest. If Blindsighted has begun, there will be a pair of wooden bridges leading up to the Arcanex from the bandit chief's perch, and the door will be unlocked.

### Irkngthand Arcanex

The remains of a bloody battle

Inside the ruin, a brazier lights the entrance. A bench and two tables are on each side of the entrance chamber. Straight ahead is another table in the entrance to a large room featuring a bandit camp, with five dead bandits. The first three dead bandits are lying beside bedrolls, the fourth is on the first set of stairs after the fire, and the last is at the top of the same stairs. There are two bear traps near the fifth bandit.

By the bedroll to the right as you first come down the stairs is a random healing potion, and to the left, behind the campfire, is an expert-locked chest. If you return to the second highest level and follow it east and south, past four stone benches, you will find an adept-locked Dwarven chest hidden in the rubble. From the last dead bandit past the camp, walk west and north, staying on the same level, and past another four stone benches. There is a master-locked Dwarven chest hidden around the corner.

Just before the exit, to the southwest, is a [Dwarven scuttle](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Scuttle "Skyrim:Dwarven Scuttle") containing a leveled [Dwarven sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere"). There is also a broken Dwarven sphere just past the scuttle. Through the corridor is a room with more remnants of battle: two [Dwarven spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") and a sphere. There is a scuttle on either side of the room, though only the far one contains a sphere. If you turn right after the next gate and follow the ledge to the end, you will find an unlocked Dwarven chest. Be careful, as you must pass another two scuttles with spheres, one in the wall to the right, and one on the level below. At the bottom of the stairs is another sphere waiting in the open, and against the south wall is another unlocked Dwarven chest.

*"This place, it's like a maze. How did the dwarves find their way around?"*

The next room contains a series of six rotating [flamethrower pillars](/wiki/Skyrim:Flamethrower_Statues "Skyrim:Flamethrower Statues"), each with four nozzles. The first two can be evaded by sticking to the walls, and the next three can be evaded by climbing over the rubble, but the last cannot be avoided, because it covers the gate you need to go through to continue. Take care while passing the pillars, as up to four leveled Dwarven spiders may emerge from scuttles in the walls. Past the gate, before the stairs around the corner, is an apprentice-locked Dwarven chest. In the next corridor, just before a lift to the right, is an apprentice-locked Dwarven chest on the wall near an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") set into a table. Strewn across the table are two flasks of [Dwarven oil](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Oil "Skyrim:Dwarven Oil"), a [chaurus egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), two [Falmer ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Ear "Skyrim:Falmer Ear"), a leveled [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), and a random potion of healing, magicka, or stamina. Continuing north past a locked gate to the left, the corridor will ascend a short ramp and end in rubble. There is an unlocked Dwarven chest hidden in the rubble, with a Dwarven spider guarding it. The gate opens above the rubble in the previous room near the fourth flamethrower pillar, and the lift leads to the Grand Cavern.

### Irkngthand Grand Cavern

[Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") and [Karliah](/wiki/Skyrim:Karliah "Skyrim:Karliah") are waiting at the bottom of the stairs after the lift. You are forced into conversation with Karliah, after which you can start the chase through the doors, which are apprentice-[trapped](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") in the bottom left-hand corner. Opening them without first disarming the trap will trigger a [swinging mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace"), the first of many traps set by [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey") to delay and perhaps kill you.

Past the doors, there are two broken Dwarven spiders lying on the floor, and on the stone table in the right-hand corner are three [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and a bottle of [Black-Briar Reserve](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Reserve "Skyrim:Black-Briar Reserve"), with a 'Guild' shadowmark etched into the top of the table. Along the corridor is another broken spider, and behind an expert-locked gate in the left-hand wall is a leveled potion of healing, a potion of strength, an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"), a [sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(item) "Skyrim:Sapphire (item)"), a [gold ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ingot "Skyrim:Gold Ingot"), a [silver ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"), a [Dwarven metal ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Metal_Ingot "Skyrim:Dwarven Metal Ingot"), and an unlocked chest. Past the gate on the right wall is a [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") fungus growing in an unlit lantern holder. In the next room, if you move to the grates and look south, you can observe Mercer stealthily killing two Falmer. Around a corner, another bleeding crown is on the right wall before a pair of closed doors. Through the doors and down the slope are some chaurus egg sacs, after which the corridor soon leads to a large room.

One of the two levers that need to be activated

Upon entering the room, there is a leveled Falmer patrolling from a Falmer tent on your right down to the bottom of connecting stairs and back again. To progress, you need to find and activate two levers, then make your way through the Falmer camp. The first lever is to the left, over the rubble. Sticking to the higher walkway, there is an unlocked Falmer chest around the corner from where you entered. Inside the nearby first tent are five [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), including three bottles of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"). There is a broken Dwarven door to the right as you continue along the path, and an empty Falmer tent on the opposite side. To the northwest of the empty tent is an expert-locked gate, behind which is a [Dwemer ballista](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Ballista "Skyrim:Dwemer Ballista"), aimed at a leveled Falmer below to the west; it is activated by a lever just below it. Past the locked room is the second lever next to an unlocked Dwarven chest. Both levers must be activated within a short time of each other, and can be checked by looking at the cogs on either side of the raised bars below. At the bottom of the connecting stairs down is a dead Falmer. There is also a broken Dwarven sphere in the rubble to the west, and to the north, behind a stone bench, is a novice-locked Dwarven chest.

There are two hidden [spinning blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Blades "Skyrim:Spinning Blades") on the stone path leading to the Falmer camp, marked by stone outcroppings in the ground. The Falmer that the ballista pointed at is to the left, and another Falmer is to the right, above the fungus 'farm'. Two Dwarven spheres can be activated in this area, which the Falmer may accidentally do before you arrive. The two scuttles are on either side of the top level, in the farm section. There is also a Falmer pen to the west containing two skeevers beside the tunnel to the next area. In the farthest northwest corner of the room, on a pile of rocks to the right of a Dwarven scuttle, there is a difficult-to-spot healing potion.

In the 'farm' area to the north and northwest there are numerous harvestable fungal growths: five bleeding crown, four [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), two [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), two [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), four [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), and three [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungi. Also on the top level is an adept-locked Dwarven chest, hidden in the rubble to the right from the top of the stairs. Behind the lower-level tent to the southwest is an imp stool, while another imp stool is just before the tent on the higher level, and a blisterwort is behind it. There are two blisterwort lower down on the same side. There is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") by the higher tent, and on the table opposite, a sample of fly amanita, a [glowing mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom"), two pieces of [chaurus chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Chitin "Skyrim:Chaurus Chitin"), a sample of Namira's rot, and a [skeever tail](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail").

*"Keep as quiet as you can. The Falmer may be blind, but they can still hear us."*

There is a bear trap around the corner in the tunnel to the next open section. There are two paths here, one high and one low. The high path starts to the left, with a short ramp up. As you turn around, a leveled Falmer will walk from the rubble behind the fallen Dwemer structure ahead and crouch down. If you follow the Dwemer-made ramp up and above the entrance to this chamber, you will find a table holding the following [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"): a piece of chaurus chitin, a Falmer ear, two glowing mushrooms, a sample of fly amanita, a skeever tail, and a sample of bleeding crown fungus. From up here, you should be able to see the leveled Falmer guarding the path across the chamber. Looking west, there is one Falmer walking on the ground above the lower path, another Falmer above the Dwemer structure to the left, and another two on the Dwemer structure in the distance to the right. The two highest Falmer are difficult to reach, but they will both drop down to the ground if they detect you and are unable to target you.

If you wish to avoid most of the Falmer, take the lower path. It starts under an improvised bridge patrolled by a Falmer. Follow the winding path, and when it widens again past some fallen stonework, climb the rubble to the left to find a tent. Go around the tent to the right and loot the Falmer chest hidden there, then drop back down to the lower path. Otherwise, you can start by killing the Falmer behind the first structure and proceeding to the chest, then double back to the Dwemer ramp to take care of the rest. From the Dwemer ramp, drop down and then climb the rubble around the front of the first fallen structure. There is one Falmer here, patrolling across the improvised bridge to a tent. There is nothing inside the tent, but growing around it are two bleeding crown, a fly amanita, and two white cap fungi.

The first time you pass the fallen Dwemer structure to the left, the whole chamber will shake. The reason for this is soon apparent: a Dwemer tower at the far end of the chamber has just fallen down. Obviously, you will need to find another way forward, but first descend the steps by the fallen tower to find an adept-locked Dwarven chest in the middle of the rubble. To the left of the stairs is an ascending Dwemer ramp. There are two leveled Falmer patrolling here: one patrols the ramp, while the second patrols the flat section at the top. The second Falmer, a magic-user, carries a [shaman's key](/wiki/Skyrim:Shaman%27s_Key "Skyrim:Shaman's Key").

*"Mercer's been here, I hope we aren't too late."*

Through the pair of doors at the top of a second ramp is a tunnel. In an alcove to the right is a bleeding crown and a Namira's rot fungi. There are three bear traps down the stairs, one on each level. In the room at the bottom of the stairs, there is a dead Falmer lying beside an improvised campfire, over which is a [charred skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") and a few [ruined](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book") and [burned](/wiki/Skyrim:Burned_Book "Skyrim:Burned Book") books. There are also a few loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on the ground near the body and around the room. On a table near the body are two more charred skeever hides and four ruined books. There are several sets of metal shelves by the table holding various [smeltable Dwemer metalwork](/wiki/Skyrim:Ores_and_Ingots#Dwemer_Metal_.28Smeltable.29 "Skyrim:Ores and Ingots"), and hidden under the table are a [scroll of Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Detect_Life "Skyrim:Scroll of Detect Life") and a leveled potion of healing. Around this room there are four wall braziers, with a total of three bleeding crown and a fly amanita growing in them. There is a storeroom to the northwest containing three empty Dwarven chests, more smeltable Dwemer metal on shelves, and a burning torch. There are also two further scrolls of Detect Life in the storeroom: one on the left-hand shelf, and the other to the right behind the gate. There is an "Empty" shadowmark on the empty chest in the middle, and on the wall above is a message written by Mercer Frey. The message reads: *One Step Ahead -Mercer*, and it is laterally inverted (a mirror image).

A Dwarven centurion in its bay

Through the unlocked gate to the southeast are two more bear traps, so avoid them before opening the doors into the next cavern. You can see that the path passes far overhead, but there is a Falmer camp to avoid or destroy first. There is a broken Dwarven sphere in front of you, and at the bottom of the stairs is a [Dwarven centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion") (see [bugs](#Bugs)) in a charging gantry. It will activate upon your approach, but not for the Falmer, even though they pass closer to it. There is a button to activate the centurion near the ground to the right next to the stairs; you can activate it to help thin the number of Falmer in the area. If [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") is installed, there are several [chaurus cocoons](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Cocoon "Skyrim:Chaurus Cocoon")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") by the stream. To safely avoid all of the Falmer in this area, you must first drop down to the ground on the right from the entrance stairs, then follow the stream (which contains two [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)")) until it turns east. (Don't activate the centurion, as this will result in the winner of the resulting battle actively seeking you out.) When the stream turns east, move to the stairs to the south and ascend them. Follow the path to the east, keeping to the walls to prevent the skeevers in the pen from detecting you. Wait in the southeastern corner until the patrolling Falmer is on the ground level, then proceed upwards.

Those wishing to clear out the area can start by dropping down and activating the centurion. There are a total of five leveled Falmer in the area: two in the camp, one patrolling the stream, one on the other side of the camp, and one patrolling the path beyond and above that. In addition, there are two skeevers in a pen to the southeast, between the final two Falmer. Two of the tents in the camp contain hay piles, and there are three harvestable [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") to the north. To the south, across the stream, are six chaurus egg sacs in front of another fungus farm. Growing in the farm area are four Namira's rot, three blisterwort, three imp stool, two white cap, two fly amanita, and one bleeding crown fungi.

Observe their actions and plan ahead

On the other side of the path is a bleeding crown fungus, and another is at the bottom of the stairs just beyond the skeever pen. Ascend the stairs, but be careful on the second set to the left, where a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") on the top step activates a [claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Claw "Skyrim:Claw") trap hidden behind the pillar to the left. The tripwire can be avoided by staying to the right of the stairs. Over to the left is the next set of stairs, with a dead Falmer lying at the bottom, and a fly amanita fungus to the right. Follow the stairs up, then take the bridge across the cavern, looting another dead Falmer in the process. Just before you leave the bridge, look to the southeast and observe the frostbite spiders in a room filled with cobwebs. In the short corridor that follows are three bear traps. The first is in the middle, the second to the left after that, and the third has apparently killed a Falmer, who is lying on top of it.

As you exit the corridor, stop again. Two leveled Falmer should appear and start patrolling across the flat section below to the southeast. You can observe their paths and sneak past if you wish. On the flat section, to the right of the right-hand tent is an unlocked Falmer chest and a [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") that can be looted. Between the left-hand tent and the door to the Slave Pens is an unlocked high-leveled Dwarven wall chest. Opposite the door are the two Falmer killed by Mercer: one on an outcropping, and another to the right and farther away. There are three frostbite spiders and one [spider egg sac](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg") in the spider room.

### Irkngthand Slave Pens

This zone is filled with a misty fog, and is in a rather more decrepit state than the previous zones. In the first room, you will find a Dwarven spider by a short set of ascending stairs which lead to an apprentice-locked gate. The only things of interest behind the gate are a [silver ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"), an [orichalcum ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ingot "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ingot"), and several pieces of smeltable Dwemer metal. Directly south of the stairs is a single glowing mushroom growing on the wall, with another three growing farther to the east. Underneath the three mushrooms is a broken Dwarven sphere, and in the rubble to the left is an unlocked Dwarven chest.

*"Even the Falmer don't deserve the pain these implements must have inflicted."*

East of the stairs are more stairs; descend them, but watch out for the [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") at the top. If you make it to the lever undetected, you can use it to activate a [spinning blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Blades "Skyrim:Spinning Blades") trap, which may kill or injure the two leveled Falmer in the torture room on the level below. You can even watch the deed through the grated fence. Don't forget to turn it off before entering the torture chamber. There is a dead [thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_(Irkngthand) "Skyrim:Thief (Irkngthand)") on one of the racks in the room, who carries a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief%27s_Last_Words "Skyrim:Thief's Last Words") about a captivating discovery. On the table are three [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a [Dwarven dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger") and [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sword "Skyrim:Dwarven Sword"), a [weak poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison"), three bottles of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"), a [weak lingering poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Lingering_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Lingering Poison"), a [lingering stamina poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Lingering_Stamina_Poison "Skyrim:Lingering Stamina Poison"), two [weak aversion to fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Aversion_to_Fire "Skyrim:Weak Aversion to Fire") poisons, a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). To the right of the table is an unlocked Dwarven chest.

There are bone chimes on either side of the exit, but they are of no consequence unless you are trying to sneak past the previous two Falmer. Spread around the next corner are three pressure plates, which activate three different [flame spouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap"): one points east, one south, and the last northwest. There are two skeletons, one lootable, in the room to the left by the fallen gate.

Around the corner past the brazier and fallen gate is a heavily guarded Falmer camp. It is almost impossible to sneak through here with [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), as they will not take the shortcut which requires dropping down off a rock; instead, they will attempt to go through the camp to reach the same area. There is a hay pile in each tent, and two unlocked Falmer chests: one in the first tent on the left, and the other in the third tent on the right. There is a charred skeever over the fire, and some bone chimes hanging from the roof. The bone chimes are merely for decoration, as some of them cannot be reached.

The Falmer have domesticated chaurus

Behind the right-hand tents is another fungus farm, with four white cap, four fly amanita, four Namira's rot, three imp stool, one bleeding crown, and one blisterwort fungi. There is another charred skeever over the campfire by the last tent, and a gate to proceed further. To the north is a table with a dead [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), four pieces of chaurus chitin, a [Falmer helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Helmet "Skyrim:Falmer Helmet"), and a blood-soaked [Falmer shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Shield "Skyrim:Falmer Shield"). To the east are four chaurus egg sacs outside an expert-locked gate to the same section as the previous unlocked gate. There is a total of thirty-eight chaurus egg sacs and a chaurus cocoon[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") in the pen and just inside the tunnel to the southeast. There are a further fourteen chaurus egg sacs through the tunnel, and two imp stool and two fly amanita fungi at the other end between the pipes.

Nowhere to hide, but no enemies to be seen

Around the pipes is yet another Falmer camp; however, this one is possible to bypass. Stick to the wall on the right and follow the raised path, where you will find an apprentice-locked Falmer chest against the right-hand wall, then continue down to where there are two chaurus or [chaurus hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Hunter "Skyrim:Chaurus Hunter")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"). Stick to the left, and quickly move through the glow of the fire when the chaurus have wandered away and are looking elsewhere. There are three Falmer in the first part of the camp: the first is in the tent to the left, the second stands by a Falmer totem to the southwest, and the third is in a line beyond the second. There are two imp stool fungus on either side of the entrance to the camp, and a single spider's egg sac in the cobwebbed area. There is one glowing mushroom on the wall beside the second Falmer, and another on the wall by the ramp down to the second part of the camp.

If you stick to the western wall to the right of this ramp and climb the pipes, they can be followed to the end, where you will find a "Thieves Cache" shadowmark. The reason for this is two potions on the ground below: a leveled healing potion, and a leveled strength potion. There is another chaurus cocoon[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") by the potions. The pipes cannot be used to get followers across the camp stealthily as, once again, they will not jump off the end. The tent to the left of the descending ramp, behind a campfire, contains an expert-locked Falmer chest. Around the next campfire where the chaurus are, there are six white cap fungus, and eight glowing mushrooms on the walls around the camp.

At the end of the second part of the camp and the beginning of the third part, you will find twenty-three chaurus egg sacs, as well as four glowing mushrooms on the walls. There are two more Falmer hiding behind the pillar overlooking the third part of the camp, so beware. This time, your followers will follow you over the drop. To the right of the gate is a level-locked Dwarven chest, while the descending tunnel beyond the gate leads to the door to the Sanctuary.

### Irkngthand Sanctuary

The Great Statue

Other than the impressive statue of a Snow Elf, there are only two dead Falmer to be found in this small zone. You will be forced into conversation with Mercer Frey after which he will start attacking you. He will approach for battle and then disappear in a burst of red light and approach again. Staying back near where you entered this room allows you to watch where he reappears and approaches you again. The room shakes during battle, and once Frey is defeated, the water level will start rising. There is a set of stairs that loops around the back of the statue, but leads nowhere. The exit tunnel is only available after Mercer Frey is dead, and is above the statue's head. The water level rising will allow you to enter a tunnel leading to [Bronze Water Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bronze_Water_Cave "Skyrim:Bronze Water Cave").

Following the quest Blindsighted, the Sanctuary becomes inaccessible from Irkngthand, instead becoming accessible from Bronze Water Cave.

## Notes

- One [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") is outside the entrance to the ruin, outside the stone wall near the rock face, 20-25 steps directly west.
- [Followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") may not enter the interior of Irkngthand, even after you have completed the related quests. They will wait outside the doors to the Arcanex.
- It's possible to reach the door to the Arcanex before the related quest by carefully falling down the mountain behind it. However, the door will be locked and require an unobtainable key.
- The unused message `dunIrkngthandRampartDoorName` would've named a door to "Irkngthand Ramparts", though no such area exists in the game.
- There are three [Shadowmarks](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") found here:
  - a "Guild" shadowmark on top of a table in front of the entrance to the Grand Cavern
  - an "Empty" shadowmark on a chest in the southwestern room of the Grand Cavern (the same room as the mirrored message)
  - a "Cache" shadowmark on top of some pipes at the end of the Slave Pens

## Bugs

- Irkngthand Slave Pens has a one-way drop that will prevent you from being able to leave if you have already completed the Thieves Guild quest Blindsighted.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
  - The `tcl` console command can be used.
  - It is possible to reach the top of the cliff again, but you **need** to have the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). Facing away from the door to the Sanctuary, climb the Falmer tent to your left, jumping repeatedly and working your way up to the top. Once you are at the top, aim at the part of the cliff nearest you (there is a small recess in the cliff edge). Get as close as possible to the cliff edge without falling in height, and use the Whirlwind Sprint Shout. If you do it correctly, you will land on the edge of the cliff.
- One of the Falmer tents is placed too low on the ground. It cannot be entered and can potentially cause you to become trapped inside if a cinematic killcam finisher is played.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- One of the bandits in [Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar") carries a key called the "[Irkngthand Consortium Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand_Consortium_Key "Skyrim:Irkngthand Consortium Key")". However, no such area exists, and the aforementioned key doesn't open anything.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, addresses this issue. The bandit will carry the [Raldbthar Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Keys#Raldbthar_Key "Skyrim:Keys") instead.
- The potions near the Cache shadowmark are intended to be sitting on the shelf on either side of the mark, but due to their placement, they will normally fall to the ground below before you get there.
- The Dwarven centurion may already be destroyed upon entering the chamber.
- The bandits outside of the dungeon respawn despite it being classed as a "no reset zone".
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Iron-Breaker Mine

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Mine: Iron-Breaker Mine ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Iron-Breaker+Mine)) | | |

| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") | 6 |

Iron-Breaker Mine

**Iron-Breaker Mine** is a small [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") in eastern [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). It contains only one zone, *[Iron-Breaker Mine](#Iron-Breaker_Mine)*.

It is owned by [Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Beitild "Skyrim:Beitild"), who will [buy iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore") from you.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Bodil](/wiki/Skyrim:Bodil "Skyrim:Bodil")  [Gjak](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjak "Skyrim:Gjak")  [Karl](/wiki/Skyrim:Karl "Skyrim:Karl") |

## Related Quests

- **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

A [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") is near the mine entrance, which is east of [the White Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Hall "Skyrim:The White Hall"). With *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* installed, a [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Stone_Quarry "Skyrim:Stone Quarry") is just west of the entrance.

### Iron-Breaker Mine

There are six iron ore veins in the mine: one on the floor at the first intersection, one in the southwest dead end at the same intersection, two at the northeast dead end at the second intersection, and two at the far end of the long narrow tunnel past the hole in the floor. The mine also features several [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), shovels, and barrels of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food").

The entrance leads into a tunnel descending to the southeast. At the bottom is a crossroads, with dead ends straight ahead and to the southwest. The mine continues to the northeast, passing a narrow point with wooden shoring. At this point, there is a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Response to Bero's Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Response_to_Bero%27s_Speech "Skyrim:Response to Bero's Speech")* on top of a barrel and a bedroll owned by [Bodil](/wiki/Skyrim:Bodil "Skyrim:Bodil"). Just beyond is a second crossroads, with an extinguished campfire in the center. To the northwest is a barrel containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") among a pile of firewood, while to the northeast is another dead end. Turning to the southeast, the tunnel narrows and starts to twist and turn, eventually rising to another dead end with a round hole in the ground. Dropping through this hole returns you to a dead end near the first junction.

## Notes

- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* describes the mine as follows:

:   *"This mine is located on the outskirts of town to the east. Karl, Irgnir, Gjak, and Bodil work here. This mine produces iron and has a smelter for extracting steel from the iron. Under the watchful (some might say, stern and overbearing) gaze of Beitild, the mine is producing a large amount of ore and is a boon to the local economy."*

- You can take freely everything from inside the mine without being flagged for theft, even if you have yet to sell iron ore to Beitild.

## Bugs

- [Ahkari](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahkari "Skyrim:Ahkari")'s merchant chest, which is underneath the playable map, can be accessed by looking between the three rocks just to the left of the mine entrance.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  Iron-Breaker Mine

# Skyrim:Iron Tusk Cave

## Overview

|  |  |  |

Iron Tusk Cave

**Iron Tusk Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") on the island of [Giant's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Giant's Tooth"). Its humid environment is home to the nearly-extinct Ironwood Tree, which can be harvested for [Ironwood Fruit](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironwood_Fruit "Skyrim:Ironwood Fruit").

## Related Quests

- **[A Dying Wish](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dying_Wish "Skyrim:A Dying Wish")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup"): Make a bitter choice.

### Exterior

The entrance to the cave is next to the giant's camp on Giant's Tooth.

### Iron Tusk Cave

The interior is forested and home to a lone [snow fox](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Fox "Skyrim:Snow Fox"). Several [snowberry bushes](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry") grow here, as well as a [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"). [Jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes") and [butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Butterfly "Skyrim:Butterfly") can also be collected within the cave. You will be sent to harvest Ironwood Fruit from one of the trees here during the related quest. Once you do, two [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") and a [spriggan matron](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan_Matron "Skyrim:Spriggan Matron") will appear and attack you, likely turning the snow fox hostile. There are six Ironwood trees in total, and they can be repeatedly harvested for fruit after the quest is over.

## Gallery

- 

  Interior
- 

  An Ironwood Tree

## Notes

- The ID in the Creation Kit refers to Iron Tusk Cave as *FrozenTusk*.

Ironback Hideout Cellar

**Ironback Hideout Cellar** is a cellar located underneath the ruined house at [Ironback Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout"). It can be accessed via a trapdoor hidden within a tent, although this entrance is initially locked.

Cellar interior

## Related Quests

- **[Night Hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Hunter "Skyrim:Night Hunter")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Elite_Crossbows "Skyrim:Elite Crossbows"): Claim the belongings of a [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") vampire hunter.

## Ironback Hideout Cellar

Once you have obtained the [Ironback Hideout Cellar Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout_Cellar_Key "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout Cellar Key") as part of the related quest, you will be directed to enter the cellar. Within, you will find an uncluttered entrance area containing an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"). The deceased Orc Kragrash used the basement to store his vampire hunting equipment, which is separated from you by a set of bars. The cellar key can be used to unlock the barred door and access these items. Behind the bars you will find a good deal of loot, including a treasure chest and a wall-mounted [silver greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Greatsword "Skyrim:Silver Greatsword"). Laid out on a table you will find an [ebony crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Crossbow "Skyrim:Ebony Crossbow"), an [Elven crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Crossbow "Skyrim:Elven Crossbow"), and several [Exploding Dwarven Bolts of Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Exploding_Dwarven_Bolt_of_Fire "Skyrim:Exploding Dwarven Bolt of Fire") and [Shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Exploding_Dwarven_Bolt_of_Shock "Skyrim:Exploding Dwarven Bolt of Shock"). These crossbow items can usually only be crafted.

# Skyrim:Ironback Hideout

## Overview

Ironback Hideout

**Ironback Hideout** is a dilapidated house to the northwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), a short distance east of [The Steed Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Steed_Stone "Skyrim:The Steed Stone"). It is the remains of a house without a roof, windows, or doors. Two [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and a bandit chief have set up camp within the ruined structure.

It can be reached by following the road towards the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") until you are east of the house and then turning west. Any other route takes a difficult climb over and around cliffs.

The [Elite Crossbows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elite_Crossbows "Skyrim:Elite Crossbows") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") adds a trapdoor beneath a tent, leading to **[Ironback Hideout Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout_Cellar "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout Cellar")**. This entrance is initially locked and must be entered as part of the related quest.

## Related Quests

- **[Night Hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Hunter "Skyrim:Night Hunter")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Elite_Crossbows "Skyrim:Elite Crossbows"): Claim the belongings of a [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") vampire hunter.[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")

## Ironback Hideout

What remains of the house are some of the walls, the fireplace, and floor. There is a broken front porch with a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") at the end, next to a doorway into the shell. Two tents have been erected inside, one of which contains a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). The fireplace is opposite the doorway and is lit, with an empty pot in front of it. With the Elite Crossbows Creation installed, *[Kragrash's Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Kragrash%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Kragrash's Letter")* can be found atop the mantel. There is a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and a bandit chief sitting on a wooden block and crate pulled up in front of the fire. To the right of the fireplace is a long wooden table with an empty metal pot, a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), and a copy of the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_(book) "Skyrim:Beggar (book)")* on the table, and a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") underneath. To the left of the fireplace is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") and a missing section of wall that leads to where one of the bandits is on lookout duty on a ledge and also a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") against the cliff face.

## Notes

- A second corundum ore vein can be found under the house at the base of the cliff.

## Bugs

- It may only become labeled as "cleared" after leaving the area.
- The two regular bandits here are also marked as bosses when only the Bandit Chief should be.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug.
- The chest will respawn extremely quickly if you travel away from the area and then travel back.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.2, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=23107)) The chest's encounter zone setting was incorrectly set, which caused it to reset so quickly. The chest's encounter zone has been corrected, and it now properly resets with the rest of the dungeon.

# Skyrim:Ironbind Barrow

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Ruin.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Ruin.png) | Nordic Ruin: Ironbind Barrow ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ironbind+Barrow)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (storage is [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers")) |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [Frostbite Spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), [Skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), [Skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), [Warlord Gathrik](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlord_Gathrik "Skyrim:Warlord Gathrik") | |

Ironbind Barrow

**Ironbind Barrow** is a small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and the tomb of [Warlord Gathrik](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlord_Gathrik "Skyrim:Warlord Gathrik"). It contains only one zone, *[Ironbind Barrow](#Ironbind_Barrow)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Coming of Age](/wiki/Skyrim:Coming_of_Age "Skyrim:Coming of Age")**: Help a [daring adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Salma "Skyrim:Salma") and [her companion](/wiki/Skyrim:Beem-Ja "Skyrim:Beem-Ja") retrieve their riches.

### Exterior: Camp

The path to the barrow is a short distance along the path east from [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn"). Just before the left-hand path to [Wayward Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Wayward_Pass "Skyrim:Wayward Pass") is a dirt path that cuts back to the northwest. There are two stone pillars near the start of the dirt path, one having fallen over and leaning against the other. There are two [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry") plants along the path, and a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") to the left along the rock face from the last upright stone pillar.

After you pass under the arch, turn right, head up the stairs, turn around, and head over the arch; there is a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and a chest lying in wait. Now head over to the camp, where a lean-to covering a bedroll, a campfire, and the adventurers [Salma](/wiki/Skyrim:Salma "Skyrim:Salma") and [Beem-Ja](/wiki/Skyrim:Beem-Ja "Skyrim:Beem-Ja") wait. They are wary of their own limited combat skills, and are deliberating over whether to tempt fate by raiding the barrow anyway. Once you arrive, they become more willing to enter the barrow.

**Salma**: *"How can you just sit here and wait? We should be in there!"*
**Beem-Ja**: *"We must gather our strength. Who knows what's inside?"*
**Salma**: *"Treasure, that's what! Get off your scaly rump and let's go."*
**Beem-Ja**: *"Hush, Salma. We aren't alone."*

If you enter the barrow without agreeing to accompany them, they will join you regardless. The only way to enter the barrow without them is to kill them outside. Salma's plan is simple: *"Let's clear the place out first. Then we'll gather our loot."* This means that they charge headlong into the barrow, not waiting for you. They cannot be killed by the enemies in the barrow, but they do ensure that this is one place where it is pointless to try to sneak up on enemies. They do not rush too far ahead of you, but instead wait after each section of the barrow for you to catch up, before heading off once again.

There is one more chance to perform a stealthy clear of the room; timed correctly, you can use the pull chain just on the other side of the portcullis to close it before they get through.

### Ironbind Barrow

The tunnel you enter is frozen. There are two [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") around the corner, but they won't detect you until you move forward. There is also a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") around the corner, by the far wall. Down the tunnel are another two frostbite spiders. There are eleven [spider eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg") lying in this chamber, and a web sac hanging from the wall to the right. The next chamber holds a giant frostbite spider; it is on a ledge at the back of the chamber, but quickly makes its way down to attack you. There is nothing else to loot here.

*"This is it. We've found Gathrik's tomb."*

The path continues northwest, and opens up to reveal a hidden Nordic ruin, Gathrik's tomb. Climb the rubble to the left as you emerge, and you will find a [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein"). Ascend the stairs and enter the well-lit area, where there is a gate blocking your path. To the right is a chest in an alcove, and in an alcove to the left there is a handle, which, when pulled, raises the gate.

There are two [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") in the next room, both inside sarcophagi. If you enter the room just enough for your fellow adventurers to move, they will continue onward, not alerting the draugr. Once you have reached the floor grate in the middle of the room, the draugr will emerge and start looking for you. Facing west when on the grate, there is an unlocked chest under the bottom of the wall. To the left of the grate is a leveled [potion of defense](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Defender "Skyrim:Potion of the Defender"). On the table opposite the entrance, there is a [hide shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Shield "Skyrim:Hide Shield"), a [scaled helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Helmet "Skyrim:Scaled Helmet"), a leveled [strength potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and some wine.

The path forward is in the northeast corner and immediately turns west, passing a sideboard on your right holding a two-handed weapon and a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide"). The corridor descends a flight of stairs before opening into a wider corridor heading north. There is a [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") in front of a closed metal gate. Before this gate, there is an alcove to the west containing an unlocked chest with a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") in front of the chest, which activates a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") from the left-hand wall. Beside the chest is a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"). Beyond the gate, the path descends another flight of stairs, where two more skeevers will be alerted to your presence, before the path opens into a room with two draugr, one leveled draugr on the same level who will come charging at you, and another on the lower level, who is an archer. Across the bridge are shelves holding a potion of minor healing. The shelves to the right hold a piece of leather, leather strips, and a random leveled potion. There is another piece of leather, a garnet, a random filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") on a stone table between the two sets of shelves. To the right is an adept-locked chest.

Follow the path through the gate below until you reach a room with a large fire. There are two draugr here. In the rubble on the other side of the room is a potion of minor healing and a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"). To the left of the double doors, themselves situated to the east of the fire, is a set of shelves, which contain a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing") and a random potion. Another set of shelves farther to the left against the north wall hold a potion. There is also a chain to the west of the fire; this opens the grate in the floor above from the room with the first two draugr encountered in the barrow. A few skeletal remains fall down, together with anything you may have left on the grate.

Through the double doors is a corridor which is similar to the corridors found before [puzzle doors](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzles#Dragon_Claw_Switch "Skyrim:Puzzles"). There is a random enchanted helmet on a [pedestal](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate"). Be careful when retrieving this helmet, because once it is removed from the pedestal, spears will shoot up from holes all around the base of the pedestal, and some more will thrust down from above. Removing the helmet causes the gate blocking your progress to lift, but there is also a chain hanging above you that activates the gate, if you don't feel confident of evading the spears. There is also a lever that activates the gate on the other side, which you can use to close the gate behind yourself.

The word wall at Ironbind Barrow

*"This is it! Gathrik awaits us!"*

Around the corner in the next corridor is an iron door which opens to the main chamber of the barrow. Three skeletons and [Warlord Gathrik](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlord_Gathrik "Skyrim:Warlord Gathrik") await to pounce on unwary, unprepared adventurers. On the walkways on either side of the room, archer skeletons patrol, while a mage skeleton is down the stairs. Warlord Gathrik sits in his throne, opposite the entrance, but facing away. Gathrik's throne faces a word wall, which holds a word for the Become Ethereal shout. The boss chest is to the left of the word wall, and around the back of the throne is the unique weapon [Steel Battleaxe of Fiery Souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Battleaxe_of_Fiery_Souls "Skyrim:Steel Battleaxe of Fiery Souls"), a random shield, and two random potions: one potion of the healer, and one potion of strength.

There is a gate to the east at the bottom of the stairs; a chain to the right opens it. There is also a soul gem, a one-handed weapon, and a satchel to the left, on the floor. Follow the winding stairs *all* the way up, and locate the door to the overlook.

### Exterior: Ironbind Overlook

The Dwemer pillars

This is an exterior zone. Open the door by raising the bar to reveal a landscape view of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") to the north, and [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") to the southwest. There is a chest that can be looted to your left.

If you follow the "path" eastward up the mountain (toward the [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Mount_Anthor "Skyrim:Mount Anthor") marker on your compass), you should come across a small Dwemer ruin. It is guarded by two [ice wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith"). All that remains are three pillars; on top of the middle pillar is a collection of seven random [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons") (see [notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironbind_Barrow#notes "Skyrim:Ironbind Barrow")). There are two chests and a random enchanted [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer") at the base of the pillar. Slightly north of the pillars is a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein").

## Notes

- An easy way to retrieve the potions is to use [Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis") while standing higher up the mountainside looking down on the top of the pillar, using either short blasts to pull them off the top of the pillar and letting them drop below for collection, or drawing them to you individually. Using the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout will spread them down the mountainside, where they can be found as far afield as the [Great Lift at Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Lift_at_Alftand "Skyrim:Great Lift at Alftand").
- Another method is to use the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") shout to land on top of the pillar. Jump repeatedly while climbing up the mountainside behind the pillars until you have a good vantage point looking down at the potions. Using the Whirlwind Sprint shout (at one-word strength) can land you on top of the pillar with the potions.
- If Warlord Gathrik uses [Disarm](/wiki/Skyrim:Disarm "Skyrim:Disarm") on Salma, that may cause her to pick up the Battleaxe. If she does, you'll either have to pickpocket the weapon from her, or kill her and loot it from her corpse.

## Bugs

- Although geographically located in the hold of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)"), Ironbind Barrow does not have a hold assigned as its parent location in the game data, making it unavailable for any radiant quests specific to a hold.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
- Beem-Ja may appear without his clothes when he enters the barrow.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
- The helmet trap that opens the door only reacts to direct interactions. If you shoot the helmet off the pedestal with an arrow, the door will not open.
  - You'll have to use the pull chain above and behind the pedestal to continue.
- Sometimes, the Steel Battleaxe of Fiery Souls and the shield will be hovering in the air. This occurs when you are of a high enough level for Warlord Gathrik to be a [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest"). When he gets off the throne, these items will be thrown into space.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  - Shooting the axe with an arrow or spell should cause it to fall to the ground.
  -  Using the console command `player.additem 40002 1` will place a copy of the battleaxe in your inventory.
- The word wall in this dungeon may not give you its word.
- Salma may not leave after you kill Beem-Ja, instead staying near him and looking at him continuously. **?**
  -  In the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"), click on Salma, then enter `disable` followed by `enable`. She'll deliver a final line then leave.
  - Leave the barrow. When you return, she'll be gone.
- The exterior areas respawn despite the dungeon being classed as a "no reset zone".
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
- The area outside the dungeon features dungeon music instead of environmental music. **?**

# Skyrim:Isild River

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page or parts of this page were previously transcluded from lore pages per [this discussion](/wiki/UESPWiki:Community_Portal/Archive_55#Lore_Transclusions_in_Gamespace "UESPWiki:Community Portal/Archive 55").** This page should be checked for potential unrelated lore and other information. Please remove this banner when the page has been cleaned up. |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Body of Water: Isild River ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Isild+River)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Isild_River "Lore:Isild River")) | | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| Northern Solstheim | |

The Isild River

**Isild River** is a river in northern [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") on the [Felsaad Coast](/wiki/Lore:Felsaad_Coast "Lore:Felsaad Coast").

Before the [Red Year](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Red_Year&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Red Year (page does not exist)") of [4E 5](/wiki/Lore:Fourth_Era#4E_5 "Lore:Fourth Era"), the Isild River ran northwest from the frozen [Lake Fjalding](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Fjalding "Skyrim:Lake Fjalding") until it merged with the [Harstrad River](/wiki/Skyrim:Harstrad_River "Skyrim:Harstrad River") at the foot of the [Moesring Mountains](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Moesring_Mountains&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Moesring Mountains (page does not exist)"). The river then continued to its mouth on the icy Felsaad Coast, west of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"). It was reportedly a beautiful part of the island, at the right time of year.

The cataclysms of the Red Year substantially changed the landscape of Solstheim. Many of the landmarks remained the same; the river is still west of Skaal Village and flows from Lake Fjalding to the coast. However, the Isild and Harstrad rivers no longer meet. Instead, each empties separately into a small bay on the northern coast.

## Notes

- The name *isild* comes from Danish and Norwegian words *is* meaning *ice* and *ild* meaning *fire*, translating it to *Icefire River*.

# Skyrim:It's All In The Taste

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Krusty](/wiki/User:Krusty "User:Krusty"), checked by [MolagBallet](/wiki/User:MolagBallet "User:MolagBallet")  **Reward**: written by [Krusty](/wiki/User:Krusty "User:Krusty"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Distribute [Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri")'s [Sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Sujamma "Skyrim:Sadri's Sujamma") to the citizens of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") |
| Location(s): | [The Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch"), [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") |
| Reward: | Leveled gold |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri")) |
| ID: | DLC2RRFavor04 |

Geldis Sadri wants you to distribute his sujamma

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") in the [Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch").
2. Distribute ten jars of [Sadri's Sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Sujamma "Skyrim:Sadri's Sujamma") to citizens of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
3. Return to Sadri at the Retching Netch to receive your reward.

### A New Mixture

In the center of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") is the only inn in town, [the Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch"). The proprietor is [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") and he can be found on his spot behind the bar around the clock. Talk to him and ask about the specialty of the house and he will proudly answer, *"The finest sujamma to cross your lips, friend. My own personal formula that I call "Sadri's Sujamma." In fact, I've just added some new ingredients to the mixture that I think makes it taste better than ever. All I need to do is get the word out that it's ready and they'll flock here for it."* Offer to help him spread the word about the new mixture and he will hand you ten samples of [Sadri's Sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Sujamma "Skyrim:Sadri's Sujamma"). You are now supposed to find ten thirsty citizens that will try out the new drink in town.

The table below shows who will taste the brew, and who will reject it. Note that Bralsa Drel may only take the sujamma after the finishing the Dragonborn questline.

| Name | Dialogue | Accept or Reject? |
| --- | --- | --- |

- Gjalund must be docked in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.1.0, fixes this bug.

### Reward

Once you have distributed all ten samples of the sujamma, return to Geldis Sadri and tell him the good news. He will be happy about the publicity and say, *"Perfect! All that's left now is to go ahead and wait for the patrons to come in. As promised, here's a little something for yourself."* He will then hand you a leveled amount of gold as reward, finishing the quest.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-29 | 250 |
| 30-39 | 500 |
| 40-49 | 1000 |
| 50-59 | 1500 |
| 60+ | 2000 |

## Notes

- If you wait 24 in-game hours after an NPC accepts a sample of the sujamma, you can give them another sample which adds to your total count.
- There are 13 possible people who will accept sujamma. Two of them are from the Severin family, whom you may have to kill as part of a quest; Drovas will be unavailable after [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward"); and Bralsa Drel will be unavailable until you complete another quest, but there will still always be the other 10 possibilities unless one or more of them are killed by other means.
- Unlike other quest items, Sadri's Sujamma is disposable. Make sure to keep them in your inventory while moving your belongings to chests.
- If you drop all of your bottles of Sadri's Sujamma before giving them to 10 people, you can ask him for more, and he will give you 2 more bottles. You can do this as many times as you like until you give 10 people the sujamma.

## Quest Stages

| It's All In The Taste (DLC2RRFavor04) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Distribute Sadri's Sujamma (<Global=DLC2RRF04DrinkCount>/10) |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Tell Geldis Sadri you've distributed his liquor samples |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 25.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2RRFavor04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2RRFavor04`.

# Skyrim:Items

## Overview

Skyrim is full of **items** both magical and mundane. The articles listed here provide information on all items in the game.

## Finding Items

Depending upon whether you are looking for a specific item or just browsing for general information, there are several different ways to navigate through the many item-related pages.

### Search

If you know the exact name of the specific item you want to find, you can search for it [here](/wiki/Special:Search "Special:Search") or at the search box at the top of the page.
0x000F71CD

### Categories

Within the category **[Skyrim-Items](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Items "Category:Skyrim-Items")** are many subcategories listing nearly every item in the game by function. If you don't know the exact spelling of a specific item, browsing through one of the categories may help you to find it.

### General Articles on Items

Most of these articles provide general information on various types of items, and also include lists of the mundane (non-enchanted and widely available) varieties of the items.

- [Ammunition](/wiki/Skyrim:Ammunition "Skyrim:Ammunition"): All arrows and bolts, magical and non-magical
- [Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"): Base unenchanted armor
- [Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"): All books in the game
- [Clothing](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing"): Base unenchanted clothing and jewelry
- [Food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"): Ingredients that can be eaten raw or [cooked](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking")
- [Ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"): A complete list of alchemical ingredients
- [Keys](/wiki/Skyrim:Keys "Skyrim:Keys"): A list of all keys in the game
- [Miscellaneous Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items"): Includes gems, minor quest items, etc.
- [Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Notes "Skyrim:Notes"): Random notes and letters found in the game
- [Ores and Ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ores_and_Ingots "Skyrim:Ores and Ingots"): Includes scrap and dwarven metal
- [Permanent Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Permanent_Items "Skyrim:Permanent Items"): Items preventing corpses from being erased, useful for necromancers
- [Potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"): All potions, beverages, and poisons
- [Quest Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items "Skyrim:Quest Items"): All quest items found in-game that cannot, for at least a time, be removed from your inventory
- [Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"): All soul gems in the game and how to use them
- [Specialty Gear](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"): Faction specific armor as well as some miscellaneous apparel
- [Template Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Template_Items "Skyrim:Template Items"): Items whose sole purpose is to define other items
- [Unobtainable Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Unobtainable_Items "Skyrim:Unobtainable Items"): Items which either cannot be seen or equipped by the player or which exist only in the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit") and cannot be seen without the use of the console.
- [Weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"): Base unenchanted weapons

### Articles on Enchanted Items

These articles provide lists of all the enchanted items available in the game, organized according to how you are likely to find or obtain the item.

- [Magic Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Items "Skyrim:Magic Items"): General information about magic items
- [Artifacts](/wiki/Skyrim:Artifacts "Skyrim:Artifacts"): Truly legendary items unlike anything else in appearance or attributes
- [Generic Magic Weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"): All enchanted weapons found in random loot
- [Generic Magic Apparel](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel"): All enchanted armor, clothing, and jewelry found in random loot
- [Magic Items with Guaranteed Locations](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Items_with_Guaranteed_Locations "Skyrim:Magic Items with Guaranteed Locations"): A list of guaranteed generic magic items
- [Leveled Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Items "Skyrim:Leveled Items"): Items obtained as quest rewards whose attributes depend on your level when you obtain them
- [Scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls "Skyrim:Scrolls"): All magic scrolls in the game
- [Staves](/wiki/Skyrim:Staves "Skyrim:Staves"): All the varieties of magical staves found in the game
- [Unique Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Unique_Items "Skyrim:Unique Items"): Unique items with fixed attributes that are only found in one place

### Articles on Item Materials

Each of these articles provides complete information on an item material: where to obtain the material, [smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") requirements to craft items, and full information on all [Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"), [Jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Jewelry "Skyrim:Jewelry"), and [Weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") made out of the material.

- [Advanced Armors](/wiki/Skyrim:Advanced_Armors "Skyrim:Advanced Armors") (including [Scaled](/wiki/Skyrim:Advanced_Armors#Scaled_Armor "Skyrim:Advanced Armors") and [Steel Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Advanced_Armors#Steel_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Advanced Armors"))
- [Amber](/wiki/Skyrim:Amber "Skyrim:Amber")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers")
- [Corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum "Skyrim:Corundum")
- [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric") (including Daedric Mail[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail"))
- [Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark "Skyrim:Dark")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers")
- [Dragon Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Items "Skyrim:Dragon Items") (including [Dragonscale](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Items#Dragonplate_Armor "Skyrim:Dragon Items") and [Dragonplate](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Items#Dragonscale_Armor "Skyrim:Dragon Items"))
- [Dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven "Skyrim:Dwarven") (including Dwarven Mail[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dwarven_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dwarven Mail"))
- [Elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") (including [Moonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") ore)
- [Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony")
- [Golden](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden "Skyrim:Golden")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers")
- [Glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite "Skyrim:Malachite") (including [Malachite](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite "Skyrim:Malachite") ore)
- [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold")
- [Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron")
- [Leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather "Skyrim:Leather")
- [Madness Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Madness_Ore "Skyrim:Madness Ore")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers")
- [Netch Leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Leather "Skyrim:Netch Leather")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Netch Leather Armor") (including Boiled Netch Leather, Shadowed Netch Leather, Shadowed Boiled Netch Leather)
- [Orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish "Skyrim:Orcish") (including [Orichalcum](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish "Skyrim:Orcish") ore)
- [Quicksilver](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver "Skyrim:Quicksilver")
- [Silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver")
- [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge")-specific items ([Ancient Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Equipment "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Equipment") and [Nord Hero](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge#Nord_Hero_Weapons "Skyrim:Skyforge"))
- [Spell Knight Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Knight_Armor_(item) "Skyrim:Spell Knight Armor (item)")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Spell Knight Armor") (Iron Spell Knight, Steel Spell Knight, Ebony Spell Knight)
- [Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
- [Steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel")
- [Vigil Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_Armor "Skyrim:Vigil Armor")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_Enforcer_Armor_Set "Skyrim:Vigil Enforcer Armor Set") (including Vigil Corrupted, Vigil Enforcer, Vigil Silver Hand, Vigil Veteran)

### Creating Custom Items

- [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy"): Create your own custom potions.
- [Baking](/wiki/Skyrim:Baking "Skyrim:Baking")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"): Create custom recipes at an oven.
- [Cooking](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking"): Create custom recipes at a cooking pot or spit.
- [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting"): Create enchantments for armor, clothes, and weapons.
- [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing"): Create and improve unenchanted armor and weapons.

### Official Add-Ons

Three of the [official add-ons](/wiki/Skyrim:Add-ons "Skyrim:Add-ons") add enough items that they are listed on their own pages. The fourth item listed takes you to a list of Creation Club items.

- [Dawnguard Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Items "Skyrim:Dawnguard Items"): New items added by the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") add-on.
- [Hearthfire Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire_Items "Skyrim:Hearthfire Items"): New items added by the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on.
- [Dragonborn Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Items "Skyrim:Dragonborn Items"): New items added by the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") add-on.
- [Creation Club Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club_Items "Skyrim:Creation Club Items"): New items separately added by Creation Club.

# Skyrim:Ivarstead

## Overview
