Ivarstead

**Ivarstead** is a milling [town](/wiki/Skyrim:Towns "Skyrim:Towns") in the western [Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift").

It is at the base of the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World") on the shores of [Lake Geir](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Geir "Skyrim:Lake Geir"), with one of the forks of the [Darkwater River](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_River "Skyrim:Darkwater River") powering the sawmill on its way to join the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"). The town consists of five buildings, with [Shroud Hearth Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shroud_Hearth_Barrow "Skyrim:Shroud Hearth Barrow") just to the east overshadowing the settlement. Some of the town's residents believe the barrow to be haunted; the innkeeper [Wilhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Wilhelm "Skyrim:Wilhelm") willingly tells you more. He runs [Vilemyr Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilemyr_Inn "Skyrim:Vilemyr Inn") at the southern end of the town opposite [Klimmek's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Klimmek%27s_House "Skyrim:Klimmek's House"). To the north is [Fellstar Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellstar_Farm "Skyrim:Fellstar Farm") opposite [Temba Wide-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Temba_Wide-Arm "Skyrim:Temba Wide-Arm")'s sawmill, and across the river is [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi")'s destroyed house.

It is a town in decline, with fewer travelers visiting since the haunting of the barrow began. Some residents fear for the town's survival, as many of the townspeople have either left for [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") or want to move away. Pilgrims and travelers often pass through the town on their way up the "[7,000 steps](/wiki/Skyrim:Climb_the_Steps "Skyrim:Climb the Steps")" to [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar").

#### Miscellaneous Quests

#### Main Quest

- **[The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice")**: Meet the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards").

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Kill Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Narfi "Skyrim:Kill Narfi")**: Kill a hapless [beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi") in Ivarstead.

#### Side Quests

- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.

#### Miscellaneous Quests

- **[Hunt and Gather](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunt_and_Gather "Skyrim:Hunt and Gather")**: Retrieve [Wylandriah](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah "Skyrim:Wylandriah")'s [spoon](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah%27s_Spoon "Skyrim:Wylandriah's Spoon"), [ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Orichalcum_Ingot "Skyrim:Quest Items"), and [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah%27s_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Wylandriah's Soul Gem").
- **[The Lover's Requital](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lover%27s_Requital "Skyrim:The Lover's Requital")**: Help [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar") locate his former [fiancée](/wiki/Skyrim:Svidi "Skyrim:Svidi"), so he can kill her.
- **[Under the Table](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_the_Table "Skyrim:Under the Table")**: Deliver a smuggled Black-Briar Mead keg to the inn at Ivarstead.

## Notes

- If *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* is installed, one [clay deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay "Skyrim:Clay") is southeast of [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi")'s dilapidated house and one [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Stone_Quarry "Skyrim:Stone Quarry") is west of it. 2 more clay deposits are on opposite sides of the bridge on the southern edge of town.
- Ivarstead is marked on your map without anyone mentioning the town once you start the quest [The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice") (from [Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater")).
- You can ask all residents except Narfi what they know about High Hrothgar.
- After the main quest is completed, if you look up at the Throat of the World, you may see the dragon [Odahviing](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing") flying around.
- Ivarstead also [appears](/wiki/Online:Ivarstead "Online:Ivarstead") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

# Skyrim:J'zargo's Experiment

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-College of Winterhold.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-College_of_Winterhold.png) | **Help [a student](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo "Skyrim:J'zargo") test out a fiery new spell.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [J'zargo](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo "Skyrim:J'zargo") |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | J'zargo as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), unused [scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo%27s_Flame_Cloak_Scroll "Skyrim:J'zargo's Flame Cloak Scroll") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([J'zargo](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo "Skyrim:J'zargo")) |
| ID: | MGRAppJzargo01 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal") | | |

J'zargo does not want to test all of his spells on his own

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Obtain the [scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo%27s_Flame_Cloak_Scroll "Skyrim:J'zargo's Flame Cloak Scroll") from [J'zargo](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo "Skyrim:J'zargo").
2. Use the scrolls to kill at least three undead enemies.
3. Return to J'zargo with your results.

### A Simple Request

If you attended [Tolfdir's](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") [lecture](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons") when you joined the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") you may have run into a conceited [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit") named [J'zargo](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo "Skyrim:J'zargo"). J'zargo is ambitious and after your adventures [under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal"), he tries to ingratiate himself and ask for your assistance: *"J'zargo has seen that Tolfdir likes you. You must be very skilled with magic, yes? J'zargo is working hard, but cannot do it alone. Can you help with this?"* It seems he has developed a new [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo%27s_Flame_Cloak_Scroll "Skyrim:J'zargo's Flame Cloak Scroll") that is especially effective against the [undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead "Skyrim:Undead"). J'zargo will give you ten scrolls and send you on your way with instructions to report back on their efficacy.

### The Scrolls vs. The Undead

Candidates for J'zargo's scrolls are [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), [ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost "Skyrim:Ghost") and [zombies](/wiki/Skyrim:Zombie "Skyrim:Zombie"), any of which can be encountered in Skyrim's numerous [barrows, tombs or ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins"). Undead may also be encountered in [The Midden](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Midden "Skyrim:The Midden"), allowing convenient completion of this quest without travel if the quest has been accepted before the first venture down there. Otherwise, the Halls of the Dead in Whiterun and Solitude are also home to a sufficient number of easily accessible, weak undead. Just be sure to order your followers to wait outside, as they may kill the undead before you, or be harmed by the scrolls.

To complete the quest, you will need to destroy three undead enemies while employing the scrolls. A quest marker will appear with each undead killed while under the effects of J'zargo's Flame Cloak. Undead do not need to be killed by the scrolls' damage; dying of other weapon or spell damage while under the effects of the scroll will satisfy the quest conditions. However, undead that are killed indirectly by the explosions of other undead do not count. If you use up all ten scrolls without killing three undead enemies, the quest will fail.

### A Slight Oversight

The scrolls inflict ten points of fire damage per second for thirty seconds. Enemies on fire take extra damage. However, to accomplish this, J'zargo's cloak causes a massive explosion making the scrolls as harmful to you and your allies as to the undead, so ask your [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") to stay behind when you test the scrolls, as the damage may kill them or turn them hostile. The scrolls can kill instantly if you are weakened with low reserves or health. Also, be wary of using a scroll when dealing with multiple undead enemies, as the multiplied effects of the ensuing explosions can be extremely damaging.

### A Job "Well Done"

Return to J'zargo after you have killed three undead to report the unfortunate side-effect. Knowing J'zargo and his ambitious intentions, you can ask him about the dubious nature of this experiment and your involvement in it. He will assure you that he meant you no harm, and was quite unsure of the effects the scrolls would have on the wielder. Upon finishing the quest you may keep the remaining scrolls and he will be accessible as a follower.

## Notes

- The scrolls also work on [undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead "Skyrim:Undead") that you have [reanimated](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate "Skyrim:Reanimate") or [conjured](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Magic#Conjuration_Spells "Skyrim:Dawnguard Magic") yourself. This does not work on reanimated animals or non-enemy humanoids.
- The scroll must actually damage the undead for the quest to register the kill, activating the scroll from a distance and killing the enemy by other means won't work.
- Activating a scroll near a draugr sarcophagus will trigger the draugr to come out.
- Activating a scroll near most followers will cause them to either retaliate or leave your service, sometimes resulting in a bounty even if you are within a dungeon.
- The active effect "J'zargo's Flame Cloak" is listed as a harmful effect, presumably because the explosion it causes damages you as well as your enemy. You can counteract this by using the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout to take advantage of the explosion without receiving damage.
- It is suggested not to give the scrolls to a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") to carry, as they will spam the fireballs at any enemy regardless of if they're undead or not. This is doubly important if you have not yet completed the quest as there is no way to obtain more copies of the scroll.
- The required kills need to be done one at a time. Killing 3 undead enemies simultaneously (e.g. the 3 skeletons in Whiterun's Hall of the Dead, all killed with a single activation of the scrolls' effect) will only credit you with 1 kill.

## Bugs

- If more than three undead are killed by the scrolls' effects, which is very possible, e.g. fighting two undead with the counter already at two, then stage 30 may not occur; J'zargo won't have the dialogue option and the quest may be unfinishable.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- You cannot speak to J'zargo if the quest [The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus") is active.

## Quest Stages

| J'zargo's Experiment (MGRAppJzargo01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | J'zargo has asked for help with a project he's been working on. I'm supposed to test out Flame Cloak scrolls he made, and report back to him when I've tried them out on several undead creatures. *Objective 20:* Test J'zargo's Flame Cloak spell on the undead (<Global=MGRJ1Test>/3) |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Speak to J'zargo |
| 200 | ☑ | I've informed J'zargo that the Flame Cloak scrolls he created don't work exactly as he intended. I doubt he'll be asking for additional help. |
| 255 | ☒ | I told J'zargo that I ran out of the scrolls he'd given me, and he no longer wants my help. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MGRAppJzargo01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MGRAppJzargo01`.

# Skyrim:Jails

## Overview

Dragonsreach Dungeon

This pages lists all the **jails** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

:   **[Castle Dour Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour_Dungeon "Skyrim:Castle Dour Dungeon")** — A large fortress in Solitude which acts as the headquarters of the Imperial Legion and residence of the Emperor in Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Dour)
:   **[The Bulwark Jail](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bulwark_Jail "Skyrim:The Bulwark Jail")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — The jail in Raven Rock, built directly into the Bulwark. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=The+Bulwark+Jail)
:   **[The Chill](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Chill "Skyrim:The Chill")** — The jail for Winterhold, located on an island north-northeast of the College of Winterhold and northeast of Septimus Signus's Outpost, across the sea. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Chill)
:   **[Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine")** — A medium-sized silver mine and forced-labor prison camp in southern Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cidhna+Mine)
:   **[Dawnstar Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Barracks "Skyrim:Dawnstar Barracks")** — The living quarters for the Dawnstar guards. It also houses Dawnstar's jail. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dawnstar+Barracks)
:    **[Dragonsreach Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach_Dungeon "Skyrim:Dragonsreach Dungeon")** — The residence of the Jarl of Whiterun Hold, the hold's seat of political power, and the location of the hold's jail. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragonsreach)
:   **[Falkreath Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Barracks "Skyrim:Falkreath Barracks")** — The living quarters for the Falkreath guards and also contains Falkreath Hold's jail. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath+Barracks)
:   **[Guardhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Guardhouse "Skyrim:Guardhouse")** — The Hjaalmarch barracks on the south side of Morthal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Guardhouse)
:    **[Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings")** — A large castle at the far end of the Valunstrad district in Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Palace+of+the+Kings)
:   **[Riften Jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Jail "Skyrim:Riften Jail")** — The jail in Riften found below Mistveil Keep. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Riften+Jail)

## Overview

Jala's House

**Jala's House** is a small house owned by [Jala](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala "Skyrim:Jala") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), located next to the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College"). She lives there along with [Ahtar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahtar "Skyrim:Ahtar").

The interior of Jala's house

Jala leaves her house every morning and returns home at 8pm. The house is locked while she is away.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Ahtar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahtar "Skyrim:Ahtar") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower")  [Jala](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala "Skyrim:Jala") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink") \* |

\* This person only sells goods at the market.

## Related Quests

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Jala's house backs onto [Evette San's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Evette San's House") and the entrance is opposite the courtyard in front of the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College"). There are three [dragon's Tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") plants growing along the side of her house. There is an  "Empty") Empty [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") on a barrel by the entrance door, which is novice-locked.

### Jala's House

Upon entering you are in a large room with the staircase to the top floor in front of you. On your right as you enter is a small unit holding a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") and a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"). On your left is a table holding two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), several cheese wheels and wedges, a [seared slaughtergish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg") and a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"). Against the southeast wall is a small set of shelves with more bread and cheese, along with a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and potatoes. To the right of this is a basket on the floor containing two cabbages and several potatoes and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") that has fallen from a rack overhead. There are a total of three racks hanging from the ceiling holding three further pheasant, two [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") and four [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). On the floor, next to the same wall is a copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Song Of Hrormir](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_Of_Hrormir "Skyrim:Song Of Hrormir")*. Above the book there is a wall shelf holding a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine").

Under the stairs are a pile of sacks, all containing foodstuffs. In the northern corner of the room are two sets of shelves containing more loaves of bread, several cheese wheels and wedges, more potatoes and cabbages, an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") and an [iron ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"). To the left of the shelves is a barrel with a further eight iron ingot on top. There are three barrels, more sacks and a basket all containing [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). In the western corner is a doorway to a bedroom with an open crate to the right of the doorway, it contains a sample of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") and an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing").

In the bedroom, the bed is in the western corner with a couple of sacks of food at the foot of the bed. There is an end table to the right of the bed with a bottle of wine on top. To the right of this is a small unit holding a woodcutter's axe, a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and an open crate containing the same as the one by the doorway. There is a wall shelf above the unit holding a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse").

Climbing the stairs, there is a small set of shelves in front of you holding a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk"), a [cave bear pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Cave_Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Cave Bear Pelt"), a [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") and a basket containing two bunches of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"). Along the northwest wall is a table and chairs with a loaf of bread and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge") on top. Against the southwest wall is a dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and having a bunch of lavender and a bowl containing a red and [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"). To the left of this is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), that may be empty. Opposite is a second chest, also unlocked and potentially empty. To the right of the second chest, in the eastern corner of a railing is a single unowned bed, with an end table holding an iron helmet beside it.

## Notes

- The [key to the house](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Jala%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Jala's House") is carried by Ahtar and Jala.
- There is an  "Empty") Empty [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") on a barrel by the entrance door, even though the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") considers her house to be a wealthy house. The house will not be empty if you are sent here on one of [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex")'s thievery jobs.
- If you are sent here for [The Burglary Job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job"), the required item is found on a nightstand upstairs.

# Skyrim:Japhet's Folly

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Settlement.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Settlement.png) | Settlement: Japhet's Folly ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Japhet%27s+Folly)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Japhet%27s_Folly "Lore:Japhet's Folly")) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (see [notes](#Notes) and [bugs](#Bugs)) |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Blood Horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker"), [Haldyn](/wiki/Skyrim:Haldyn "Skyrim:Haldyn") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| JaphetsFollyOrigin, JaphetsFolly02 | |
| Region | |
| [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Arcane Enchanters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") | 1 |
| # of [Grindstones](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") | 1 |
| # of [Workbenches](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") | 1 |

Japhet's Folly

**Japhet's Folly** is a self-contained [worldspace](/wiki/Skyrim:Worldspaces "Skyrim:Worldspaces") far northeast of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") containing [Blood Horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker") and their leader [Haldyn](/wiki/Skyrim:Haldyn "Skyrim:Haldyn"). It contains only one zone, *[Japhet's Folly Towers](#Japhet.27s_Folly_Towers)*.

It is on the remote Rockjoint Island in the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts"), and may only be visited during the quest [Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East") (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

## Related Quests

- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").

### Japhet's Folly Towers

Entry is made via the [Sea Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_Cave "Skyrim:Sea Cave") under the fort, and can only happen during the related quest (see [bugs](#Bugs) for details). The door into the fort leads to the bottom of a curving staircase typical in Nordic forts. On your right is a storage area containing many crates, barrels, and sacks of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), as well as two sets of shelves holding mainly clutter, four loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), or [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"). There is a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on a stack of crates, and by the bottom of the stairs is a long wooden table with seven loose coins and a bottle of [Honningbrew Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") on top. You can hear some of the Blood Horkers talking above, so caution is advised.

At the top of the first flight of stairs is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that triggers a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") on the left. There are two barrels on the right with a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on top. There is a second flight of stairs rising behind. A Blood Horker is patrolling up and down this second flight of stairs, and another is resting in the room at the top. At the top of the stairs is a table with two loose [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"), five loose coins, and a random quiver of [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows") on top. To the right is a circular room containing three unowned bedrolls, a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), and an open, empty chest. There are also several sacks around the room. To the southeast is a wooden door, and to the southwest is an alcove, where more stairs would have originally been; however, these have caved in. There is a table and chair near the cave-in, with a bottle of Nord mead and a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") on top. Beside the table is a stack of crates with a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") on top, several sacks, and another open, empty chest.

Behind the door to the southeast is a wide passage with a set of shelves on the left and several stacks of crates along it. The shelves hold three bottles of Nord mead, two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and another cheese wheel. A bit farther along is a small shelving unit on the right with an unlocked chest on top. Next on the left is a key-locked wooden door leading to the [exterior](#Exterior). To the left of the door is a stack of crates. This door will serve as your exit later.

Past the door is a table on the right and a couple more stacks of crates near the end. The passage opens into a large circular room with a single Blood Horker patrolling from this room and down some stairs to the southwest. There are also more stairs to the northeast climbing higher. The room itself contains a table against the wall to the north with a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets") on top. A set of shelves to the east has an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") on top. In the western corner, behind some rubble near the top of the stairs the Blood Horker is patrolling, an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") and a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") are on the ground. The stairs descend, passing some barrels and sacks on the first landing, then a wardrobe with a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") on top on the second landing. At the bottom is a long table with seven loose coins and a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on top. Beyond this is a small table and chairs where two Blood Horkers sit. There are another nineteen loose coins on this table, suggesting the bandits were gambling. Beyond this is another circular room on the left, and past this another table with three samples of [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), two [briar hearts](/wiki/Skyrim:Briar_Heart "Skyrim:Briar Heart"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), and a [vigor poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigor_Poison "Skyrim:Vigor Poison") on top. Against the rear wall are more crates with another gourd on top. There is also an expert-locked wooden door to the northeast.

The circular room contains a table that has been used for butchering meat, with two fillets of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat"), two [raw rabbit legs](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), a haunch of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"), and an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe") on top. An apprentice-locked chest is nearby, as are two sets of shelves holding four loaves of bread, four [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steak, a sample of slaughterfish scales, a haunch of raw venison, several pieces of cheese, two fillets of [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat"), a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), and a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). Between the two shelving units is a barrel with another fillet of horker meat on top. There are also several racks hanging from the ceiling holding a total of eight [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and six [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). Finally, there is a barrel by a central pillar containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients").

Behind the expert-locked door is a small room filled with cobwebs, with a small table with the body of [Japhet](/wiki/Skyrim:Japhet "Skyrim:Japhet"), who carries a few coins, in front. On the table is his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Japhet%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Japhet's Journal") and a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), and in the corner is a master-locked chest.

Climbing back up to the room above and taking the exit to the northeast, there are spear holes in the ground in the doorway, and a table by the bottom of the stairs leading up, with two random potions of magicka, an empty [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"), and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on top. As you climb the stairs, you will hear the spears blocking the route back. At the top of the first flight is a small table with a sample of [small antlers](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Antlers "Skyrim:Small Antlers") and an empty petty soul gem on top. Haldyn will be alerted to your presence; he uses strong shock magic and is wearing leveled heavy armor. He carries a copy of the [Japhet's Folly Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Japhet%27s_Folly_Key "Skyrim:Japhet's Folly Key"). Once he is dead, the East Empire Company will start the bombardment.

The room at the top contains two sets of shelves holding a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), two [grass pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod"), a [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") flower, and several items of crockery including a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") containing two [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"), as well as a small table with a leveled, empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") on top. Hanging from the ceiling are three bunches of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") and two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). To the southeast is a room containing an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), a small shelving unit holding four common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") and a random potion of healing, magicka, or stamina, an unlocked chest, a dresser of clothes, and a soul gem stand holding a random filled soul gem to the right of the dresser. When Haldyn dies, the spears at the bottom of the stairs lower, allowing access back the way you came. Returning to the wide corridor and the door to the outside, you will see the end of the passage has collapsed due to the bombardment. Thus, your only option is to exit through the door out onto the island.

### Exterior

Japhet's Folly under attack

The exterior before the bombardment starts consists of a series of buildings on descending levels, with wooden palisades separating the levels descending toward the docks. The first wooden palisade has gates in the middle. Through the gates are a total of four Blood Horkers, including two magic users who can be very challenging, as they use strong fire and storm spells. The first level has a campfire between two shacks. The shack on the left has a woodshed containing a woodcutter's axe, and inside the shack are two unowned bedrolls, a barrel, and a small table with a fillet of horker meat and a loaf of bread on top. The shack on the right contains a counter and several small tables and chairs, and is set up as a bar. There is a bottle of Nord mead on the counter, and behind it is a cupboard with four more bottles of Nord mead and three pieces of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef") on the shelves.

Through a gap in the next wooden palisade are two more shacks. The shack on the right has an unowned bedroll inside. The shack on the left has two sets of shelves holding four fillets of salmon meat, three fillets of horker meat, four seared slaughterfish steaks, and two samples of slaughterfish scales. There is a firepit beside this shack, with a rack holding seven whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") hanging over it. From here there is a wooden ramp down between another wooden palisade to another level with three more shacks. The left shack contains a long wooden table with [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") consisting of three random [helmets](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), two pairs of random [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets"), and a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") on top, and two pairs of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor") underneath. In front of this shack is a table with many unusable barrels stacked behind, and eight bottles of Nord mead on and around the table. The middle shack is completely empty. The right shack has a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") in front, with a [steel greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Steel Greatsword") on top of the workbench, and two baskets beside the workbench containing three [iron maces](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") and an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"). Inside the shack is a long table with four [iron daggers](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), an iron mace, and an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe") on top.

Through another gate in another wooden palisade and down another wooden ramp is a final level, where there are two more shacks. The shack on the left contains an unowned single bed at one end and two unowned bedrolls at the other. The last shack on the right contains only unusable barrels. Down on the docks is a fifth Blood Horker, who is an archer guarding the docks and two boats. The boat to the southeast has a table on deck, with two fillets of horker meat and several pieces of cheese on top. The second boat to the northwest has three weapon racks holding two random [bows](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), and a table with a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") on top.

Once you have killed Haldyn, the ships brought by the East Empire Company start a bombardment which destroys all the shacks, sets fire to them, and scatters the items everywhere. You may find a few of the items lying around, but most will be lost. Taking on the Blood Horkers during the bombardment can make the battle much harder. The key carried by Haldyn opens the master-locked stockade gate closest to the docks. When you reach the table and barrels and the completely empty shack, there is now an unlocked chest containing minor loot partially buried in the floor of the shack. Down by the docks, you may find and get attacked by a single [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") before reaching and speaking to [Adelaisa](/wiki/Skyrim:Adelaisa_Vendicci "Skyrim:Adelaisa Vendicci").

## Notes

- You are unable to travel to Japhet's Folly before the quest Rise in the East.
- Do not return to Japhet's Folly via the Sea Cave after the bombardment has started, or you will be trapped. The top area of Japhet's Folly will be blocked by rubble, and the door from the Sea Cave will be gone, preventing you from returning back the way you came.
- Do not store anything in containers outside the fort. The containers may be destroyed and disappear once the bombardment has begun, and their contents may be lost.
- If you attempt to swim away from the island, you will be blocked by an invisible barrier in the water.
- Japhet and his journal are in the lowest part of the tower in a locked room. A locked chest can also be found here.
- According to the game data, the fort area is under the encounter zone of Rockjoint Island.

## Bugs

- Once you have discovered the location via the quest, do not return, as you will be unable to depart. Japhet's Folly has its own worldspace in the game, and has invisible boundaries which you cannot swim past. You are also unable to fast travel away from Japhet's Folly; you are presented with the same message as when trying to fast travel from an indoor place.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
  -  You can avoid being locked in Japhet's Folly by using the console command `coc whiterun` to teleport out.
- The standalone bandit on the island isn't affiliated with the Blood Horkers like everyone else.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.5, fixes this bug.
- If you go to Japhet's Folly with a follower, your follower may disappear.
- The explosions bombarding the tower are invisible arrows with no name. You can collect these arrows by getting hit; to use them, you must use your last standard arrow, and the invisible arrows will then become equipped.
- If you have exited the towers and proceeded through the quest to the point when the bombardment has finished, then go back into the tower and back out, the bombardment will continue endlessly.
-  After returning from Japhet's Folly to complete the quest, the location icon will not appear on the map. You can visit the island as shown on the map, but all of Japhet's Folly will be gone.

## Maps

- 

  Japhet's Folly Towers

.jpg)

Jarl's Longhouse in Falkreath

**Jarl's Longhouse** is the seat of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath")'s government and home to its [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl"). It is in the center of Falkreath, opposite [Grave Concoctions](/wiki/Skyrim:Grave_Concoctions "Skyrim:Grave Concoctions") to the east and opposite [Falkreath Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Barracks "Skyrim:Falkreath Barracks") to the north.

.jpg)

The main hall of the Jarl's Longhouse

## Related Quests

- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader (Jarl)")**: Slay a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") leader for [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir"), the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Rare Gifts](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts")**: Do a favor by finding a rare item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Thane of Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Falkreath "Skyrim:Thane of Falkreath")**: Prove you are worthy of the title [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") by assisting the people of [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

There is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") to the right of the entrance and a [guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Guard "Skyrim:Falkreath Guard") stood to the right of the door, on duty.

| Plants | Mushrooms | Animals |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 3 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")  2 [Thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") | 1 [Fly Amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") | 1 [Goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") |

### Jarl's Longhouse (Falkreath)

Entry is made directly into the main room where the Jarl holds court. There is a long fire pit in the center of the room. Against the northwest and southeast walls are flights of stairs leading up to balconies and small bedrooms on the upper floor. Under the stairs there is a door leading to the Jarl's bedroom, to the southeast and a doorway to the northwest to the military advisor's room. The Jarl's throne is at the far end of the room on a raised platform.

The Jarl's bedroom consists of a king sized bed on a raised platform in the center of the room. Against the northeast wall is a long [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot, two tall and a small wardrobe all containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and footwear. There are a couple of [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") and a [jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug") on the small wardrobe. Against the southeast wall are two locked display cases, the one on the left is expert-locked and contains a copy of the rare book *[The Night Mother's Truth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Night_Mother%27s_Truth "Skyrim:The Night Mother's Truth")*, a copy of *[Ghosts in the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_in_the_Storm "Skyrim:Ghosts in the Storm")*, and copy of the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Guide to Better Thieving](/wiki/Skyrim:Guide_to_Better_Thieving "Skyrim:Guide to Better Thieving")*, while the one on the right is adept-locked and contains an amulet (see [notes](#Notes)), and a [gold necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Necklace "Skyrim:Gold Necklace"). In the southern corner are several sacks and a barrel containing [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") and a barrel containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). To the right of these, along the southwest wall are three more wardrobes containing fine clothes. In the western corner is a round wooden table and two chairs holding two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and seven loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). Finally along the northwest wall is a wooden bench.

In the military advisor's room, the center of the room is taken over by a long wooden table with a large map of Skyrim showing the current state of the civil war. The military advisor spends all his waking hours poring over the map. On the southeast wall is a row of six weapon racks holding a variety of [iron weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons"), while in the southern corner there are a food barrel with a [potion of plentiful stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Stamina") and a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") on top. To the right, along the southwest wall are several straw bales with two practice dummies in front. In the western corner and continuing along the northwest wall there are more barrels. Along the northeast wall is a long wooden table, an unlocked chest containing minor loot and an owned cot, used by the advisor. On the table are four [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") healing of differing strengths, a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") and a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Death Blow of Abernanit](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Blow_of_Abernanit "Skyrim:Death Blow of Abernanit")*. Above the cot is a wall shelf holding a couple of loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat") and seven bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead").

At the top of the stairs to the southeast is a balcony consisting of a round wooden table and two chairs against the southwest wall and a wooden bench opposite. The door to [Nenya](/wiki/Skyrim:Nenya "Skyrim:Nenya")'s bedroom is to the southwest. There is a long unlocked chest on the left as you enter, with a dresser to the northeast. On the dresser are two [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), a boiled creme treat and a couple of pieces of cheese. In the southern corner is an owned single bed, with a set of shelves next to it in the western corner holding three [green](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") and two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), three bottles of Nord mead, two bottles of alto wine and a [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") with a leveled lock. There are several sacks of food either side of these shelves.

Opposite, to the northwest is another balcony, which consists of an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") built-in to a round wooden table in the northern corner and against the northeast wall is another round wooden table holding a bottle of alto wine, one of wine, two carrots and an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"). The door to the northwest leads to [Helvard](/wiki/Skyrim:Helvard "Skyrim:Helvard")'s bedroom. It consists of an owned single bed in the western corner with a small wardrobe holding a copy of *[The Wispmother](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wispmother "Skyrim:The Wispmother")* and a [steel war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Steel War Axe") to the left. To the left when entering, on the southeast wall are two wall shelves holding four bottles of Nord mead, a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), an empty [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"), an empty [common soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem") and a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* which will initiate the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)") when read for the first time. Along the northwest wall is a long unlocked chest containing minor loot, with a food barrel in the corner to the right. Against the northeast wall is a dresser with a large coin purse and six loose septims. On the other side of the door is a set of shelves holding four bottles of wine, two bottles of alto wine two pieces of cheese and two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato").

## Notes

- The [Ancient Nord Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Amulet "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Amulet") found in an adept-locked display case in the Jarl's bedchambers, is the only of its kind in the game.

## Bugs

- If you receive the *Letter from the Jarl of Falkreath*[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") before becoming Thane, Siddgeir may automatically treat you as friendly, and allow you to take low value things from the longhouse without it being considered theft. **?**
- Speaking to the Jarl of Falkreath and then reading the courier's letter will cause the "Speak to the Jarl of Falkreath" objective to become permanently stuck in your journal.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- Opening the display cases in the Jarl's quarters can cause them to clip through the wall decorations hanging over them.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Winterhold)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

.jpg)

The Jarl's Longhouse in Winterhold

The **Jarl's Longhouse** is a large two-story house in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), and the court of the city's [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir").

It is opposite [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth"), and the first house on the left when entering Winterhold from the main road. It is also where the military advisor for the [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") resides.

## Residents

| [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") Court | Position | [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") Court |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") | [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") | [Kraldar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kraldar "Skyrim:Kraldar") |
| [Malur Seloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Malur_Seloth "Skyrim:Malur Seloth") | [Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward") | Malur Seloth |
| [Thaena](/wiki/Skyrim:Thaena "Skyrim:Thaena") | [Housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl") | [Thonjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonjolf "Skyrim:Thonjolf") |
| [Kai Wet-Pommel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kai_Wet-Pommel "Skyrim:Kai Wet-Pommel") | Military Advisor | [Legate Sevan Telendas](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Sevan_Telendas "Skyrim:Legate Sevan Telendas") |
| [Assur](/wiki/Skyrim:Assur "Skyrim:Assur") | Korir and Thaena's son |  |

## Related Quests

([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Thane of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Thane of Winterhold")**: Gain the title of [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Jarl's Longhouse (Winterhold)

.jpg)

The Jarl of Winterhold's Longhouse

There are a couple of [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes outside, with two [chickens](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") scratching in the dirt and a chicken coop around the back of the building containing a single [chickens' nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"). The entrance leads directly into the main room where the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") holds court. There are two round firepits down the middle of the room. The Jarl's throne is at the far end on a raised section. When the Jarl is sitting there, his [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl") stands beside him. There are two round wooden tables and chairs against the side walls both holding a selection of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"). This is where you will often find [Malur Seloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Malur_Seloth "Skyrim:Malur Seloth"). By either side of the throne are low tables with several goblets and [jugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug") on top. There are barrels and sacks throughout the building mostly containing [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), but some containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients").

There are two flights of stairs, one against the south wall and the other against the north wall leading up to two balconies and bedrooms. Under the south stairs is a doorway into the room used by the military advisor and containing a row of six weapon racks against the north wall, holding a selection of [iron weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") and a barrel to the right of them with two [potions of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and a [potion of plentiful stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Stamina") on top. Against the west wall are several bales of straw with practice dummies set up in front. Against the south wall is an owned cot used by the advisor with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") to the right and a wall shelf above the chest. On the shelf are four potions of minor healing, two [potions of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") and two [potions of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina"). On a raised section in front of the east wall is a long wooden table with a map of the whole of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") showing the progress if any of the civil war.

_02.jpg)

The Military Advisor's Room

Under the stairs to the north is a door that opens into the Jarl's bedroom which contains a king-sized bed in the center of the room on a raised section. On your left, in the southwest corner are a couple of barrels with a basket on top of one of them containing a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Twin Secrets](/wiki/Skyrim:Twin_Secrets "Skyrim:Twin Secrets")*. Further to the right is a large round wooden table with a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, two goblets and a jug on top. Against the north wall are a row of four wardrobes, the outer ones taller than the middle two, all containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"). On the smaller ones is a [Grand Staff of Repulsion](/wiki/Skyrim:Grand_Staff_of_Repulsion "Skyrim:Grand Staff of Repulsion") and a copy of *[Feyfolken III](/wiki/Skyrim:Feyfolken_III "Skyrim:Feyfolken III")* with two wall shelves above holding three [petty](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"), a [lesser](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem") and a [common](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem") [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), all of which are filled. Against the east wall is an unlocked long chest.

The balcony to the south has two round wooden tables and chairs one has a bottle of alto wine and two bottles of Nord mead on top, with a further three bottles of Nord mead on a barrel beside and the other has three more bottles of Nord mead on top. The door to the bedroom is in the middle of the south wall and contains a single owned bed in the southeast corner with a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and five loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on a barrel beside it. Two tall wardrobes containing fine clothes flank the door on the north wall and on the west wall is a set of shelves that hold two bottles of alto wine, four bottles of wine, a bottle of Nord mead, two [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and a medium coin purse, with a chair in the southwest corner.

The balcony to the north has a couple of bales of straw with a round wooden table and chair with a bottle of each alto wine, wine and Nord mead on the table, with a door into [Assur's](/wiki/Skyrim:Assur "Skyrim:Assur") small bedroom. His bedroom contains an owned single bed in the northeastern corner, two wall shelves against the south wall, one either side of the door, holding an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a potion of minor healing, a potion of minor magicka and several [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"). Against the west wall is an unlocked long chest, with a chair to the right of it. Finally against the north wall is a small wardrobe with a lockpick and five loose septims on top and containing fine clothes.

## Notes

- Despite not being in a closed city, the music that plays inside this Jarl's palace is the same that plays in ones within walled cities, such as [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") and the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace").

## Bugs

- Thaena can be found occupying Korir's throne, due to it being owned by the `WinterholdJarlFaction`, of which Korir isn't a part, while Thaena is.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, addresses this issue. The faction error has been corrected.
- Oddly, since the longhouse is marked as being owned by the Winterhold crime faction, if you help anyone in the hold (including [Kjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjar "Skyrim:Kjar") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and ironically enough, anyone from the [College](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)")), you will be able to take things from the longhouse without it being considered theft.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19319)) A new faction was created specifically for the residents of the longhouse in order to set ownership correctly.

# Skyrim:Jerall Mountains

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Landmark: Jerall Mountains ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Jerall+Mountains)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Jerall_Mountains "Lore:Jerall Mountains")) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Regions | |
| [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"), [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| Southern border of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") | |

The Jerall Mountains in the far south of Falkreath Hold

The **Jerall Mountains** are a mountain range that stretches along the southern border of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim").

The mountains form the southern border of [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") and [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"). Its harsh, cold climate has made the mountains nearly inhospitable, with few inhabitants living there and no major settlements throughout history. Some points of interest include the town of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), [Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad"), [Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne"), the dragon shrines of [Ancient's Ascent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient%27s_Ascent "Skyrim:Ancient's Ascent") and [Lost Tongue Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Tongue_Overlook "Skyrim:Lost Tongue Overlook"), the Dwemer ruins of [Rkund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Rkund "Skyrim:Ruins of Rkund"), and the large [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") of [Arcwind Point](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcwind_Point "Skyrim:Arcwind Point").

The [Goblins](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblins "Skyrim:Goblins") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") adds a subterranean mountain passage known as [Gromm's Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Gromm%27s_Pass "Skyrim:Gromm's Pass"), although access to [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil") was recently cut off by a tunnel collapse.

[The Cause](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause") adds an underground [Ayleid](/wiki/Lore:Ayleid "Lore:Ayleid") ruin beneath the mountains known as [Rielle](/wiki/Skyrim:Rielle "Skyrim:Rielle"). It extends into Cyrodiil, but its southern tunnels have been blocked by rubble.

# Skyrim:Joining the Legion

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Imperial Legion.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Imperial_Legion.png) | **Prove yourself worthy to join the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | CW00A: anyone who can be asked about the Imperial Legion CW01A: [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") |

Castle Dour, the base of the Imperial Legion

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Go to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").
2. Speak to [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius").
3. Speak to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke").
4. Clear out bandits from [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad").
5. Return to Legate Rikke.
6. Take the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") oath.

### Imperial Introductions

*"I'm telling you, Ulfric's planning an attack on Whiterun."*

Anytime after escaping [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") during [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound"), anyone you meet with ties with the Imperial Legion (like [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar")) will encourage you to travel to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") to enlist. This will start the miscellaneous quest [Imperial Introductions](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Introductions "Skyrim:Imperial Introductions"). In particular, some of them will specify to talk to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") at [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour"). When you enter, you will witness her trying to convince an ill-informed [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") that [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") will follow their traditions, even in a time when loyalty is tested. Apparently, rebel leader [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") is preparing to attack [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") so the two strategists have their hands full. After the scene, if you try to speak to Legate Rikke, General Tullius will approach you. He will recall you from Helgen and, by any of your dialogue options, point you towards Legate Rikke for putting someone as resourceful as you to good use.

Rikke will commend you for surviving the destruction of Helgen and tell you that she has arranged a small test of your skills before you're allowed to join the Legion. When asked which test she will explain: *"The kind that evaluates your usefulness during... duress. I'm sending you to clear out Fort Hraagstad. If you survive, you'll pass. If you die, then I'll have no further use for your corpse."*. She will then explain that the Legion will set up a garrison at [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad") but that the place has been overrun with [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and needs to be cleared. She will not take no for an answer and will just angrily say: *"What's the matter, soldier? I gave you an order. I want that fort, and I want it now. Move it!"*. This will complete the miscellaneous quest Imperial Introductions and start Joining the Legion. If you have already visited Fort Hraggstad and cleared it, she will be quite surprised: *"Is that so? I was right about you."*. This will complete Imperial Introductions and start Joining the Legion with the [first stages](#The_Oath) completed.

#### Prove Your Usefulness

The fort is located near the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy"), west of Solitude in the snowy terrain past [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave"). Once there, a number of bandits will attack you on sight. The fort has archers, atop towers, so approach with caution. Once the exterior area is clear, locate the entrance to the fort and enter. It consists of two interior zones: the main zone and the prison, both of them accessible from separate entrances in the courtyard. In the prison, two bandits await you in the first room, with another guarding the area downstairs. In the main zone, two bandits and their chief will ambush you upon entering. You can find a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books"), *[The Gold Ribbon of Merit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gold_Ribbon_of_Merit "Skyrim:The Gold Ribbon of Merit")* upstairs. When all is said and done return to Legate Rikke in Solitude.

#### The Oath

*"Long live the Emperor! Long live the Empire!"*

Upon your next enter in the castle, Legate Rikke and Tullius will once again be debating, this time about the [Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown"). Tullius will once again show a lack of respect for Nordic tradition. After the scene, Rikke will approach you and will be pleased to see your success, complimenting you on a job well done: *"Welcome back, soldier. I'm glad you made it in one piece. I'll send men to garrison the fort right away. You did well. I'm impressed. But before we go any further, it's time for you to officially join the Legion."*. General Tullius will then approach you to take the oath binding you to the service of the emperor and the Legion. Repeat the oath after him:

:   *"Upon my honor I do swear undying loyalty to the Emperor, Titus Mede II..."*
:   *"...and unwavering obedience to the officers of his great Empire."*
:   *"May those above judge me, and those below take me, if I fail in my duty."*
:   *"Long live the Emperor! Long live the Empire!"*

Tullius will then welcome you to the Legion and send you to the castle's blacksmith, [Beirand](/wiki/Skyrim:Beirand "Skyrim:Beirand"), starting the miscellaneous quest [Get Outfitted](/wiki/Skyrim:Get_Outfitted "Skyrim:Get Outfitted"), who will provide you with a set of [Imperial armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Armor"). You may choose heavy, medium, or light Imperial armor. Once Tullius has sent you towards Beirand the quest ends and the next one starts, your first assignment for the Empire as an [Auxiliary](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion#Ranks "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") of the Imperial Legion, [The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Imperial)").

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked when you complete this quest:

-  **Taking Sides** (10 points/Bronze) — Join the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") or the [Imperial Army](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion")

## Notes

- Joining the Legion and [Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks") are mutually exclusive quests: completing one automatically fails the other (if it was started or the prerequisite miscellaneous quest was started).
- You can still join the Imperial Legion after completing the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"). The oath you take upon joining omits "Titus Mede II", but he'll still say "Long Live the Emperor!"
- Even though Legate Rikke says she will send troops to garrison the fort straight away if you return to Fort Hraggstad before speaking to her Imperial soldiers will already be present. Because you have not taken the Imperial oath yet you will be trespassing if you enter the buildings and you will get attacked if you do not leave.
- If you clear [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad") before starting this quest, [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") will have different dialogue, surprised by your go-ahead. Nevertheless it won't affect the course of the quest.
- After completion of this quest, random spawned groups of [Stormcloak Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier") may attack you and you will no longer be welcome in Stormcloak [camps](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks#Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") or [forts](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts#Civil_War_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts").

## Bugs

- If [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad") is not the first [Civil War Fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts#Civil_War_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") you clear, after clearing it of [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), even during this quest, soldiers will never garrison and enemies respawn instead. This is due to a hidden quest not ending after clearing the first Civil War Fort. See this [talk](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim talk:Fort Hraggstad") section for info.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
  - The console command `resetquest CWFortObserver` can be used to reset the hidden quest, then clear the fort again. Repeat this for every Civil War Fort you want to be garrisoned.
- You may encounter a bug/message "No Active Quest" or when you get closer to the fort the quest arrow may just disappear. Go ahead and clear out all the bandits around and in the prison first. Then, head to the main zone. The quest arrow will then reappear and point to the chief bandit. You can then properly clear out the fort and complete the quest.
- One or more bandits may be in a completely different part of Skyrim.

## Quest Stages

| Imperial Introductions (CW00A) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 1 |  | *(Heard from anyone Imperial Legion relatad)* *Objective 1:* Join the Imperial Legion |
| 7 |  | *(Spoken to Legate Rikke, approached by General Tullius)* *Objective 1:* Join the Imperial Legion |
| 10 |  | *(Spoken directly to General Tullius)* *Objective 1:* Join the Imperial Legion |
| Joining the Legion (CW01A) | | |
| 1 |  | In order to prove myself to Legate Rikke, I am to clear out the bandits living at Fort Hraggstad. *Objective 1:* Clear out Fort Hraggstad |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Report to Legate Rikke |
| 160 |  | *Objective 160:* Take the oath |
| 200 | ☑ |  |
| 999 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table:
  - CW00A: 0, 2, 5.
  - CW01A: 0, 150.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CW00A
  CW01A stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CW00A
  CW01A`.
