# Skyrim:Joining the Legion

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Imperial Legion.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Imperial_Legion.png) | **Prove yourself worthy to join the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | CW00A: anyone who can be asked about the Imperial Legion CW01A: [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") |
| Location(s): | [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad"), [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") |
| Reward: | Induction into the Imperial Legion, [Auxiliary](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion#Ranks "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") rank |
| ID: | CW00A CW01A |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** *[Imperial Introductions](#Imperial_Introductions)* | **Next →** [The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Imperial)"), [Get Outfitted](/wiki/Skyrim:Get_Outfitted "Skyrim:Get Outfitted") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | *[Imperial Introductions](#Imperial_Introductions)* | | → Next | [The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Imperial)"), [Get Outfitted](/wiki/Skyrim:Get_Outfitted "Skyrim:Get Outfitted") | | |

Castle Dour, the base of the Imperial Legion

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Go to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").
2. Speak to [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius").
3. Speak to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke").
4. Clear out bandits from [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad").
5. Return to Legate Rikke.
6. Take the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") oath.

### Imperial Introductions

*"I'm telling you, Ulfric's planning an attack on Whiterun."*

Anytime after escaping [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") during [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound"), anyone you meet with ties with the Imperial Legion (like [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar")) will encourage you to travel to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") to enlist. This will start the miscellaneous quest [Imperial Introductions](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Introductions "Skyrim:Imperial Introductions"). In particular, some of them will specify to talk to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") at [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour"). When you enter, you will witness her trying to convince an ill-informed [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") that [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") will follow their traditions, even in a time when loyalty is tested. Apparently, rebel leader [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") is preparing to attack [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") so the two strategists have their hands full. After the scene, if you try to speak to Legate Rikke, General Tullius will approach you. He will recall you from Helgen and, by any of your dialogue options, point you towards Legate Rikke for putting someone as resourceful as you to good use.

Rikke will commend you for surviving the destruction of Helgen and tell you that she has arranged a small test of your skills before you're allowed to join the Legion. When asked which test she will explain: *"The kind that evaluates your usefulness during... duress. I'm sending you to clear out Fort Hraagstad. If you survive, you'll pass. If you die, then I'll have no further use for your corpse."*. She will then explain that the Legion will set up a garrison at [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad") but that the place has been overrun with [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and needs to be cleared. She will not take no for an answer and will just angrily say: *"What's the matter, soldier? I gave you an order. I want that fort, and I want it now. Move it!"*. This will complete the miscellaneous quest Imperial Introductions and start Joining the Legion. If you have already visited Fort Hraggstad and cleared it, she will be quite surprised: *"Is that so? I was right about you."*. This will complete Imperial Introductions and start Joining the Legion with the [first stages](#The_Oath) completed.

#### Prove Your Usefulness

The fort is located near the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy"), west of Solitude in the snowy terrain past [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave"). Once there, a number of bandits will attack you on sight. The fort has archers, atop towers, so approach with caution. Once the exterior area is clear, locate the entrance to the fort and enter. It consists of two interior zones: the main zone and the prison, both of them accessible from separate entrances in the courtyard. In the prison, two bandits await you in the first room, with another guarding the area downstairs. In the main zone, two bandits and their chief will ambush you upon entering. You can find a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books"), *[The Gold Ribbon of Merit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gold_Ribbon_of_Merit "Skyrim:The Gold Ribbon of Merit")* upstairs. When all is said and done return to Legate Rikke in Solitude.

#### The Oath

*"Long live the Emperor! Long live the Empire!"*

Upon your next enter in the castle, Legate Rikke and Tullius will once again be debating, this time about the [Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown"). Tullius will once again show a lack of respect for Nordic tradition. After the scene, Rikke will approach you and will be pleased to see your success, complimenting you on a job well done: *"Welcome back, soldier. I'm glad you made it in one piece. I'll send men to garrison the fort right away. You did well. I'm impressed. But before we go any further, it's time for you to officially join the Legion."*. General Tullius will then approach you to take the oath binding you to the service of the emperor and the Legion. Repeat the oath after him:

:   *"Upon my honor I do swear undying loyalty to the Emperor, Titus Mede II..."*
:   *"...and unwavering obedience to the officers of his great Empire."*
:   *"May those above judge me, and those below take me, if I fail in my duty."*
:   *"Long live the Emperor! Long live the Empire!"*

Tullius will then welcome you to the Legion and send you to the castle's blacksmith, [Beirand](/wiki/Skyrim:Beirand "Skyrim:Beirand"), starting the miscellaneous quest [Get Outfitted](/wiki/Skyrim:Get_Outfitted "Skyrim:Get Outfitted"), who will provide you with a set of [Imperial armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Armor"). You may choose heavy, medium, or light Imperial armor. Once Tullius has sent you towards Beirand the quest ends and the next one starts, your first assignment for the Empire as an [Auxiliary](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion#Ranks "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") of the Imperial Legion, [The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Imperial)").

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked when you complete this quest:

-  **Taking Sides** (10 points/Bronze) — Join the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") or the [Imperial Army](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion")

## Notes

- Joining the Legion and [Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks") are mutually exclusive quests: completing one automatically fails the other (if it was started or the prerequisite miscellaneous quest was started).
- You can still join the Imperial Legion after completing the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"). The oath you take upon joining omits "Titus Mede II", but he'll still say "Long Live the Emperor!"
- Even though Legate Rikke says she will send troops to garrison the fort straight away if you return to Fort Hraggstad before speaking to her Imperial soldiers will already be present. Because you have not taken the Imperial oath yet you will be trespassing if you enter the buildings and you will get attacked if you do not leave.
- If you clear [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad") before starting this quest, [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") will have different dialogue, surprised by your go-ahead. Nevertheless it won't affect the course of the quest.
- After completion of this quest, random spawned groups of [Stormcloak Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier") may attack you and you will no longer be welcome in Stormcloak [camps](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks#Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") or [forts](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts#Civil_War_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts").

## Bugs

- If [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad") is not the first [Civil War Fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts#Civil_War_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") you clear, after clearing it of [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), even during this quest, soldiers will never garrison and enemies respawn instead. This is due to a hidden quest not ending after clearing the first Civil War Fort. See this [talk](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim talk:Fort Hraggstad") section for info.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
  - The console command `resetquest CWFortObserver` can be used to reset the hidden quest, then clear the fort again. Repeat this for every Civil War Fort you want to be garrisoned.
- You may encounter a bug/message "No Active Quest" or when you get closer to the fort the quest arrow may just disappear. Go ahead and clear out all the bandits around and in the prison first. Then, head to the main zone. The quest arrow will then reappear and point to the chief bandit. You can then properly clear out the fort and complete the quest.
- One or more bandits may be in a completely different part of Skyrim.

# Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Eddie the head](/wiki/User:Eddie_the_head "User:Eddie the head"), checked by [Sheeprin](/wiki/User:Sheeprin "User:Sheeprin")  **Reward**: written by [Sheeprin](/wiki/User:Sheeprin "User:Sheeprin"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Stormcloaks.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Stormcloaks.png) | **Prove yourself worthy of being a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebel.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") in Windhelm |
| Location(s): | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), [Serpentstone Isle](/wiki/Skyrim:Serpentstone_Isle "Skyrim:Serpentstone Isle") |
| Reward: | Stormcloak membership, Fur Boots, Fur Gauntlets, Hide Helmet, Stormcloak Cuirass; title of "Unblooded" |
| ID: | CW01B |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | |  | **Next →** [The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Stormcloaks)") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | [The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Stormcloaks)") | | |

Test your mettle, kill an Ice Wraith!

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Head to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and speak with [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak").
2. Speak with [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist").
3. Travel to [Serpentstone Isle](/wiki/Skyrim:Serpentstone_Isle "Skyrim:Serpentstone Isle").
4. Kill the [Ice Wraith](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith").
5. Take the oath.

### Joining

Proceed to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and enter the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings"). If this is your first time in the palace, then Jarl [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") and his lieutenant, [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist"), will have a long conversation concerning the war. Speak with Ulfric, who recognizes you from [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") and will direct you to speak with his lieutenant. Galmar will ask you why you want to join, then tell you that to prove yourself worthy of joining the Stormcloaks, you must travel to the [Serpentstone Isle](/wiki/Skyrim:Serpentstone_Isle "Skyrim:Serpentstone Isle") and defeat an [Ice Wraith](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith#Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith"). If you are below level 20, he will also give you an [Elixir of Resist Cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Elixir_of_Resist_Cold "Skyrim:Elixir of Resist Cold") and three [Ice Wraith Banes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Bane "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Bane"), both of which can be incredibly helpful on this quest if you are at a low level.

### Test Your Mettle

Serpentstone Isle will be your proving grounds

Travel to the Serpentstone Isle, located far north of Windhelm. Once you're there, kill the Ice Wraith. Using a fire spell or adding the Ice Wraith Bane to your weapon will make the fight easier. Remember to use the resist frost potion before you engage if you need it. You can also find the Serpent Stone while there.

### The Victorious Return

Travel back to the Palace of Kings to speak with Galmar. When you return, Galmar and Ulfric will be discussing your next mission for the Stormcloaks. Galmar will express his surprise at seeing you return and ask you to take the Stormcloak oath:

:   *"I do swear my blood and honor to the service of Ulfric Stormcloak..."*
:   *"...Jarl of Windhelm and true High King of Skyrim."*
:   *"As Talos is my witness, may this oath bind me to death and beyond..."*
:   *"...even to my lord as to my fellow brothers and sisters in arms."*
:   *"All hail the Stormcloaks, the true sons and daughters of Skyrim!"*

Repeat the oath as Galmar says it and he will reward you with Fur Boots, a Stormcloak Cuirass, Fur Gauntlets and a Hide Helmet.

### Reward

Upon completion of the quest and repeating the oath you will be awarded the following:

- Hide Helmet
- Fur Gauntlets
- Stormcloak Cuirass
- Fur Boots

"You're a Stormcloak now, you ought to look the part. "--Galmar Stone-Fist

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked at the end of this quest:

-  **Taking Sides** (10 points/Bronze) — Join the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") or the [Imperial Army](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion")

## Notes

- [Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion") and Joining the Stormcloaks are mutually exclusive quests: completing one automatically fails the other (if it was started or the prerequisite miscellaneous quest was started).
-  The German version of the quest name is "So jung und schon bei den Sturmmänteln?", which is a take-off of the German translation of Princess Leia's famous Star Wars quote to Luke, "Aren't you a little short for a Stormtrooper?" The word "Sturmmänteln" (Stormcloak) is substituted for the original "Sturmtruppen", however.

## Bugs

- [Galmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") would not complete Joining the Stormcloaks properly if [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") was an active quest.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- Galmar refers to all players as "brother", including females, when telling them to get kitted out after joining the Stormcloaks.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Joining the Stormcloaks (CW01B) | | |

| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Return to Galmar |
| 160 |  | *Objective 160:* Take the oath |
| 200 | ☑ |  |
| 999 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 150.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CW01B stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CW01B`.

# Skyrim:Jorgen and Lami's House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Jorgen and Lami's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Jorgen+and+Lami%27s+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| MorthalJorgenandLamisHouse | |
| Region | |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | |
| Location | |
| [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Jorgen and Lami's House

**Jorgen and Lami's House** is an unassuming, one-room cottage where [Jorgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorgen "Skyrim:Jorgen") and [Lami](/wiki/Skyrim:Lami "Skyrim:Lami") live. It lies in the outskirts of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") across from the lumber mill.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Jorgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorgen "Skyrim:Jorgen")  [Lami](/wiki/Skyrim:Lami "Skyrim:Lami") [Apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Apothecary") [Trainer (Common)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Common)")[Alchemy (Common)](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Alchemy (Common)")\* |

\* This person lives here but works at the [Thaumaturgist's Hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Thaumaturgist%27s_Hut "Skyrim:Thaumaturgist's Hut").

## Related Quests

- **[Pieces of the Past](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past")**: Retrieve the scattered pieces of [Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Mehrunes' Razor") and reforge this deadly blade.

### Exterior

The sawmill that supports Jorgen and Lami's lives

Their house is separated from the rest of the town of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") as their house is across a bridge from the rest of the buildings. There are a few steps leading up to the porch at the front of the house, the door is normally novice-locked. Opposite the house is the saw mill with two [wood chopping blocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"), a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") beside it. There are two [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") plants near where the sawn logs stack once cut and a [swamp fungal pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod") slightly uphill to the north.

### Jorgen and Lami's House

Inside the house

They live rather simply in a one room home. To the left as you enter is a set of shelves holding two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulb and three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). Above these shelves are two garlic braids, three [elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") all hanging from the ceiling. To the left of the shelves is a basket containing two leeks and to the right of the shelves is a barrel of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), with a bucket on top hiding a copy of the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Morning Star, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Morning_Star,_v1 "Skyrim:2920, Morning Star, v1")*. Behind the barrel is a unique item, a bottle of [Jessica's Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Jessica%27s_Wine "Skyrim:Jessica's Wine"). Classed as a [beverage](/wiki/Skyrim:Beverages "Skyrim:Beverages"), it restores five points of [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina").

In the middle of the south wall is a queen sized bed, at the end of the bed is an adept-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), which is identified as Jorgen's chest. To the right of the bed is a wooden table holding a copy of *[Songs of the Return, Vol 56](/wiki/Skyrim:Songs_of_the_Return,_Vol_56 "Skyrim:Songs of the Return, Vol 56")* and two bottles of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"). Next to this, against the west wall is a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). In the middle of the west wall is a fireplace, with a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") on the mantlepiece, a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front of the fire and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes "Skyrim:Shoes") in front of the hearth. Hanging from the ceiling to the left of the fireplace is a rack holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)").

In the northwestern corner, still against the west wall is a long wooden table and bench. On the table are two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and two [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"). Under the table is a [potion of vigor](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigor "Skyrim:Potion of Vigor"). In the northeastern corner is a square wooden table with two chairs, holding a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [potion of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina"), a [taproot](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot"), a [creep cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster"), a [torchbug thorax](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug_Thorax "Skyrim:Torchbug Thorax"), a bowl of [spriggan sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan_Sap "Skyrim:Spriggan Sap"), a bowl of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), a sprig of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a [spider egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg"). To the left in the middle of the north wall is a food barrel.

## Notes

- If you have started the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past") to retrieve the parts of [Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Mehrunes' Razor"), speaking to Jorgen can result in him giving you his [house key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Jorgen_and_Lami%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Jorgen and Lami's House") and [chest key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Jorgen%27s_Chest "Skyrim:Key to Jorgen's Chest"). The [hilt of the razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hilt_of_Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Hilt of Mehrunes' Razor") can be found in Jorgen's chest.

Jorrvaskr

**Jorrvaskr** is the mead hall headquarters of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions"). It is up the stairs from the central plaza in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). It was founded around the [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge") before Whiterun even existed. The city itself built up around it.

The entire building is an overturned longship. According to the book *[Songs of the Return, Vol 7](/wiki/Skyrim:Songs_of_the_Return,_Vol_7 "Skyrim:Songs of the Return, Vol 7")*, Jorrvaskr was the name of one of the ships that sailed from [Atmora](/wiki/Lore:Atmora "Lore:Atmora") under the command of [Ysgramor](/wiki/Lore:Ysgramor "Lore:Ysgramor"). The crew carried the ship across land and made it their shelter when its captain, Jeek of the River, founded the [Great City](/wiki/Lore:Whiterun "Lore:Whiterun").

It contains two zones: *[Jorrvaskr](#Jorrvaskr)* and *[Jorrvaskr Living Quarters](#Jorrvaskr_Living_Quarters)*.

## Residents

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

### Companions Quests

- **[Take Up Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_Up_Arms "Skyrim:Take Up Arms")**: Prove you are worthy to join the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").
  - **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(A) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (A)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to kill an invading beast.
  - **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den.
  - **[Escaped Criminal](/wiki/Skyrim:Escaped_Criminal "Skyrim:Escaped Criminal")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to hunt down an escaped [criminal](/wiki/Skyrim:Criminal "Skyrim:Criminal").
  - **[Family Heirloom](/wiki/Skyrim:Family_Heirloom "Skyrim:Family Heirloom")**: Fulfill a contract for the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to retrieve a stolen family heirloom.
  - **[Hired Muscle](/wiki/Skyrim:Hired_Muscle "Skyrim:Hired Muscle")**: Fulfill a contract for the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to bring a citizen back in line.
  - **[Rescue Mission](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_Mission "Skyrim:Rescue Mission")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to rescue a kidnapped citizen.
  - **[Trouble in Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Trouble_in_Skyrim "Skyrim:Trouble in Skyrim")**: Fulfill a contract for the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a troublesome area.
- **[Proving Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proving_Honor "Skyrim:Proving Honor")**: Claim a [Fragment of Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragment_of_Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Fragment of Wuuthrad") from [Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn").
- **[The Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand")**: Join the ranks of [the Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Circle "Skyrim:The Circle") and clear [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock") of werewolf hunters.
  - **[Retrieval](/wiki/Skyrim:Retrieval "Skyrim:Retrieval")**: Journey to a random location to retrieve a fragment of [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad").
  - **[Stealing Plans](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealing_Plans "Skyrim:Stealing Plans")**: Search a Silver Hand hideout for information on the location of their headquarters.
  - **[Striking the Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Striking_the_Heart "Skyrim:Striking the Heart")**: Assassinate a leader of the Silver Hand.
- **[Blood's Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood%27s_Honor "Skyrim:Blood's Honor")**: Claim the head of a [Glenmoril Witch](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch") for [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane").
- **[Purity of Revenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity_of_Revenge "Skyrim:Purity of Revenge")**: Retrieve the Fragments of Wuuthrad and wipe out the [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand").
- **[Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead")**: Cure [Kodlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane")'s spirit and become Harbinger of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").
  - **[Dragon Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Seekers "Skyrim:Dragon Seekers")**: Go to a [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") with [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") or [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") and kill the dragon. *(Requires [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") quest completion)*
  - **[Purity](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity "Skyrim:Purity")**: Help a member of the Circle give up their beasthood. *(2 available)*
  - **[Totems of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Totems_of_Hircine "Skyrim:Totems of Hircine")**: Journey to the given location to find a Totem of Hircine. *(3 available) (Requires [lycanthropy](/wiki/Skyrim:Lycanthropy "Skyrim:Lycanthropy"))*

### Other Quests

- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.

### Exterior

The east side is the courtyard where the Companions meet for missions and training sessions. There are chairs and combat dummies. All the items here are free to take after completing [Take Up Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_Up_Arms "Skyrim:Take Up Arms").

The north side has a stone door that serves as an entrance to the [Underforge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Underforge "Skyrim:The Underforge"), and stairs leading up to the [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge").

The west side is the main stairs linking the building to the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen").

### Jorrvaskr

Jorrvaskr interior

The main hall is where the Companions meet for meals and relaxing between training and missions. It consists of one large 'horseshoe' shaped table around a fire; there are only nine chairs, which is less than the total number of Companions. On both the east and west sides of the hall, there are two sets of double doors, above which can be seen four shields. The table has several food items scattered throughout.

On the south side of the hall is the main weapon display area. The fragments of [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad"), several of which are missing, are placed in the middle of the wall, above which are two shields which are inaccessible. On the pillars of the stairs are four weapon plaques, three with greatswords and the other with a warhammer, none of which can be taken. On the side walls are two weapon racks, one on either side, and these weapons can be taken. On an end table facing the fire, is the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Hallgerd's Tale](/wiki/Skyrim:Hallgerd%27s_Tale "Skyrim:Hallgerd's Tale")*. All the items here are free to take after completing [Take Up Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_Up_Arms "Skyrim:Take Up Arms").

On the north side of the hall is a separate bedroom belonging to [Vignar Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Vignar_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Vignar Gray-Mane"), where [Brill](/wiki/Skyrim:Brill "Skyrim:Brill") sleeps as well. There are two unusable beds in here, as well as some high-value potions, two silver ingots, and a mammoth tusk. Nothing in this room is free to take at any time.

### Jorrvaskr Living Quarters

This area is where most Companions sleep, and it mainly consists of beds. To the southwest is where the lower-ranking Companions and [Tilma the Haggard](/wiki/Skyrim:Tilma_the_Haggard "Skyrim:Tilma the Haggard") sleep; there are eight usable beds ([rested](/wiki/Skyrim:Rested "Skyrim:Rested") bonus only).

To the west are [Aela the Huntress](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress") and [Skjor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjor "Skyrim:Skjor")'s bedrooms. Aela's is on the south, and has one unusable bed, an expert-locked display case with a leveled bow, and the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") skill book *[The Marksmanship Lesson](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Marksmanship_Lesson "Skyrim:The Marksmanship Lesson")*. On the bookshelves are four [ice wraith teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth"), and there are some pelts on the table. To the north is Skjor's bedroom, which has one unusable bed and an expert-locked display case with a steel dagger. There is a batch of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts") on the shelves by the bed and three silver ingots on the shelves by the door.

To the east is [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas")' bedroom. Vilkas' bedroom has one unusable bed. There is the rare book *[Lycanthropic Legends of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Lycanthropic_Legends_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Lycanthropic Legends of Skyrim")* and one sample of ice wraith teeth on the shelves by the bed, nine [chaurus eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs") on the end table by the door, and some high-value potions on the stand on the other side of the door. The bar contains one unusable bed used by [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas"), a lute, and unsurprisingly, a large amount of mead.

The items in Aela's bedroom are only free to take through marriage; the items in Vilkas' and Skjor's bedrooms, and around the bar, are never free to take. The items in the hall and the communal bedroom are free to take after completing [Take Up Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_Up_Arms "Skyrim:Take Up Arms").

The Harbinger's quarters consists of a bedroom and a study. The study contains four display cases, three of which are locked by expert locks; the other is atop a set of shelves, and is not locked. The three locked cases display a dagger, a warhammer, and a greatsword (all leveled). The unlocked display case is empty. On the map table is a [giant's toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe") and the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") skill book *[Song Of Hrormir](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_Of_Hrormir "Skyrim:Song Of Hrormir")*; on the end table beside that table is a [daedra heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart"). The bedroom contains one unusable bed and an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"). All ingredients respawn. Everything here, including the bed, becomes free to take after completing [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead").

## Notes

- There is a  "Danger") Danger [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") on the right hand pillar ascending the stairs to the front door. The Companions have a low view of thieves and will not hesitate to kill you if you are caught stealing. They will, however, be lenient if you are a member of the Guild, but you must still pay a fine to them.
- There is at least one safe container inside Jorrvaskr. It's a chest behind the wooden railing on the west side of the hall (to your left when entering from the main front doors).
- Jorrvaskr's doors lock during the [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun") quest. The locks cannot be picked, and any members or quest items inside are inaccessible. The doors unlock sometime before the end of the following quest, [Rescue from Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Neugrad"), or [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") if you have sided with the Imperials.
- When you complete a Companions job and want to enter Jorrvaskr to finish the quest, the map marker will actually point you to the back doors. However, the Shield Sibling who gave you the quest will be standing closer to, and even facing, the front doors, fully expecting you to enter through them instead.
- If you clip through the diagonal wooden walls on the north side of the building and turn around, you can easily make your way to the merchant chest underneath the Skyforge.

## Bugs

- One or more of the Companions inside or behind Jorrvaskr may attack you on sight for no apparent reason. They will not accept your yield, and may not be killable due to being tagged as essential. **?**
  - Commit a minor crime, such as assault, in front of a Whiterun guard, then clear your bounty. This should end their hostility immediately, even if they are in the middle of attacking you.
- In Jorrvaskr Living Quarters, when you first enter the area you see 2 sets of shelves if you Whirlwind Sprint (only tested with tempest level) it takes you off the map and resets you at the door.
- The doors to Jorrvaskr may remain locked after completing Battle for Whiterun.
- The copy of *Hallgerd's Tale* may partially clip through the end table it sits on.
- The chest in the Harbinger's bedroom may respawn even though it's never supposed to.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Journeyman's Nook

## Overview

Journeyman's Nook

**Journeyman's Nook** is a small [outdoor Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") southeast of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit").

## Walkthrough

The Nook is made of two concentric circles, with the living quarters in the innermost section. When you first arrive, a leveled bandit will be residing there. Entering the outer circle of the Nook, you will see windows around the perimeter of the inner wall. The entrance is toward the rear of the shelter on the north side. The Nook itself is cozy, with the exception of a slain college apprentice named [Borvir](/wiki/Skyrim:Borvir "Skyrim:Borvir") on the floor. An [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") is across the room, with a [potion of illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Illusion "Skyrim:Potion of Illusion") and a [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"). Borvir's body is on the floor by the lab, with three [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") by his back and his [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Borvir%27s_Dagger "Skyrim:Borvir's Dagger") just by his hand. Two barrels hold the usual clutter, but the crate on the east wall acting as a table has [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"), a [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Magicka"), a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), and an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"). Next to the satchel is copy of the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Herbalist's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbalist%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:Herbalist's Guide to Skyrim")*. A bedroll is laid out by the fire, and a small table on the south wall, by the entrance, holds a [leg of goat roast](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat_Roast "Skyrim:Leg of Goat Roast") and a medium coin purse. A [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") is tucked away behind the table. Opening it reveals a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), a piece of jewelry, and [Treasure Map II](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_II "Skyrim:Treasure Map II").

## Notes

- A small abandoned camp can be found northwest of Journeyman's Nook, past the leaning pillar. The camp contains two tents. One of the tents is occupied by a dead skeleton, while the other contains an adept-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=125603&y=86720&zoom=17&legacy=true).
- A steep, narrow trail north-northeast of Journeyman's Nook leads down to the sea. At the base of the trail, two [horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker") sit in front of a small alcove in the cliff wall, which contains a novice-locked chest and a copy of the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") skill book *[2920, Rain's Hand, v4](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Rain%27s_Hand,_v4 "Skyrim:2920, Rain's Hand, v4")* [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=135134&y=87629&zoom=17&legacy=true). There is also a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") on the ground in front of said alcove, as well as an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") on your left just before reaching the coast. A second iron ore vein is also nearby on the northwest side of the island, seen just a few yards across the coast.
- Borvir's Dagger respawns, along with the knapsack and apothecary's satchel.

## Bugs

- Borvir's Dagger might clip beneath the floor, making it unreachable without use of the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console").

# Skyrim:Kagrenzel

## Overview

Kagrenzel

**Kagrenzel** is a small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") southeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"). It contains only one zone, *[Kagrenzel](#Kagrenzel)*.

Magical orb

### Exterior

You can reach the ruin by following an unmarked path into the [Velothi Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Velothi_Mountains "Skyrim:Velothi Mountains") east of the tower of [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund"). Be careful as you progress, as you may encounter a leveled [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer") at the tower and some [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") along the path.

There is an unmarked [hunter's camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places#Hunter.2C_Fishermen_and_Other_Camps "Skyrim:Unmarked Places") a short distance south of the path on a ridge, where the path turns to the northeast and just before the start of several flights of stairs leading up to the ruin. It is inhabited by two [hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter"), and contains a campfire with a wooden bench beside it. There are two small tents containing unowned bedrolls, with a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush between the tents and a few barrels of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") around the fire, one of which has a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Father Of The Niben](/wiki/Skyrim:Father_Of_The_Niben "Skyrim:Father Of The Niben")* on top. The skill book is marked as unowned, and is free to take.

There is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") by the top of the first flight of stairs. There are three more flights to climb and two square arches to pass under. At the top, you can see a large Dwemer building. The entrance is on the east side of the building, with three damaged square arches in front. A short distance east is a [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein"), and a short distance northwest is a [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein").

### Kagrenzel

Passage infested with Falmer hives

Through typical large metal doors found in Dwemer ruins, the entrance opens into an empty room with stairs opposite leading to another pair of metal doors. These open into a cavernous room with three pillars in a row opposite. The room is fairly dark, with rubble all around. In the center of the room is a stone pedestal with the bodies of two dead [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") lying on the ground beside it. A bright orb appears above the pedestal accompanied by musical chimes when you get close enough, as defined by a large invisible rectangular area. Moving around the edges of the room will result in you leaving this unmarked rectangle and will turn off the orb. There is a metal circle on the floor surrounding the orb and bodies. It is best to save at this point. Touching the strange orb causes a Dwemer cage to ensnare you as the orb rotates around the outside several times, then falls into the pedestal it was above originally. The floor gives way shortly afterward. As you plummet hundreds of feet below the surface of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), you can guide your fall. If done properly, you will survive by landing in a deep pool of water littered with the bones of a [mammoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth"). One way to minimize the chance of hitting anything on the way down (and dying) is to clear the platform of all bodies and pots before you touch the orb. Then, stand in the exact center of the platform and wait for the floor to open.

Kagrenzel bridge

Swimming down from where you landed in the pool, you will discover an expert-locked Dwemer [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). There is a tunnel near the edge of the pool to the south with unoccupied [Falmer hives](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Hive "Skyrim:Falmer Hive") on either side and an unlocked Falmer chest sitting just to the right on a large rock. As you head up the tunnel, it turns east after a few paces and starts to climb very steeply. There are Falmer hives on the walls; however, most of these are empty. The use of [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") or the [Aura Whisper](/wiki/Skyrim:Aura_Whisper "Skyrim:Aura Whisper") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") is recommended. The ground may shake and the occasional rock may roll down, causing minor injuries if it strikes you. At the top, a moonstone ore vein is found where the passage turns north. You will eventually reenter the main chamber on an L-shaped stone bridge with a large fire pot burning in the corner. On the left-hand side of the fire pot is a small adept-locked Dwemer chest, with a random [potion of invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Brief_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Brief Invisibility") beside it. A patrol of three Falmer will enter onto the bridge from the opposite end, then cross to the side you entered through before returning the way they came. There is also a fourth Falmer hidden in a hive on the wall at the far side.

Kagrenzel treasure

Crossing the bridge and continuing to follow the passage, you will pass several more Falmer hives until you reach a section with two waterfalls, one in front and one on the left, an archway, and another Falmer chest. Climbing up to the waterfall on the left will reveal a [centurion dynamo core](/wiki/Skyrim:Centurion_Dynamo_Core "Skyrim:Centurion Dynamo Core") within the stream. A [flawless diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Diamond "Skyrim:Flawless Diamond") will be visible from this position atop the archway; it can be obtained using several methods, including [Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis"), the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout, or an [arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows"). Following the stream under the arch leads to [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave").

## Notes

- Facing the entrance from outside, you are facing west; however, as soon as you enter, with your back against the door, you are now facing south.
- If you view the large pool room on your map, you will see several massive rib cages, which are possibly mammoth remains.
- With the [Nchuanthumz: Dwarven Home](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuanthumz:_Dwarven_Home "Skyrim:Nchuanthumz: Dwarven Home") Creation, [Frostroot Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostroot_Cave "Skyrim:Frostroot Cave") is north of this dungeon.

## Bugs

- For quests related to Kagrenzel, your map marker may point you to Stony Creek Cave. This also applies to the [Clairvoyance](/wiki/Skyrim:Clairvoyance_(spell) "Skyrim:Clairvoyance (spell)") spell.
- You can reach the glowing orb's room from the pool room by swimming through a gap in the eastern wall north of the rocks that jut into the pool.
- If you have a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), they may enter Kagrenzel with you from the trapdoor direction, then disappear and not return. This often occurs because the game placed the follower at the top of the main chamber instead of beside you, and they fell and died outside your view. **?**

## Gallery

- 

  Path to Kagrenzel

Kagrumez

**Kagrumez** is a small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") south of the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak").

Map of Kagrumez

## Related Quests

- **[The Kagrumez Gauntlet](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Kagrumez_Gauntlet "Skyrim:The Kagrumez Gauntlet")**: Survive the Kagrumez trials to claim a unique [prize](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Black_Bow_of_Fate "Skyrim:Dwarven Black Bow of Fate").
- **[Stealer of Souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealer_of_Souls "Skyrim:Stealer of Souls")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Archer_Pack "Skyrim:Arcane Archer Pack"): Learn how to craft [Soul Stealer Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Stealer_Arrow "Skyrim:Soul Stealer Arrow").

### Exterior

A large tent contains the corpse of the conjurer [Raleth Eldri](/wiki/Skyrim:Raleth_Eldri "Skyrim:Raleth Eldri") and his [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"). It seems he was so interested in studying Dwemer ruins and their attendant dangers that he failed to account for the more mundane threat of bandits: he was killed by the [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") who now occupy the ruin, one of whom carries his research [notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Raleth_Eldri%27s_Notes_on_Kagrumez "Skyrim:Raleth Eldri's Notes on Kagrumez"). The nearby stairs lead down to the lift which descends into the ruin, with a Dwarven [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") in the rubble to the west behind the lift. A [ruby geode](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby_Geode "Skyrim:Ruby Geode") can be found southwest of the dungeon.

### Kagrumez

The lift leads to a chamber lined with large shelves holding miscellaneous Dwemer items. A Dwarven chest is under one of the shelves, and two destroyed [Dwarven spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") are on the ground nearby. Stairs to the east descend to a door, which opens to the arena-style main chamber. Several reavers occupy the chamber. A pedestal on a platform in the center of the room is set with a 3x3 grid, into which [Kagrumez resonance gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrumez_Resonance_Gem "Skyrim:Kagrumez Resonance Gem") can be inserted. There are five resonance gems in total. Two gems can be found on the reaver in the main chamber who also carries Raleth Eldri's notes. Another gem can be bought or pickpocketed from [Revus Sarvani](/wiki/Skyrim:Revus_Sarvani "Skyrim:Revus Sarvani"), who camps near his [silt strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Silt_Strider "Skyrim:Silt Strider") northwest of [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)"). Another gem can be found at the end of [Fahlbtharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz"). The final gem can be found in [Nchardak](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchardak "Skyrim:Nchardak") during the quest [The Path of Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Path_of_Knowledge "Skyrim:The Path of Knowledge"). Only four gems are needed to explore the entire ruin.

There are three doors in the ruin, which can only be opened by placing resonance gems in the pedestal in three specific patterns; the patterns are engraved on the corresponding doors. Placing the gems in these patterns will trigger three arena matches. During each match, you will be locked in the main chamber, and several Dwarven automatons will attack you. For the first round, you will have to defeat three [ballistae](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ballista "Skyrim:Dwarven Ballista") and three spiders. For the second round, you will have to defeat two [spheres](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere") and five spiders. For the third round, you will have to defeat two ballistae, one sphere, and two spiders. A round is over when all automatons have been destroyed; the second and third rounds have environmental hazards as well.

The first door requires two resonance gems to open, the second door requires three gems, and the third door requires four gems. Beyond the first door on the north wall of the main chamber is a room with a large shelf holding Dwemer items, a Dwarven chest, and the [Steadfast Dwarven Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Steadfast_Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Steadfast Dwarven Spider"), a potential [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers#Dragonborn_Creatures "Skyrim:Followers"). Beyond the second door is a room with a Dwarven chest and the [Steadfast Dwarven Sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Steadfast_Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Steadfast Dwarven Sphere"), another potential follower. Beyond the third door is a room with a destroyed [Dwarven centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion"), a chest, a [flawless diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Diamond "Skyrim:Flawless Diamond"), two [diamonds](/wiki/Skyrim:Diamond "Skyrim:Diamond"), a quiver of [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows"), and the unique [Dwarven Black Bow of Fate](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Black_Bow_of_Fate "Skyrim:Dwarven Black Bow of Fate"). With the [Arcane Archer Pack](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Archer_Pack "Skyrim:Arcane Archer Pack") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, several [Soul Stealer Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Stealer_Arrow "Skyrim:Soul Stealer Arrow") can be found next to the bow; when taken, you will automatically learn how to craft the arrows. A corridor to the west leads to a balcony with three chairs overlooking the main chamber.

Three alcoves with gates are set high in the walls of the main chamber, and serve as the spawn areas for some of the Dwarven automatons during the arena matches. The alcove to the south can be reached by using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") from the balcony above the chamber. The alcoves to the northeast and northwest can be reached by using Whirlwind Sprint from the balcony to a pipe in the center of the chamber, then using Whirlwind Sprint from there to the northeast alcove. Another sprint across will get you to the northwest alcove. There is nothing behind the gates.

## Notes

- You can only have one steadfast automaton follower at a time.
- Respawning mechanism of [Steadfast Dwarven Sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Steadfast_Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Steadfast Dwarven Sphere") and [Steadfast Dwarven Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Steadfast_Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Steadfast Dwarven Spider") have nothing to do with time, there's a respawning point as long as you walk into, they will respawn immediately, it's about on the small flat area downstair from the entrance. Thus you can upgrade the [Ebony Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Blade "Skyrim:Ebony Blade") to maximum without waiting at all.

## Bugs

- Sometimes, the corpse of Raleth Eldri will not appear.
- Sometimes, the Dwarven automatons become stuck in their spawn alcoves around the main chamber during an arena match. If the match won't end and you think you've destroyed all of the automatons, get as close as possible below each alcove, and if a red enemy dot appears on your HUD, you will know an automaton is above. To destroy the automaton, back up as far as possible and shoot arrows or destruction spells into the alcove, or use the spell [Unbounded Storms](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbounded_Storms "Skyrim:Unbounded Storms") from the [Arcane Accessories](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Accessories "Skyrim:Arcane Accessories") Creation.
- Sometimes, after all Dwarven automatons are destroyed during an arena match, you will still be trapped in the main chamber, and will have no choice but to load a prior save.
- Sometimes, the steadfast automaton followers will not appear.
- Though the steadfast automaton followers are supposed to respawn in their nooks if they are killed in battle, they might not and you'll never be able to use them again. **?**

Sometimes you will not be able to recruit either steadfast automaton as a follower. The cause of this is unknown.

# Skyrim:Karth River

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Body of Water: Karth River ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Karth+River)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Karth_River "Lore:Karth River")) | | |
| Regions | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | |
| Location | |
| Between [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") and [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | |

Karth River

The **Karth River** is a river flowing from [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").

The Karth River originates in [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") at Lost Valley Redoubt from a waterfall flowing from the mountain range. It is unknown where the river that supplies that waterfall flows from without consulting with another provincial map of a region such as Hammerfell or High Rock. From there it flows north and northeast, temporarily splitting in two around the [Karthspire](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire "Skyrim:Karthspire"), then passing [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") and [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") before finally reaching the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts") near Solitude. This river is fed from at least four different sources, including the waterfalls at [Lost Valley Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valley_Redoubt "Skyrim:Lost Valley Redoubt"), the stream at [Hag Rock Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag_Rock_Redoubt "Skyrim:Hag Rock Redoubt"), also known as the [Reachwater River](/wiki/Lore:Reachwater_River "Lore:Reachwater River"), the stream sourced from the three waterfalls that flow through Markarth from the mountains above, and the waterfall just above [Deep Folk Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Deep_Folk_Crossing "Skyrim:Deep Folk Crossing") near the border with High Rock.

# Skyrim:Karthspire

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Karthspire (top) and Karthspire Camp (bottom)

**Karthspire** is a large [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and cave east of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). It contains only one zone, *[The Karthspire](#The_Karthspire)*.

The area includes two map markers, "Karthspire" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Karthspire&zoom=14&legacy=true) and "Karthspire Camp" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Karthspire+Camp&zoom=14&legacy=true), counting as two separate locations for the "Locations Discovered" statistic. *The Karthspire*, the cave near the latter marker, leads to the entrance to [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple"), which can only be accessed after starting the quest [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall").

## Related Quests

- **[Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall")**: Locate the prophecy within [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple").
- **[Crypt of the Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Crypt_of_the_Heart "Skyrim:Crypt of the Heart")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Spell Knight Armor"): Investigate rumors of a ghost that haunts the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River").[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")

### Exterior: Karthspire Camp

Forsworn camp

To reach the camp, head east on the main road from Markarth over the first bridge and past the path leading south to [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal"). At the crossroads, continue east. After passing [Reachwater Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachwater_Rock "Skyrim:Reachwater Rock") to the south, cross the next bridge heading east-southeast. Continue past an overturned cart until you come to another bridge on your left heading north-northwest. This leads directly to the camp.

The camp is sprawling and built on several levels, with the main level built on a series of wooden platforms over the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River") linked via wooden bridges. It is extremely difficult to approach the camp or take out the individual Forsworn guards without alerting the whole camp. If you are at a low character level, consider avoiding the area entirely.

From the above direction, you will come to steps leading up onto the first platform. This is where you will appear if fast-traveling to this location. There is a tent on your left with a Forsworn inside sitting on a bench. In front of you is a pile of crates, barrels, and sacks. On one of the crates is an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") and a sample of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), and on a barrel is a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). Be careful, as right by the tent opening is a hole in the wooden platform. In front of the tent the platform continues to the northwest, with a wooden bridge leading to the northeast. Under this bridge is a [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") plant. Following the bridge you will come to a turning to the east. At this corner is another Forsworn. The path passes a set of stone stairs leading up to the higher levels of the camp. The first level has another Forsworn and two bastions overlooking the river in both the westerly and southerly directions. There are a tent and a lit brazier between them. The tent only contains a hay pile.

There is another wooden ramp by the top of the stone stairs leading to the highest level of the camp. To the right of the ramp is a barrel. At the top of the ramp you will find two more Forsworn, one of which is a magic user who specializes in frost magic. You also find a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") with an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") on top. To the right of the forge are three barrels, a hay bale, a sack, and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest").

Hagraven camp

From the bottom of the stone steps the path continues to the east, passing between two lit braziers and leading to the [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") and her camp. This consists of a tent containing an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") built in to a wooden table with two apothecary's satchels attached to the front edge and a boss level unlocked chest. On the alchemy lab are a [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), an [eye of sabre cat](/wiki/Skyrim:Eye_of_Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Eye of Sabre Cat"), and a sample of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"). A campfire is lit in front of the tent. Farther to the east is a dead [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") laid out on a rock with a bowl in front containing a bowl of [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts"), an eye of sabre cat, and a [giant's toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe").

Back by the initial tent, just past the tent is a path heading southwest up a wooden ramp to a campfire guarded by a Forsworn. Beside the fire is a bench, and behind this is a hay pile. There is a flight of stone steps heading up to the south from this level; at the top of the steps are a Forsworn guard, campfire, and bench. *[The Karthspire](#The_Karthspire)* is accessed from this level through the nearby cave entrance.

The main platform below continues over another wooden bridge to the northwest and branches off to the northeast. This part of the camp has two Forsworn guards and contains a tent, a large table and benches, a rack with three hanging [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"). To the right of the rack are two crates with a leveled warhammer and a [draught of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Draught of Enhanced Stamina"). On top of the table is an apothecary's satchel. Inside the tent are a hay pile, four sacks, and a crate with a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Dance in Fire, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v2 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v2")*. Leaning against the crate is a [hide shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Shield "Skyrim:Hide Shield"). To the right of the tent are a crate and sack with two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on the crate, two benches, and a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"). To the right of the tanning rack are two [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips").

Continuing to the northwest from the junction over another wooden bridge is another Forsworn guard and a tent containing a hay pile, a barrel, three sacks, and a crate with a bottle of leveled poison on top. To the left of the tent are three more barrels and two crates with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") leaning against them. On top of one barrel is a sample of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), on top of one crate is a leveled greatsword, and on top of another barrel are a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root") and a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"). In front of these items to the west is a ramp leading down to the water.

### The Karthspire

The campfire

Upon entering, you are in a natural cave with a campfire in front of you and a wooden ramp to the left of the fire which leads up to the main living area. Beside the campfire is a sleeping Forsworn guard and three bedrolls, and behind these is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"). Following the ramp up, you will pass on your left a dresser with a [potion of ultimate stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Ultimate_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Ultimate Stamina") and two random [fear poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Fear_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Fear Poison"). There are many food barrels around the cave, including two in the southeast corner, one of which has three gold coins on top. To the right of these barrels is a table with a chair and a small mead barrel and a fillet of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat") on top. There are two narrow wooden bridges across a small gap, and between these are a small table and chair; a Forsworn guard is sitting here.

Crossing one of the bridges, you will encounter the [Forsworn Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart"). There is a table next to a stone pillar holding a random potion, a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), a bowl of void salts, a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), and a wooden plate containing a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") and a canis root. There is a barrel next to the table with a lit lantern on top. There are three more bedrolls next to the north wall. In the southwestern corner is an unowned double bed, an unlocked chest, and a small table.

The wooden planking continues to the west and then turns to the north, then continues until you reach a table holding a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). It then turns back to the west. The tunnel opens into a large open-roofed cavern. There are stairs on your right against the northeastern wall. On the wall, just before the stairs start, is a second iron ore vein. On the other side of the stairs is a [juniper](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper "Skyrim:Juniper") tree. Passing between two parts of a stone bridge structure, farther back into the cavern on the ground level, is a tree stump with a [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") growing on it.

The puzzle pillars

At the top of the stairs are three rotatable pillars with unusual symbols. Unless you are here as part of the quest Alduin's Wall, or have already completed it, this is as far as you can go.

During this quest, you unlock the stone bridge and cause it to drop into place, allowing further progress to be made. There is a second juniper tree on the far side of the bridge, with stairs leading south into a tunnel. The tunnel turns to the west again and opens into a room full of pressure plate tiles on the floor. Follow the correct symbols to the pull chain that deactivates the traps and drops a second bridge heading north over the previous large open-roofed cavern. As you cross this second stone bridge, there is another juniper tree on your right on a lower ledge only accessible by dropping down onto it. There is nothing else of interest there. Continue to follow the path into another tunnel that turns to the west and up some more steps. It then turns south again, and you are now at the highest level within the large open-roofed cavern. The path forward heads west and opens into a large stone chamber with an unlocked chest in the middle and a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein"), which doesn't respawn. This is the entrance to Sky Haven Temple. You need to activate the blood seal to gain entrance.

## Notes

- If the quest Alduin's Wall has been started, a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") will spawn here. Also, the Forsworn at the camp will be much more dangerous.
- As the exterior camp does not have a Forsworn Briarheart, and the cave and its Briarheart don't respawn, Karthspire is the only Forsworn location that cannot be revisited to examine a Briarheart for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") as part of his quest [Briarheart Necropsy](/wiki/Skyrim:Briarheart_Necropsy "Skyrim:Briarheart Necropsy").
- If you fast travel to Sky Haven Temple, you will arrive inside *The Karthspire* in front of the blood seal and the door to the temple.
- An alternative to following the trail across the pressure plates is simply to point yourself at the pillar opposite, with the pull chain on it, and use Whirlwind Sprint.
-  With the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") v2.0.2 (or later) installed, the Forsworn in the camp will no longer respawn ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=14862)).

## Bugs

- A section of the dungeon not far from the Akaviri puzzle pillars, has two large gaps between the floor and rock walls. These gaps are large enough for NPCs to get wedged into with no way to get them out.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, addresses this issue. A pair of wooden planks have been placed to cover the holes so this won't happen. The navmesh in this part of the dungeon was also badly constructed and has been fixed.
- Despite being part of The Reach and having large sections exposed to the sky above, Karthspire Redoubt (the part of Sky Haven Temple where the puzzle doors are) only ever uses fog weather which doesn't match the parent worldspace.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- A giant rock formation in the cave may disappear as you get closer, depending on what angle you look at it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.0, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=18656))
- Even after the Forsworn at the camp stop respawning with Unofficial Skyrim Patch 2.0.2, the containers there may continue to respawn despite the camp now being classed as a "no-reset zone".
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

| # of [Tanning Racks](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning") | 1 |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Karthwasten Hall

**Karthwasten Hall** is a farmhouse in the southeastern part of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten"), located next to [Enmon's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Enmon%27s_House "Skyrim:Enmon's House").

It is the home of [Ainethach](/wiki/Skyrim:Ainethach "Skyrim:Ainethach"), the owner of Karthwasten's mines. It consists of one zone, *[Karthwasten Hall](#Karthwasten_Hall)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Ainethach](/wiki/Skyrim:Ainethach "Skyrim:Ainethach") |

## Exterior

| Plants | Mushrooms | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 2 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  3 [Juniper Berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") | 1 [White Cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") | 3 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken")  2 [Goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg")  1 [Tanning Rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") |

## Karthwasten Hall

Ground floor

The front door opens to a bedroom area on the right and a kitchen and dining area to the left. Immediately to the right is a single bed (belonging to the [KarthwastenAinethachHouse](/wiki/Skyrim:KarthwastenAinethachHouse "Skyrim:KarthwastenAinethachHouse") faction) in the northwest corner. Farther along the west wall is a small table holding five gold coins, five [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"), and a medium-sized [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). A non-respawning wardrobe stands along the south wall nearby, next to a woven basket containing two [potions of vigor](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigor "Skyrim:Potion of Vigor"). A double bed, owned by the same faction, is situated to the left, with a small non-respawning chest at its foot. To the left of the bed is the home's fireplace, with a [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace") on its mantel and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") at its base. A hanging rack with three freshly caught [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") can be found just to the left of the fireplace.

The east side of the north wall hosts the dining and food storage area, starting with a large dining table. The table is set with two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), one bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), three [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a serving of [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a head of [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), and two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). On the floor next to the table is a woven basket containing two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), and a set of shelves which hold two more leeks, three potatoes, and a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulb, as well as some [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), and a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") sitting on top. Above the shelves are several hanging ingredients, including two garlic braids, three portions of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and some dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). A respawning food barrel can be found in the northeast corner.

Basement

Heading downstairs will lead to the basement, which is relatively bare. A garlic braid and one portion each of dried frost mirriam and dried elves ear are hanging above a small round table which holds a single loaf of bread. A set of shelves on the south wall holds various kitchenware, and two respawning food barrels sit to the right. A training dummy stands near the center of the west wall with a non-respawning large sack nearby. A long work table sits against the north wall near the stairs, holding nothing except a medium-sized coin purse, and another respawning food barrel rests to the right.

## Notes

- The front door has a novice lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Karthwasten_Hall "Skyrim:Key to Karthwasten Hall") to which is carried by [Ainethach](/wiki/Skyrim:Ainethach "Skyrim:Ainethach").
- Two respawning food barrels can be found next to the steps to the porch, which hosts a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning"), six more respawning food barrels, and a table holding four bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread").
- If you [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") Ainethach, you will have the option of living here.
