Karthwasten Miner's Barracks

**Karthwasten Miner's Barracks** is the collective housing area for local miners in [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten"), located between [Enmon's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Enmon%27s_House "Skyrim:Enmon's House") and [Fenn's Gulch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Fenn%27s_Gulch_Mine "Skyrim:Fenn's Gulch Mine") in the northwestern part of town.

Local miners [Belchimac](/wiki/Skyrim:Belchimac "Skyrim:Belchimac"), [Lash gra-Dushnikh](/wiki/Skyrim:Lash_gra-Dushnikh "Skyrim:Lash gra-Dushnikh"), and [Ragnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnar "Skyrim:Ragnar") reside here. It consists of one zone, *[Miner's Barracks](#Miner.27s_Barracks).*

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Belchimac](/wiki/Skyrim:Belchimac "Skyrim:Belchimac")  [Lash gra-Dushnikh](/wiki/Skyrim:Lash_gra-Dushnikh "Skyrim:Lash gra-Dushnikh")  [Ragnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnar "Skyrim:Ragnar") |

## Exterior

| Plants | Other |
| --- | --- |
| 1 [Juniper Berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") | 1 [Tanning Rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack")  1 [Stone Quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") |

## Miner's Barracks

Miner's Barracks interior

This housing area is well stocked and set up for the local miners, with all the required supplies and amenities in the small space. On the south side of the building is a single bed along the east wall, owned by [Lash gra-Dushnikh](/wiki/Skyrim:Lash_gra-Dushnikh "Skyrim:Lash gra-Dushnikh"). A respawning food barrel sits in the southeast corner, next to a non-respawning cupboard holding various kitchenwares. The west wall hosts a dining table which holds two [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and a bucket containing three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). Above the table are some hanging ingredients, including some dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), two portions of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids. Next to the hanging ingredients is a hanging rack with three freshly caught [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and three [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). A respawning food barrel sits on the floor to the right, next to a set of shelves holding one bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and two bottles of alto wine on top, a copy of the book *[Songs of the Return, Vol 19](/wiki/Skyrim:Songs_of_the_Return,_Vol_19 "Skyrim:Songs of the Return, Vol 19")* on the middle shelf, and two bottles of alto wine and three bottles of wine on the bottom shelf.

The fireplace is situated farther to the right on the western wall, with a copy of *[Olaf and the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_and_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Olaf and the Dragon")* sitting on the right side of its base. A small table in front of the fireplace holds one bottle each of wine and alto wine, along with one loaf and one piece of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). On the north side of the room, a non-respawning end table sits at the center, between [Ragnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnar "Skyrim:Ragnar")'s single bed on the left, and [Belchimac](/wiki/Skyrim:Belchimac "Skyrim:Belchimac")'s single bed on the right. At the foot of each bed is a small non-respawning chest, and the end table holds a single bottle of Nord mead. Finally, on the eastern wall, just north of the front door, a respawning food barrel sits next to a non-respawning dresser, which holds three bottles of Nord mead and two [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"). Above the dresser are three hanging garlic braids, some dried elves ear, and some dried frost mirriam.

## Notes

- The front door has a novice lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Karthwasten_Miners%27_Barracks "Skyrim:Key to Karthwasten Miners' Barracks") to which is carried by Belchimac, Lash gra-Dushnikh, and Ragnar.
- A [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") can be found behind the building, and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") can be found on the front porch, with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") lying nearby.

Karthwasten

**Karthwasten** is a mining [town](/wiki/Skyrim:Towns "Skyrim:Towns") in the northern [Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach").

[Ainethach](/wiki/Skyrim:Ainethach "Skyrim:Ainethach") is the owner of the whole town including the two surrounding mines. The mines at Karthwasten are two of the few mines in the Reach that are not owned by a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord").

When you first enter Karthwasten, you will see the townsfolk squaring off against a group of mercenaries sent by the [Silver-Blood family](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonar_Silver-Blood#Silver-Blood_Family "Skyrim:Thonar Silver-Blood") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to stop them from working [Sanuarach Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine") until Ainethach agrees to sell the land to them.

The town consists of three buildings in a semicircle: [Karthwasten Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten_Hall "Skyrim:Karthwasten Hall"), where Ainethach lives, [Enmon's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Enmon%27s_House "Skyrim:Enmon's House"), where [Enmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Enmon "Skyrim:Enmon") lives with his wife [Mena](/wiki/Skyrim:Mena "Skyrim:Mena") and daughter [Fjotra](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra"), and the [miner's barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten_Miner%27s_Barracks "Skyrim:Karthwasten Miner's Barracks"), where [Belchimac](/wiki/Skyrim:Belchimac "Skyrim:Belchimac"), [Lash gra-Dushnikh](/wiki/Skyrim:Lash_gra-Dushnikh "Skyrim:Lash gra-Dushnikh"), and [Ragnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnar "Skyrim:Ragnar") live. There is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") in front of Karthwasten Hall and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") on the deck in front of the miner's barracks.

Sanuarach Mine is the main [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") mine. Its only entrance is north of Karthwasten Hall. In front of the entrance is a [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter"), three pieces of [silver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore") in a cart opposite, and a [Juniper](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") tree on a rock. The entrance to [Fenn's Gulch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Fenn%27s_Gulch_Mine "Skyrim:Fenn's Gulch Mine") is at the northwestern end of town and has another smelter, two [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"), and a piece of silver ore to the left of the entrance, with another Juniper tree to the right of the entrance.

- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").

## Notes

- Northeast of Karthwasten, there is a small bloodied altar holding a [black soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem") and a piece of bloodied cheese.
- East-northeast of Karthwasten, on a hill facing down to the river next to a circle of ancient stones, there is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein").
- West of Karthwasten, below the hill with the [Shrine to Peryite](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_to_Peryite "Skyrim:Shrine to Peryite"), there is an unmarked stone totem with a dead body and some loot.
- Karthwasten appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")* as [Karthwasten Hall](/wiki/Arena:Karthwasten_Hall "Arena:Karthwasten Hall"), and also [appears](/wiki/Online:Karthwasten "Online:Karthwasten") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

Katla's Farm

**Katla's Farm** is a small [farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Farms "Skyrim:Farms") and [stable](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables") along the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River"), outside of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). The farm is owned by [Katla](/wiki/Skyrim:Katla "Skyrim:Katla"), who lives here with her husband [Snilling](/wiki/Skyrim:Snilling "Skyrim:Snilling"), and their son [Knud](/wiki/Skyrim:Knud "Skyrim:Knud").

The [Hearthfire add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") adds a straw bed to the stables and a [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") named [Blaise](/wiki/Skyrim:Blaise "Skyrim:Blaise") who works on the farm.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Blaise](/wiki/Skyrim:Blaise "Skyrim:Blaise")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")  [Katla](/wiki/Skyrim:Katla "Skyrim:Katla")  [Knud](/wiki/Skyrim:Knud "Skyrim:Knud")  [Snilling](/wiki/Skyrim:Snilling "Skyrim:Snilling") |

## Related Quests

- **[Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity")**: Infiltrate a party at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy").
- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Horse Whisperer](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Whisperer "Skyrim:Horse Whisperer")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Wild Horses"): Purchase a map that lets you find wild horses.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The northern part of the farm is [Solitude Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Stables "Skyrim:Solitude Stables"). The farm also boasts a mill. There are numerous sacks in piles around the farm. The crops are grown in two patches, one by the front door and the other behind the building. There is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") under a roofed area to the right of the front door.

| Crops | Plants |
| --- | --- |
| 2 [Cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage")  9 [Leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek")  12 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato")  3 [Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") | 1 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")  3 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")  2 [Thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") |

### Katla's Farm

Katla's Farm

The farm is not locked during the day, if you have [sold crops](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat") to Katla, you will be able to enter without any issues. On your left as you enter is a barrel of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") and a basket containing [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). To the right of these against the north wall is a set of shelves containing several cheese wheels and wedges, along with a cabbage and five potatoes. Against the east wall is a table holding two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), one bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), two potatoes, a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), several [goat cheese pieces](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") and a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"). Under the table is an open crate containing a sample of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") and an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing"). To the right is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and two bottles of wine on the mantle above. On the hearth is a piece of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef") and a cabbage in a cast iron pot.

There is a small wooden table set for two in the middle of the room holding a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bottle of Alto wine, two portions grilled leeks, two seared slaughterfish, a loaf of bread, an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") and a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"). Coming out from the east wall, to the right of the fireplace is an internal wall with an open crate against it containing five [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), three potatoes and two cabbages. Against the west wall are two open crates containing three [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), two potatoes, a cabbage, four [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") and three garlic bulbs. Hanging from the ceiling are five garlic braids. The stair up to the top floor are also against the west wall.

Behind the internal half-height wall is Katla and Snilling's bedroom containing an unowned double bed in the middle of the south wall with and end table to the left holding a bottle of wine and a stool to the right. Above the bed is a wall shelf holding two bottles of wine, one bottle of alto wine and three bottles of Nord mead. Against the internal wall is a cupboard holding a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"), three garlic bulbs and a gourd. To the right against the east wall is another cupboard holding a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"), a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") and an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"). Under the stairs are two sets of shelves containing a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), three bottles of Nord mead, a bottle of wine, two sheaves of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), two loaves of bread, three [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), potatoes and cabbages as well as several cheese wheels.

At the top of the stairs against the south wall is a small set of shelves holding a woodcutter's axe. In the southeastern corner is a small round wooden table and chair. On the table is a bottle of wine, a bottle of alto wine and a loaf of bread. Against the east wall, by a doorway to another bedroom is a small unit holding a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk"), a [cave bear pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Cave_Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Cave Bear Pelt"), a [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") and a basket containing two bunches of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), with a sack beside it. Through the doorway into Knud's bedroom, on your left is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), and against the west wall a table holding a bottle of wine, a bottle of alto wine, a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"), an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"), a [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace"), an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe") and a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"). Under the table is a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). In the northeastern corner is an unowned single bed, with an end table to the left holding a common book.

## Notes

- The [key to the farmhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Katla%27s_Farm "Skyrim:Key to Katla's Farm") is carried by Katla, Knud, and Snilling.
- If you [sell leeks, potatoes, or wheat to Katla](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat"), the horses in the [stable](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Stables "Skyrim:Solitude Stables") become free to take. However, you will not own them and they will walk back to the stable once you dismount. Also, the bed in the farmhouse becomes free to sleep in.

## Bugs

- The chickens and goats may not be marked as owned by the farm.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.
- If you buy a horse from here and the horse is killed, attempting to purchase a new horse from the same stable results in 1000 gold being deducted, and Geimund stating that your horse is "the one with the saddle", despite no saddled horse appearing at the stables here. Instead, the new horse spawns at the [Riften Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Stables "Skyrim:Riften Stables").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- Selling crops to Katla will allow you to ride the horses at [Solitude Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Stables "Skyrim:Solitude Stables") for free, due to her being in the same ownership faction as the stablemaster. The problem is that horses cost 1,000 gold, making them way too valuable to let stablemasters let you ride them for free after completing a small favor.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, addresses this issue. The ownership of the horses was changed to just Geimund, rather than the faction, preventing this issue.
- None of the inhabitants here own the beds assigned to them. **?**

# Skyrim:Khajiit Traders

## Overview

The **Khajiit traders** are caravans of roving [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit") [merchants](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant "Skyrim:Merchant") who travel between different settlements in Skyrim with their entourages, which includes [trainers](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") and mercenaries who protect the groups. After completing several quests for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), a merchant in each caravan will become a [fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Skyrim:Fence (merchant)") and purchase stolen goods. All three caravans are owned and operated by [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad"), though he has divided his workers into three smaller groups and assigned each of them a different trading route.

The Khajiit caravans can be encountered on the road traveling between their destinations. When arriving at a city, they will establish a camp outside the main entrance to the city. These camps will have tents and a campfire; in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") the camp will have a tanning rack as well. The caravan will stay for a while, then resume traveling. Both setting up and breaking camp will only happen off-screen. Whether at their camp or on the road, they will always be ready to do business. Their merchandise levels with you, so the higher your level, the greater the quality of what they have for sale.

Each caravan has a [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest") assigned to it. One of them can be found near a rock formation outside of [Iron-Breaker Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron-Breaker_Mine "Skyrim:Iron-Breaker Mine") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). Another one can be found near a stone wall and a Juniper tree outside of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). The third can be found near a plant formation outside of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). Their contents level with you, so the higher your level, the greater the quality. You can loot each chest for free, and all 3 will respawn every 48 hours. Be warned, however, that the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") will cause these chests to be inaccessible.

The [Rare Curios](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Curios "Skyrim:Rare Curios") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") adds a number of items that are exclusively available from the Khajiit traders, most of which are rare ingredients with otherwise unobtainable [alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") effects. The traders are also the only source of [Aloe Vera Leaves](/wiki/Skyrim:Aloe_Vera_Leaves "Skyrim:Aloe Vera Leaves"), added in [Special Edition Patch 1.6.1130](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch#1.6.1130 "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch").

For more information, see the [main lore article](/wiki/Lore:Khajiit_Caravans "Lore:Khajiit Caravans").

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Balance of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Balance_of_Power "Skyrim:Balance of Power")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers"): Put a stop to two bandit gangs wielding strange otherworldly equipment.
- **[Find the Thalmor Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Find_the_Thalmor_Assassin "Skyrim:Find the Thalmor Assassin")**: The [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") are after [Malborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Malborn "Skyrim:Malborn"). Help him get to safety.
- **[Kill Ma'randru-jo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ma%27randru-jo "Skyrim:Kill Ma'randru-jo")**: Assassinate [Ma'randru-jo](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27randru-jo "Skyrim:Ma'randru-jo") to complete a [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") contract.
- **[Missing Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_Merchant "Skyrim:Missing Merchant")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail"): A powerful set of armor has come on the market.
- **[Spirits Away](/wiki/Skyrim:Spirits_Away "Skyrim:Spirits Away")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Help a Khajiit trader recover his shipment of [aged flin](/wiki/Skyrim:Aged_Flin "Skyrim:Aged Flin").
- **[Thieves Guild Caravan Fence Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_Caravan_Fence_Quest "Skyrim:Thieves Guild Caravan Fence Quest")**: Deliver [moon sugar](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Sugar "Skyrim:Moon Sugar") to [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad").

### Ri'saad's Caravan

[Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad")'s own caravan has a trade route between [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), and includes the fence [Atahbah](/wiki/Skyrim:Atahbah "Skyrim:Atahbah") and the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") target [Ma'randru-jo](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27randru-jo "Skyrim:Ma'randru-jo"). They are protected by the mercenary [Khayla](/wiki/Skyrim:Khayla "Skyrim:Khayla"), who is a common [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") trainer. The merchant chest assigned to his caravan is near a stone wall and a Juniper tree outside of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").

### Ahkari's Caravan

[Ahkari](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahkari "Skyrim:Ahkari") is accompanied by the fence [Zaynabi](/wiki/Skyrim:Zaynabi "Skyrim:Zaynabi") and travels between [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") and [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). They are protected by the mercenaries [Dro'marash](/wiki/Skyrim:Dro%27marash "Skyrim:Dro'marash"), a common [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") trainer, and [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"), who becomes a follower after [retrieving his Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon"). The merchant chest assigned to her caravan is near a rock formation outside of [Iron-Breaker Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron-Breaker_Mine "Skyrim:Iron-Breaker Mine") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").

### Ma'dran's Caravan

[Ma'dran](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27dran "Skyrim:Ma'dran")'s route between [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") has proven to be very profitable during the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). He is protected by the mercenary [Ra'zhinda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ra%27zhinda "Skyrim:Ra'zhinda") and is also accompanied by [Ma'jhad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27jhad "Skyrim:Ma'jhad"), who is both a fence and an expert trainer in [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking"). The merchant chest assigned to his caravan is near a plant formation outside of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").

## Dialogue

For the shared dialogue used by the caravaneers, see [this page](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Dialogue#Khajiit_Caravan_Dialogue "Skyrim:Generic Dialogue").

## Notes

- The caravans would have originally been accompanied by horses, which still exist in the files, but go [unused](/wiki/Skyrim:Unused_Creatures#Horses "Skyrim:Unused Creatures") in the final game. The caravan's leader would have presumably ridden on them.
- 12 NPCs were created as part of the caravans, but only 11 made it into the final game. The only one that goes unused is, notably, an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") by the name of [Grushnag](/wiki/Skyrim:Unused_NPCs#Grushnag "Skyrim:Unused NPCs"). Based on his Form ID, it's known that he was created alongside the caravan Khajiit, and he's also present in the list `CaravansNPCList` which just lists all relevant NPCs. Based on his placement in said list, as well as his equipment, he was in all likelihood a guard for a caravan. However, for which caravan this was, is unknown, as he has no remaining dialogue and he is not mentioned anywhere else; not in the game nor its files.
- If you start "[Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound")" as a Khajiit, [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") will ask: *"You with one of the trade caravans, Khajiit?"*
- If you start the quest to retrieve Kharjo's Moon Amulet and obtain it, you'll always know where Ahkari's caravan is due to the quest marker, as long as you don't return the amulet to Kharjo.
- Unlike regular general goods merchants, Khajiit traders don't sell arrows. With [Rare Curios](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Curios "Skyrim:Rare Curios") installed, they will sell [Corkbulb Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Corkbulb_Arrow "Skyrim:Corkbulb Arrow")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club").

## Bugs

- The Khajiit caravans may fail to set up tents and just stand in place.
  -  Entering the following console commands in sequence can be used to reset bugged caravans. Do this at a location distant from the caravan stop points and save your game beforehand.

Relevant Commands

:   :   `prid 0010372F`
    :   `disable`
    :   `prid 001030E2`
    :   `disable`
    :   `prid 00104AD6`
    :   `disable`
    :   `prid 00103774`
    :   `disable`
    :   `prid 0010311B`
    :   `disable`
    :   `prid 0010332A`
    :   `disable`
    :   `set CaravanIsCampedA to 0`
    :   `set CaravanIsCampedB to 0`
    :   `set CaravanIsCampedC to 0`
    :   `set CaravanLocationA to 0`
    :   `set CaravanLocationA to 1`
    :   `set CaravanLocationB to 0`
    :   `set CaravanLocationB to 1`
    :   `set CaravanLocationC to 0`
    :   `set CaravanLocationC to 1`

- A bug similar to the above occurs when the tents and campsite are set up at one caravan stop (say, Ri'saad's camp is outside Whiterun), but the Khajiit merchant in question is on the other side of the map at their other stop (in Risaad's case, Markarth), without the camp. Once this bug happens to a particular Khajiit merchant, it will continue for them.
- Investing with [Belethor's General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Belethor%27s_General_Goods "Skyrim:Belethor's General Goods") also adds gold to Khajiit caravans.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=13209))
- Members of a Khajiit caravan will join [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") and [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") in fighting you if they witness the battles, due to faction relationships being set up incorrectly.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Nordic Ruin: Kilkreath Ruins ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kilkreath+Ruins)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Kilkreath_Ruins "Lore:Kilkreath Ruins")) | | |
| # of Zones | 3 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (storage is [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers")) |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 24 |
| Occupants | |
| [Corrupted Shades](/wiki/Skyrim:Corrupted_Shade "Skyrim:Corrupted Shade"), [Malkoran](/wiki/Skyrim:Malkoran "Skyrim:Malkoran") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Battle of Red Mountain](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_Red_Mountain "Skyrim:Battle of Red Mountain")* [Dawnbreaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnbreaker "Skyrim:Dawnbreaker") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| KilkreathRuinsExterior01, KilkreathRuinsExterior02, KilkreathRuinsExterior03, KilkreathRuinsExterior04, KilkreathRuinsExterior05, KilkreathRuins01, KilkreathRuins02, KilkreathRuins03 | |
| Region | |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | |

| West of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") Southeast of [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Arcane Enchanters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") | 1 |

Kilkreath Ruins

**Kilkreath Ruins** is a large [ruined temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing [corrupted shades](/wiki/Skyrim:Corrupted_Shade "Skyrim:Corrupted Shade") created by the necromancer [Malkoran](/wiki/Skyrim:Malkoran "Skyrim:Malkoran"). It contains three zones: *[Kilkreath Temple](#Kilkreath_Temple)*, *[Kilkreath Ruins](#Kilkreath_Ruins)*, and *[Kilkreath Catacombs](#Kilkreath_Catacombs)*.

The [temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines"), situated below the [Statue to Meridia](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_to_Meridia "Skyrim:Statue to Meridia"), is dedicated to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Meridia](/wiki/Lore:Meridia "Lore:Meridia"). You must activate a series of pedestals to redirect a beam of light in order to progress through the ruin. Until you have retrieved [Meridia's Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Meridia%27s_Beacon "Skyrim:Meridia's Beacon"), the temple will be inaccessible.

## Related Quests

- **[The Break of Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Break_of_Dawn "Skyrim:The Break of Dawn")**: Find [Meridia's Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Meridia%27s_Beacon "Skyrim:Meridia's Beacon") and use its light to cleanse her temple of undead.

### Exterior

Kilkreath Ruins during the related quest

Outside is the Statue to Meridia, which will initiate or progress a [Daedric quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Quests "Skyrim:Daedric Quests") to find and return Meridia's Beacon when you approach. Once the beacon has been recovered, [Meridia](/wiki/Skyrim:Meridia "Skyrim:Meridia") will unlock the doors to the temple in order for you to enter and cleanse the ruin of Malkoran and the corrupted shades he has created from those who have died in the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). She sends down a beam of light, which you will need to guide through the ruins in order to open the doors along the route to *Kilkreath Catacombs*, where you will confront Malkoran. The entrance is to the west, built into the base of the structure supporting the statue. A short distance uphill northeast of the statue is a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") which teaches a word of the [Elemental Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Fury "Skyrim:Elemental Fury") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). Visible along the outside of the ruins to the east are large stone sculptures topped with refracting gems, which are used in the related quest.

### Kilkreath Temple

The entrance leads into a wide passage, with stairs down to the south. A black smoke-like atmosphere and the [desecrated corpses](/wiki/Skyrim:Desecrated_Corpse "Skyrim:Desecrated Corpse") of the corrupted shades are found throughout the ruins, with the first two corpses lying just inside the entrance. These corpses can be looted for large amounts of gold (see [notes](#Notes)). There are also many [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") and [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") within the ruins. At the bottom of the stairs, behind some fallen masonry, is a patch of [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") fungus. The passage is staggered to the left by a statue, with three burial urns and another desecrated corpse beside it. Farther along, on the left, is an adept-locked door which opens to a short passage with a lever at the end. Opposite this door on the right side of the main passage is a doorway blocked by a lowered metal gate, which is raised by the lever. This provides access to another short passage, which features an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and an [ancient Nord sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Sword "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Sword") lying next to it.

The passage turns to the east (with another desecrated corpse at the corner), then splits; both directions lead down into the same chamber, with large arches and stone pillars supporting the ceiling high above. In the center is a refracting gem atop a pedestal, with light streaming into it through a hole in the roof. To the right of the pedestal, next to a statue that has been knocked over by falling masonry, is an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"), while an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") is to the southwest. There are five desecrated corpses in the chamber: one near the iron shield, two among some rubble to the northwest, and two near the southeast corner. There are large double doors at the far eastern end. You will need to activate each of the pedestals you find as you continue through the ruins in order to open doors and continue toward the Catacombs. Beyond the eastern doors is a long flight of stairs down to another opened set of doors, with a [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungus before the open doors on the right. Through the doors, you will see two corrupted shades, which appear as little more than a black smoky outline in their original armor. A third shade will join the fight once battle has commenced. When the shades are killed, they leave behind their [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") and form faintly black puddles, similar to those formed by [ice wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith").

Through the doors is a large room, with rows of stone benches facing another pedestal with a refracted gem on top to the east on the first of three rising levels. There is a door down a short passage to the south. The pedestal is on the first level to the east. On the second level is a set of shelves holding a [candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick") and eight [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"), as well as a sideboard with a random empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") on top. The final level has large urns at either end, and double doors in the middle to the east. Both the eastern and southern doors will only open when you activate the pedestal. From the highest level, it is possible to jump on top of the shelves and reach a ledge along the north wall in front of a barricaded room containing a set of shelves holding seven burned books, a ruined book, a leveled invisibility potion, and a damage health poison, all of which are out of reach and require the use of [telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis") to obtain. Alternatively, these items can be dislodged with arrows or spells until they roll close to the ledge. Behind the double doors to the east is a cave-in with a small gap the beam of light can shine through, but you will need an alternate route. The door to the south opens to a room that contains two corrupted shades, two large urns, several windows on the left into the room behind the cave-in, and a set of shelves holding an iron dagger and more ruined books on the left. There is also a wooden door at the southern end of the room.

This door opens to a passage that takes two turns and descends a flight of stairs before reaching another door to another room, which contains two desecrated corpses, two large urns, a sideboard holding a random potion of healing, magicka, or stamina, and an unlocked chest. A passage heading east leads into another large room, with balconies on three sides and wooden stairs leading up to the south and east. There are two corrupted shades in this room: one on the lower level, and the other on the balcony to the north. There is one desecrated corpse on the lower level. The balcony to the east links with the one to the north. A bridge links the northern balcony to a central platform with a refracted gem on a pedestal in the middle, beyond which is a second span of the bridge to the southern balcony that has collapsed, although the gap can be jumped. At the rear of the northern balcony is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), with a lowered gate, a level-locked iron door, and a large urn to the right. Behind the door is a lever that raises the gate, and behind the gate is an unlocked chest. Once you activate the pedestal, an iron door on the southern balcony will be opened. The southern balcony also features two burial urns and a large urn. Behind the door is a short passage featuring another desecrated corpse and another iron door, which leads outside to a balcony.

### Exterior: Kilkreath Balcony

The balcony is high on the mountainside far above the road between Solitude and [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"), with views of the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River") as it winds its way toward Solitude from [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") in the southwest and of [Eldersblood Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldersblood_Peak "Skyrim:Eldersblood Peak") far to the southeast. There is a narrow walkway on your left, with an expert-locked chest and stairs leading up to another iron door to *Kilkreath Ruins* on the far side.

It is possible to climb down (or if on [horseback](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses"), up) onto the balcony without entering the rest of the ruins and without starting (or if already in your journal, completing) the quest. However, only the chest can be looted this way; the doors to the Temple and Ruins are both key-locked until Meridia's light has been guided through the Temple. There are six refracting gems on tall statues linking the light from *Kilkreath Temple* to *Kilkreath Ruins*.

### Kilkreath Ruins

Kilkreath Ruins interior

Through the iron door on the balcony is a passage heading north. Flights of stairs upward past two turns and a large urn lead to a large room guarded by three corrupted shades on the ground level, with a fourth on a caged walkway above. There is a locked iron door in the middle of the south wall. In the southwestern corner is a table with a desecrated corpse and two burial urns on top. A broken stone table beside it has three loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a [gold emerald ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Emerald_Ring "Skyrim:Gold Emerald Ring"), and another burial urn. Two large urns are found elsewhere on the ground level.

Wooden stairs to the east lead up to a balcony, where two sideboards flank another locked iron door. One of the sideboards holds a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") and a random [potion of resist magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Magic"). There is also a short walkway out onto a platform with a refracted gem on a pedestal. Activating this opens the door on the balcony.

The passage behind the balcony door leads to a room guarded by one corrupted shade. To the right of the entrance is a large urn, and along the west wall is a raised area holding four burial urns, with an unlocked chest in the northwest corner next to a passage to the north. On the north wall to the right of the passage, a leveled [trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") connects to a wooden door that triggers a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") from the floor, with a desecrated corpse leaning against the door. This door opens into a smaller room containing an unlocked chest, a large urn, a set of shelves holding a candlestick, a random pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"), a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), and another random potion of healing, magicka, or stamina, and a sideboard holding an unlocked [strong box](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox").

The passage to the north soon turns to the west, where a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") triggers a [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") trap in the passage beyond. At the far end is a lever that deactivates the trap. From here, the passage turns south and leads out to the large room onto a caged walkway that passes over and around two platforms to a third platform that isn't caged, where the fourth corrupted shade was originally.

From the third platform, jump to a separate platform just to the south to activate the pedestal there. Then return to the third platform and cross a narrow walkway to the north to reach a narrow balcony that wraps around to the west. In the northwestern corner is a stone table with a desecrated corpse on top, as well as a novice-locked chest between two sets of shelves holding an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), two random [potions of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a random potion of healing, and a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Battle of Red Mountain](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_Red_Mountain "Skyrim:Battle of Red Mountain")*. A large urn is to the south, just before the iron door on the west wall unlocked by the previous pedestal.

Through the now unlocked door, the passage leads to another large room guarded by two more corrupted shades. There are four desecrated corpses and four large urns on the ground level. Two flights of wooden stairs lead up to two of four raised sections around the room. The other two areas are blocked by wooden walls. The stairs on the west wall lead up to a small area with a random potion on a plinth with a [weight sensitive plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate") that triggers a single spear from the wall behind.

At the top of the stairs against the east wall, jump to a nearby wooden ledge on the north wall to loot another desecrated corpse. To the east is a doorway to a wide passage, which turns south after a few paces past three burial urns before leading back out onto a platform high above the large room with the caged walkway. On the platform is another refracted gem on a pedestal and another desecrated corpse. Activating this pedestal opens the southern door on the ground level far below you. Either backtrack, or jump down on top of the cage, then to a platform, and finally to the ground. Through the southern door on the ground level is a short flight of stairs descending to an iron door leading to *Kilkreath Catacombs*.

### Kilkreath Catacombs

Through the door is a wide passage that descends a flight of stairs and turns twice before opening into a large room. The room contains three desecrated corpses, one of which is leaning against the raised section in the middle of the room and has an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and three loose septims beside it. In both the northeastern and southeastern corners, on small raised sections, is a random potion of healing, magicka, or stamina. In the southeast corner, there is also an unlocked chest and two burial urns.

Activating the final refracting gem on top of the central pedestal opens double doors to the east, which lead to two descending flights of stairs ending in a large room. Once you proceed approximately halfway down the stairs, the double doors will close and lock, with no way to reopen them. The powerful necromancer Malkoran waits with several corrupted shades. There are eighteen desecrated corpses scattered around the room, along with an iron dagger, an iron shield, and an iron sword. A raised section to the northwest features two large urns and a stone table holding two burial urns and a random potion or poison. Following this section back to the right of the room's entrance, a random potion of healing, magicka, or stamina is on the ground. A similar raised section to the southwest includes three burial urns, two large urns, and a leveled [paralysis poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Paralysis_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Paralysis Poison").

After Malkoran and his shade have been destroyed, the one-handed [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") and Daedric [artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Artifacts "Skyrim:Artifacts"), [Dawnbreaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnbreaker "Skyrim:Dawnbreaker"), will appear in the pedestal where the light from the refracted gems terminates. Upon taking Dawnbreaker, you will be transported high in the sky to commune with Meridia again. Afterward, the quest will conclude, and you will be lowered to the ground in front of the statue.

## Notes

- There are 43 desecrated corpses throughout the ruin, as detailed in the walkthrough above. If you loot them all, you may obtain a total amount of gold in the range of 1075-5375.
- There is an oversized jug (almost three times the size of a standard jug) in the latter half of the dungeon before you reach Malkoran.
- Standing in the light path can cause you to take both shock and magicka damage.
- The last section of *Kilkreath Catacombs* becomes inaccessible after the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Break_of_Dawn "Skyrim:The Break of Dawn"). You may not be able to retrieve [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") told to wait in that area.
  - There is a workaround: use the plate and Whirlwind Sprint combo, and you'll regain access to Malkoran's chamber, but you won't find anything in there except for the Desecrated Corpses from before. To get out, you'll either have to reload or use the same combo again.
  - If not told to wait, the follower will teleport with you back to the shrine, though most commonly they can be found in the first or second chambers. Thralls (elemental or undead) can also be found in the same location.
  - After 72 hours, a message will appear stating that your follower has grown tired of waiting and has returned to their home or original location.
- You can obtain a duplicate Dawnbreaker by knocking it off its pedestal with an area-of-effect spell during the battle with Malkoran. Retrieve the sword on the ground prior to the sword in the stand to keep both.
  - Version 4.1.3 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch") removes the duplicate Dawnbreaker.
- The location also appears as [Kilkreath Temple](/wiki/Online:Kilkreath_Temple "Online:Kilkreath Temple") in [ESO: Greymoor](/wiki/Online:Greymoor "Online:Greymoor").

## Bugs

- The word wall here may not work. **?**
  - Either save, exit to the title screen, and reload, or fast travel away and back again.
- The swinging blade trap on the second level of the ruins may only swing once if you break the tripwire. **?**
- The expert-locked chest on the balcony may respawn despite the dungeon being classed as a "No Reset Zone". **?**
- The double doors in *Kilkreath Catacombs* that lead to Malkoran's lair were never supposed to close and lock themselves once you open them and make your way across. As a result, the plate trick mentioned above is your only way back in.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.5, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  Kilkreath Temple
- 

  Kilkreath Ruins
- 

  Kilkreath Catacombs

# Skyrim:Kill Agnis

## Overview

Your target is on contested ground

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir").
2. Kill [Agnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Agnis "Skyrim:Agnis").
3. Return to Nazir.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After speaking to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir"), you are told to locate and assassinate a target known as [Agnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Agnis "Skyrim:Agnis"). She can be found inside the keep of [Fort Greymoor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greymoor "Skyrim:Fort Greymoor") which is west of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). The fort is initially garrisoned by bandits, whom you can either sneak past or kill. However if you have advanced far enough in the civil war quest line (beyond the [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun")), it is garrisoned by soldiers of whichever faction controls Whiterun - *your* faction, that is, making the assassination much easier. Either way, Agnis is easily found inside the keep and, having only a dagger and some modest clothing for protection, is equally easy to kill.

If you approach Agnis before you kill her, you will receive three dialogue options; you will only be able to choose one as you can not initiate conversation with her again. Note that none of these dialogue options will cause her to become hostile.

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **"You've cleaned your last room, servant."** | *"But I have many more rooms to clean. Fort Greymoor is quite large, and rather filthy if I do say."* |
| **"Sleep now, old woman. Embrace the Void."** | *"Sleep? I can't sleep now! There's too much to be done. And what's this Void you're rambling on about?"* |
| **"(Remain silent)"** | *"I swear, you people are an odd bunch. Please, just step aside, that I may return to my duties!"* |

After the kill, report back to Nazir for a leveled gold as a reward.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

## Notes

- When receiving payment for the finished job, [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") will say *"Infiltrating an occupied fort and making it out in one piece is nothing to joke about. Well done."*, but his voice dialogue actually says *"Infiltrating an occupied **military** fort and making it out in one piece is nothing to joke about. Well done."*
- Certainly with the Unofficial Skyrim Patch (Legendary or Special Edition) installed, and maybe without it: If you clear the fort of bandits without harming Agnis, but without having taken sides in the Civil War, it will be re-garrisoned with Imperials, since Jarl Balgruuf opposes the Stormcloaks. These Imperials will be neutral (and thus non-hostile) to an unaligned player, just as they would to a pro-Imperial one (i.e. one who has brought the Jagged Crown to General Tullius, even if the Battle of Whiterun has not yet taken place): the only way to face a hostile garrison is if the player has cleared the fort of bandits, then subsequently sided with the Stormcloaks (by bringing the Jagged Crown to Ulfric instead) and then decides to go in and murder Agnis \*before\* the Battle of Whiterun - for instance, if they bring Ulfric's axe to Balgruuf and then visit Fort Greymoor while Balgruuf is still in charge of Whiterun, before returning to Ulfric and starting the battle quest.

## Bugs

- Agnis belonging to the Dark Brotherhood faction can cause you to get expelled from the Dark Brotherhood if she gets attacked at the wrong time.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.7, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Contract: Kill Agnis (DBSideContract09) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I must kill the old woman Agnis, who serves as a servant in Fort Greymoor. I may use any means at my disposal. When I am done, I am to report back to Nazir at the Sanctuary and collect my reward. *Objective 10:* Kill Agnis |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Report back to Nazir |
| 200 | ☑ | Agnis is dead, and I have collected my reward from Nazir at the Sanctuary. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DBSideContract09 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DBSideContract09`.

# Skyrim:Kill Anoriath

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Kill [Anoriath](/wiki/Skyrim:Anoriath "Skyrim:Anoriath") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") |
| Location(s): | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") |
| Reward: | Leveled gold |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =-2 ([Elrindir](/wiki/Skyrim:Elrindir "Skyrim:Elrindir") if kill directly) |
| ID: | DBSideContract08 |
| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Kill Hern](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Hern "Skyrim:Kill Hern"), [Kill Lurbuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Lurbuk "Skyrim:Kill Lurbuk"), [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death") (Start) | **Concurrent** [Kill Deekus](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Deekus "Skyrim:Kill Deekus"), [Kill Ma'randru-jo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ma%27randru-jo "Skyrim:Kill Ma'randru-jo") | **Next →** [Kill Agnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Agnis "Skyrim:Kill Agnis") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Kill Hern](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Hern "Skyrim:Kill Hern"), [Kill Lurbuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Lurbuk "Skyrim:Kill Lurbuk"), [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death") (Start) | | Concurrent | [Kill Deekus](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Deekus "Skyrim:Kill Deekus"), [Kill Ma'randru-jo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ma%27randru-jo "Skyrim:Kill Ma'randru-jo") | | → Next | [Kill Agnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Agnis "Skyrim:Kill Agnis") | | |

Anoriath lets loose an arrow

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get your orders from [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir").
2. Kill [Anoriath](/wiki/Skyrim:Anoriath "Skyrim:Anoriath").
3. Return to Nazir.

## Detailed Walkthrough

When you receive this contract from Nazir, he says Anoriath is a hunter who hunts on the plains outside Whiterun. However, prolonged stalking reveals that he does not in fact leave the city. During the day he works at his stall in the market, and at night he retires to [The Drunken Huntsman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Drunken_Huntsman "Skyrim:The Drunken Huntsman"), which is run by his brother, to sleep. Your best bet to take him out without a bounty is to either shoot him during the day from a remote spot such as Jorrvaskr, or to sneak into his bedroom at night and slit his throat. However, both are very difficult to do without incurring a bounty, so plan for this.

As third option; when Anoriath is working his stall, go straight behind him and climb the rock until you reach the walls corner. Time an Illusion Frenzy or one-shot bow attack properly (meaning no guards patrolling the road to your left when facing Anoriath), and you will incur no bounty.

Alternatively, like most other assassination targets, you have the option to talk to Anoriath, which gives you three dialogue choices, one of which will turn Anoriath hostile, allowing you to kill him anywhere without fear of incurring a bounty (except if you initiate conversation outside, say at his stall, and then he retreats somewhere inside, like The Bannered Mare, in which case, he will cease to be hostile and it will be considered murder to kill him then). You can only pick one as you will not be able to initiate conversation again.

| Topic | Dialogue | Response |
| --- | --- | --- |
| *(Remain silent)* | *"Well now, you are a strange one. You remind me a bit of myself, when I'm stalking a deer. I'm not quite sure how I feel about that..."* | Walks away |
| *"I am the predator. You are my prey."* | *"Is that so? We shall see, villain. We shall see!"* | Turns hostile and attacks |
| *"Only cowards hunt animals. True game walks on two legs."* | *"Are you... threatening me? Walk away fool. It's not worth it."* | Walks away |

Once Anoriath is dead, return to Nazir. Upon rewarding you with leveled gold, Nazir will remark *"Ah, so the hunter came to know the fear of the hunted, hmm?"*.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

## Notes

- Regardless of whether you are caught killing Anoriath or not, if you deal the killing blow, your relationship with his brother, [Elrindir](/wiki/Skyrim:Elrindir "Skyrim:Elrindir"), will be lowered by two points.
- If [Deceiving the Herd](/wiki/Skyrim:Deceiving_the_Herd "Skyrim:Deceiving the Herd")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") sends you to Whiterun and this quest is also active, you can plant the Incriminating Letter on Anoriath's corpse and advance both quests together.
- Despite what Nazir and the quest log may tell you, Anoriath is never actually found hunting outside the city.

## Quest Stages

| Contract: Kill Anoriath (DBSideContract08) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |

| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Report back to Nazir |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DBSideContract08 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DBSideContract08`.

# Skyrim:Kill Beitild

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Resolve a feud in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Nazir |
| Location(s): | [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary"), [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). |
| Reward: | Leveled gold |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =-2 ([Karl](/wiki/Skyrim:Karl "Skyrim:Karl") if kill directly), =-2 ([Irgnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Irgnir "Skyrim:Irgnir") if kill directly) |
| ID: | DBSideContract03 |
| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanctuary "Skyrim:Sanctuary") | **Concurrent** [Kill Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Narfi "Skyrim:Kill Narfi"), [Kill Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Kill Ennodius Papius") | **Next →** [Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanctuary "Skyrim:Sanctuary") | | Concurrent | [Kill Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Narfi "Skyrim:Kill Narfi"), [Kill Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Kill Ennodius Papius") | | → Next | [Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes") | | |

Beitild swinging her pickaxe

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get the contract from [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir")
2. Kill Beitild in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").
3. Claim your reward.

### Get the Contract

The assassination of [Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Beitild "Skyrim:Beitild") is part of the first batch of contracts handed to you by [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir"). After giving you the contract, he will readily tell you a bit about her background: *"She separated from her husband several months ago. Now the two run competing mining operations. Beitild's angry and desperate. A fighter."*

### Kill Beitild

In the town of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") it is common knowledge that Beitild and her husband [Leigelf](/wiki/Skyrim:Leigelf "Skyrim:Leigelf") are feuding, most evident by overhearing Leigelf arguing with the puzzled [Lond](/wiki/Skyrim:Lond "Skyrim:Lond") in front of [Quicksilver Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Mine "Skyrim:Quicksilver Mine") and by talking to the participants themselves. Beitild now runs [Iron-Breaker Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron-Breaker_Mine "Skyrim:Iron-Breaker Mine"), keeps a close eye on her workers at all times, and never misses the opportunity to bad-mouth the "fat-head owner" of the competing Quicksilver Mine.

When you approach Beitild, you will be given three dialogue options, you can only pick one of them and will not be able to choose another one by trying to talk to her again.

| Topic | Dialogue | Response |
| --- | --- | --- |
| *(Remain silent)* | *"I've a mine to run, so if you'll excuse me..."* | Beitild walks away |
| *"I represent the Dark Brotherhood. Your death is at hand!"* | *"What? Well, we'll see about that now, won't we?"* | Draws pickaxe and attacks |
| *"Someone wants you dead, Beitild."* | *"And let me guess, that someone is my so-called husband Leigelf? Well the feeling's mutual."* | Ends conversation |

An alternative is to use [stealth](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealth "Skyrim:Stealth") and kill Beitild in her sleep. She will return to her house at midnight and rest there until 8am. The lock on her front door can be picked or unlocked using the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Beitild%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Beitild's House") she carries about her person.

When Beitild is disposed of, you can pay a visit to her husband for an emotionless reaction: *"My wife Beitild is dead. Can't say I miss that old sabre cat."*

### Reward

Return to Nazir in the [sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary") for a leveled gold reward. When you tell him Beitild is dead he will respond *"Of course she is. I hear the mining business is extremely cutthroat. And those hours... they're murder."*

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

## Notes

- While this quest is active, it is impossible to [sell ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore") to Beitild as only the three dialogue options mentioned above are available.
- It's quite possible for Beitild to have already died by the time you would normally get this contract quest. If this is the case, then the contract will just be skipped entirely.
- If [Silus Vesuius](/wiki/Skyrim:Silus_Vesuius "Skyrim:Silus Vesuius") is on his porch and you kill Beitild while outside, Silus will become hostile even if you remained undetected.
- Killing directly will render disposition with [Karl](/wiki/Skyrim:Karl "Skyrim:Karl") and [Irgnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Irgnir "Skyrim:Irgnir") to -2, so better way is to poison to avoid this happening.

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DBSideContract03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DBSideContract03`.

Kill Deekus

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get the contract from [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir").
2. Travel to [Hela's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Hela%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Hela's Folly").
3. Assassinate [Deekus](/wiki/Skyrim:Deekus "Skyrim:Deekus").
4. Report back to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") to collect your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Another simple assassination. Head to [Hela's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Hela%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Hela's Folly"), northeast of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). [Deekus](/wiki/Skyrim:Deekus "Skyrim:Deekus") is by himself, so he is easily picked off. Spread about his camp are some miscellaneous items such as [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems") and a [Dibella Statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items#Dibella_Statue "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items"), presumably items he has looted from shipwrecks. There are two chests with Novice- and Apprentice-level locks that contain some minor loot; one is next to his tent and one is inside the shipwreck. The chest near the tent is protected by a bear trap, so opening it from behind is recommended. The chest in the shipwreck is located in the sunken half of the ship.

Like most assassination targets, you may choose to have a conversation with Deekus.

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| *"I'm going to kill you. Slowly. Painfully."* | *"You'll have to catch me first!"* |
| *(Remain silent)* | *"Go away! I don't know who you are, but this is my spot! Whatever's on that ship is mine!"* |
| *"I'm sorry, egg brother, but I've been sent to kill you."* (If the player is an [Argonian)](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian")   *"I'm sorry, Argonian, but I've been sent to kill you."* (if the player is not Argonian) | *"What? Why? I don't understand... I have done nothing to wrong you. Please, mercy!"* |

After the kill, report back to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") for some leveled gold as a reward.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

A paranoid Ennodius Papius

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to [Anga's Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill "Skyrim:Anga's Mill").
2. Kill [Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Ennodius Papius").
3. Report back to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir").

## Detailed Walkthrough

Simply travel to [Anga's Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill "Skyrim:Anga's Mill") and walk to the camp just up the road from the mill to the west. Kill [Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Ennodius Papius"), who is staying at the camp. He is far away enough to not attract any attention from patrolling guards or lumberjacks at the mill. During the day he is usually found around the water or his campfire; at night he'll be asleep in the tent. He will panic and flee on attack, but will not go far. Any incurred bounty while attacking him will revert on his death.

Alternatively, like most other assassination targets, you have the option to talk to Ennodius which gives you three dialogue choices, all of which will either turn Ennodius hostile (allowing you to kill him without fear of incurring a bounty) or run away in fear if your level is high enough.

| Your Options | Ennodius' Reply | Response |
| --- | --- | --- |
| *"You were right to be paranoid, Ennodius."* | *"What? What do you mean? Oh! Oh... no... No!"* | Turns hostile and attacks or runs away |
| *"Die, worm!"* | *"Aiiiiiiiieeeeee!"* |
| *(Remain silent)* | *"Who are you? You... you're with the Dark Brotherhood, ain'tcha? I knew it. I knew you'd come for me!"* |

### Reward

Return to the sanctuary and speak with Nazir, who will comment, *"How went your meeting with Ennodius Papius? Did you prove his paranoia legitimate?"* and rewards you with leveled gold.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

## Notes

- The target does not spawn prior to acquiring this quest. Completing this quest has no repercussions on other quests.
- There is a skeleton floating face down in the water behind his tent, a bit to the west, with a small amount of gold. Continuing west to the cliff, there is a quicksilver ingot under the water, and at the end, a locked strongbox in some debris under the cliff edge.
- Ennodius is a foe of [Kodrir](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodrir "Skyrim:Kodrir"), who may [reward you](/wiki/Skyrim:An_enemy%27s_gratitude "Skyrim:An enemy's gratitude") for his death ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")).

## Bugs

- The kill on Ennodius Papius may not register at all, with the quest marker still pointing to his corpse. This will cause progress in the Dark Brotherhood quest lines to stall out.
- Ennodius Papius may not spawn at all, with the quest marker pointing to his empty tent.
- If you kill Ennodius Papius while he is sleeping, he may fall through the floor out of the world.

## Quest Stages

| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Report back to Nazir |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DBSideContract02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DBSideContract02`.

# Skyrim:Kill Helvard

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Kill [Helvard](/wiki/Skyrim:Helvard "Skyrim:Helvard") in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") |
| Location(s): | [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") |
| Reward: | Leveled gold |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =-2 (Jarl of Falkreath) |
| ID: | DBSideContract11 |
| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Kill Agnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Agnis "Skyrim:Kill Agnis") | **Concurrent** [Kill Maluril](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Maluril "Skyrim:Kill Maluril") | **Next →** [Kill Safia](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Safia "Skyrim:Kill Safia") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Kill Agnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Agnis "Skyrim:Kill Agnis") | | Concurrent | [Kill Maluril](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Maluril "Skyrim:Kill Maluril") | | → Next | [Kill Safia](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Safia "Skyrim:Kill Safia") | | |

Helvard fighting back inside the [Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Falkreath) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Falkreath)")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Get the contract from [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir").
2. Kill [Helvard](/wiki/Skyrim:Helvard "Skyrim:Helvard").
3. Return to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir").

## Detailed Walkthrough

Once you have spoken to Nazir you will have found out that [Helvard](/wiki/Skyrim:Helvard "Skyrim:Helvard") is the Housecarl to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). You may find Helvard in the [Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Falkreath) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Falkreath)") in Falkreath.

If you approach Helvard before attacking him, you will be given 3 dialogue options, you can only pick one as you won't be able to speak to him again.

| Topic | Dialogue | Response |
| --- | --- | --- |
| *"You protect the Jarl. But who protects you?"* | *"And why would I... Oh. Oh! Guards! Guards, I need assistance!"* | Turns hostile and attacks |
| *"The Dark Brotherhood has come! "* | *"Fiend! You will not leave here alive! Guards! Guards!"* | Nobody will come, but Helvard turns hostile and attacks |
| *(remain silent)* | *"Right. Well. If you have some kind of official business with the jarl, I'm afraid now's not the time. Go on then. Off with you."* | Walks away |

An alternative is to use [stealth](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealth "Skyrim:Stealth") and kill Helvard while he sleeps in the Jarl's Longhouse.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

## Bugs

- Completing this quest may make it impossible to purchase [Lakeview Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Lakeview_Manor "Skyrim:Lakeview Manor")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") from [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
  - If [Dengeir of Stuhn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn") becomes or already is jarl, you may still purchase the property.
  - You may also still purchase property if you complete Siddgeir's quests after killing Helvard, or exile him in [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") and later retake [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") for him.
  -  You can inspect the [relationship rank](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") with the jarl by using the `player.getrelationshiprank` console command (normally you should get -2 foe, or worse) likewise you may set a good relation (positive, max 4) with the jarl by using this `player.setrelationshiprank 19822 4` command. A relationship rank of 3 or better will allow you to purchase property.

- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.

# Skyrim:Kill Hern

Hern and Hert

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Go to [Half-Moon Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Half-Moon_Mill "Skyrim:Half-Moon Mill").
2. Kill [Hern](/wiki/Skyrim:Hern "Skyrim:Hern") the vampire.
3. Return to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir").

## Detailed Walkthrough

Hern is a fairly easy kill, even if he is a vampire. He is usually with his wife in Half-Moon Mill's only home. They can both be killed with any weapons—as long as Hern dies, the mission completes. During the day, you'll find him outside, hanging out on a bridge. You can sneak into a shack next to the bridge and attack him safely with a ranged attack from an open window. His wife usually won't notice if it's a one-hit kill. You could also wait until morning for his wife to leave for the lumber. She always leaves before him, presenting a window where he can be found alone inside the house. If you have [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") installed, and her disposition is high enough for her to give you free lumber, you can ask her for free lumber when they are together inside the house; she will go outside to supervise your cutting of logs, and you will be alone with Hern. Also when they are entering or leaving the house if you engage Hern in conversation and hold him behind you can then sneak attack and kill him after Hert leaves the area.

Alternatively, like most other assassination targets, you have the option to talk to Hern which gives you three dialogue choices, two of which will turn Hern hostile.

| Topic | Dialogue | Response |
| --- | --- | --- |
| *"I know what you are, nightspawn."* | *"Well then, you won't be leaving here alive!"* | Becomes hostile and attacks |
| *"Assassin versus vampire. A fight for the ages."* | *"Ah, so the Brotherhood has come for old Hern, has it? Well then, let us meet as equals."* | Becomes hostile and attacks |
| *(Remain silent)* | *"Hmph. Don't say much, but there's a strange aura about you. You walk in the shadow of death... Leave here. Leave here and never return."* | Hern walks away |

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

Note that there is no reward for killing Hert, although if she witnesses you killing Hern, you can kill her to avoid the bounty.

## Notes

- Attacking Hern can incur a bounty, just like any other assault. Speaking to him will provide two dialogue options that will cause him to attack you, preventing a bounty. Either that, or kill any last witness (usually his wife).

| 200 | ☑ | Hern is dead, and I have collected my reward from Nazir at the Sanctuary. |

- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DBSideContract04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DBSideContract04`.
